♦ _*FAZILAT-E-SURAH YUNUS*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1436)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الۤرۚ تِلۡكَ ءَایَـٰتُ ٱلۡكِتَـٰبِ ٱلۡحَكِیمِ.*

_"Alif, Laam, Raa! Ye Hikmat o Danish wali Kitab ki Ayaat hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 1)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Al Hamdo lillah ab tak 9 Surah ki Tafseer mukammal ki aur next Surah Yunus ki Tafseer ki shuruat karte hain.

📚

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Lafz *الر* ke maani hai: *اَنَا اللّٰهُ الرَّؤوف* "Mein Shafeeq Allah hun."_

(Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

Huroof Maqatta'at ka Topic ham Surah Ale Imraan aur Surah Aaraaf ke aghaz mein zikr kar chuke hain.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Jo shakhs har doosre ya teesre Mahine Surah Yunus ki Tilawat kare to woh Jahelin mein qarar na payega aur aisa shakhs Roze Qayamat muqarrabin mein shumar hoga."_

(Kitab Sawabul Amaal)

📖

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Jo Shakhs Surah Yunus padhega to use Ummat e Yunus aur gharq hone wale Lashkare Firaun ki tadaad se Das guna zyada Ajr diya jayega."_

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Lafz *الر* ka talluq 'Ism e Azam' ke alaihda Huroof se hai. Jab Rasool aur Imam un Huroof ko jod kar Dua maange to uski Dua qubool hoti hai.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*Dua-e-Hafeza (Memory):* Har Namaz ke baad padhe. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Ali (as) ko taleem di thi:

*سُبْحَانَ مَنْ لَايَعْتَدِىْ عَلٰى اَهْلِ مَمْلَكَتِهِ سُبْحَانَ مَنْ لَا يَاْخُذُ اَهْلَ الْاَرْضِ بِاَلْوَانِ الْعَذَابِ سُبْحَانَ الرَّؤُفِ الرَّحِيْمِ اَللّٰهُمَّ اجْعَلْ لِىْ فِىْ قَلْبِىْ نُوْرًا وَ بَصَرًا وَ فَهْمًا وَ عِلْمًا اِنَّكَ عَلٰى كُلِّشَىْ ءٍ قَدِيْرٌ ۔*

(Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           *3rd Shawwal 1441*

   *27th May 2020, Wednesday*

               ♦ _*HAKEEM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1437)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الۤرۚ تِلۡكَ ءَایَـٰتُ ٱلۡكِتَـٰبِ ٱلۡحَكِیمِ.*

_"Alif, Laam, Raa! Ye Hikmat o Danish wali Kitab ki Ayaat hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 1)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Allah Ta'ala ne bahut se maqamaat par Qur'an Majeed ko "Hakeem" kaha hai aur Hakeem Saahebe Hikmat ko kaha jata hai. Qur'an Kareem ko Hakeem kahne ki ek wajah ye hai ke ek Azeem Aasmaani Kitab Hikmat par mushtamil hai.

Mufasserin ki aksariyat ka bayan hai ke Lafz "Hakeem" be maani "Haakim" hai. Qur'an Majeed Eteqaadat mein Haakim hai aur Haq o Baatil se alaihda karnewala hai aur Sawab o Khata ko juda karnewale hai aur Qur'an Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ki Nabuwwat ki Daleel e Akbar hai.

Baaz Ulama bayan karte hain ke "Hakeem" be maani "Mohkam" hai aur Qur'an itna Mohkam hai ke safiyan guzar jaane ke bawajood is mein kisi tarah ki tehreef o tarmeem (changes) nahi ho saki.

Qur'an Kareem ko Hakeem kehne ki ek wajah ye bhi hai ke Allah ne is mein Adl o Ehsaan ka hukm diya hai aur Ahle ita'at ke liye Jannat aur Ahle Isyaan ke liye Dozakh ka Faisla karta hai.

📚

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Qur'an ke ajaayeb ko shumaar nahi kiya ja sakta aur uske garaaib ka ihaata nahi kiya ja sakta. Qur'an Hidayat ka Chiraag aur Hikmat ka Minaar hai."_

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p557)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Hikmat ka sirf ek kalma (word) jise koi kisi se sune aur doosro'n se kahe, ya khud uspar amal kare, ek saal ki Ibadat se behtar hai."_

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p686)

🚩

Riwayat:

"Imam Mahdi (atfs) ki daur e hukumat mein tamaam logo'n ko Ilm o Hikmat ki taalim di jayegi, yahaa'n tak ke gharo'n ke andar auratein Kitaab o Sunnat se faisle karengi."

(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v52, p352, Aimma e Ahlebait (as) ki Fikr o Siyaasi Zindagi, p583)

🤲🏻

*..يَا مَنْ هُوَ فِيْ صُنْعِهِ حَكِيْمٌ، يَا مَنْ هُوَ فِيْ حِكْمَتِهِ لَطِيْفٌ،..*

(Joshan Kabir No. 18, Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

**********************************

              *4th Shawwal 1441*

       *28th May 2020, Thursday*

      ♦ _*KUFFAR KO TAJJUB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1438)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَكَانَ لِلنَّاسِ عَجَبًا أَنۡ أَوۡحَیۡنَاۤ إِلَىٰ رَجُلࣲ مِّنۡهُمۡ أَنۡ أَنذِرِ ٱلنَّاسَ وَبَشِّرِ ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوۤا۟ أَنَّ لَهُمۡ قَدَمَ صِدۡقٍ عِندَ رَبِّهِمۡۗ قَالَ ٱلۡكَـٰفِرُونَ إِنَّ هَـٰذَا لَسَـٰحِرࣱ مُّبِینٌ.*

_"Kya logon ke liye ye baat tajjub khez ban chuki hai ke Hamne un mein se ek Aadmi par Wahy bheji ke logon ko khabardar kar de aur jo Imaan laaye unhe is baat ki khush khabari de de ke unke liye unke Rab ke paas Sachchi Izzat o Sarfrazi hai. Kafiron ne kaha ke ye to khullam khulla Jadugar hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 2)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Kuffare Quraish ko is baat par tajjub hua ke Allah ne Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ko Risalat o Wahy ke liye kyon chun liya hai.

Kuffar ke tajjub ki kuchh wujuhat hain thin:

(1) Woh ye kehte the:

_"Usne to bahut se Ma'boodon ki jagah sirf ek hi Ma'bood qarar diya hai, yaqeenan ye to tajjub khez baat hai.(Saad:5)"_

Tauheed se inkaar.

(2) Agar ye hona hi tha to Hazrat Muhammad (saww) ko hi chuna.

_"Ye Qur'an Makkah ya Taif ke kisi Maaldar shakhs par kyon nahi utara gaya."_(Zukhruf:31)

Ek ye wajah ye thi:

_"Kya Khuda ne bashar ko hi Rasool bana kar bhej diya."_

(Bani Israel:94)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Sachchi Izzat se Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ki Wilayat murad hain."_

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Maqsad ye hai ke Allah Ahle Imaan ko Wilayat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali ka Aqeeda ata karta hai.

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Phrase *قدم صدق* se Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki Shafa'at murad hai"

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

Iska ek mafhoom ye hai ke Allah Ta'ala Qayamat ke Din Ahle Imaan ko sab se pahle mab'oos farmayega.

Isi liye Masoom (as) ne farmaya:

_"Ham agarche Akheri Ummat hain lekin Qayamat ke Din ham hi sab se aage honge."_

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*وَ اجْعَلْ لِيْ قَدَمَ صِدْقٍ عِنْدَكَ مَعَ الْحُسَيْنِ وَ اَصْحَابِ الْحُسَيْنِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ الَّذِيْنَ وَاسَوْهُ بِاَنْفُسِهِمْ وَ بَذَلُوْا دُوْنَهُ مُهَجَهُمْ وَ جَاهَدُوْا مَعَهُ اَعْدَاۤءَكَ ابْتِغَاۤءَ مَرْضَاتِكَ وَ رَجَاۤئِكَ وَ تَصْدِيْقًا بِوَعْدِكَ وَ خَوْفًا مِنْ وَعِيْدِكَ اِنَّكَ لَطِيْفٌ لِمَا تَشَاۤءُ يَاۤ اَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِيْنَ۔*

_"Khudaya! Mujhe Roze Qayamat Shafa'at e Husain (as) ata farma aur Sibat e Qadam dena Husain (as) aur Ashaabe Husain (as) ke saath."_

(Ziyarat e Ashura)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

     ♦ _*KHILQAT-E-AALAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1439)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ رَبَّكُمُ ٱللَّهُ ٱلَّذِی خَلَقَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضَ فِی سِتَّةِ أَیَّامࣲ ثُمَّ ٱسۡتَوَىٰ عَلَى ٱلۡعَرۡشِۖ یُدَبِّرُ ٱلۡأَمۡرَۖ مَا مِن شَفِیعٍ إِلَّا مِنۢ بَعۡدِ إِذۡنِهِۦۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكُمُ ٱللَّهُ رَبُّكُمۡ فَٱعۡبُدُوهُۚ أَفَلَا تَذَكَّرُونَ*

_"Yaqeenan tumhara Parwardigar wohi Allah hai Jisne Aasmaano aur Zameen ko Chhe (6) Dino (6 Times) mein paida kiya, phir Takht e Hukumat par Jalwagar hua, aur Kynat ka Intezaam chala raha hai. Uski Ijazat ke baghair Shafa'at Karnewala nahi hai. Yehi Allah hi tumhara Rab hai pas tum Uski hi Ibaadat karo. Kya tum Nasihat hasil na karoge?"_

(Surah Yunus: 3)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Allah Ta'ala ne Saal ke 12 Mahine banaye aur 30 Din ke hisaab se Saal ke Din 360 bante hain. Lekin Allah ne 360 Dino mein se Arz o Sama ki takhleeq ke 6 Din nafi (minus) kiye hain, isliye kuchh Mahine 29 Din ke hote hain."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Ye Islamic Lunar year hain.

🌎

Imam Ali Reza (as):

_"Allah Tadbeer e Umoor (Manage) karta hai lekin Harkat ke baghair."_

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Mere kuchh Momin Bande aise hain jo apne liye Ibaadat ka Darwaza khulwana chahte hain, lekin mein inhe isse rokta hun, taake un mein Khud Pasandi na paida ho aur Khud Pasandi ki wajah se woh halaak na ho jaayen."_

_"Mere kuchh Momin Bande aise bhi hain jin ka Imaan Iflaas ke baghair qayem nahi reh sakta. Agar mein unhe Daulatmand bana dun to woh halaak ho jayenge. Mere kuchh Bande aise bhi hain jinka Imaan Daulat o Amaarat ke baghair qayem nahi reh sakta. Agar mein unhe Ghurbat o Iflaas mein mubtila kar dun to woh halaak ho jayenge. Mere kuchh Bande aise bhi hain jin ka Imaan Sahet o Tandrusti ke baghair qayem nahi reh sakta. Agar mein unhe Bimaari de dun to woh halaak ho jayenge. Mein apne Bando ke Dilon ko achhi tarah se jaanta hun aur apne Ilm ke mutabiq unke Umoor ki tadbeer karta hun. Mein hi Sahibe Ilm aur Khabar hun."_

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*اَللّٰهُمَّ لَكَ الْحَمْدُ اَنْ خَلَقْتَ فَسَوَّيْتَ وَ قَدَّرْتَ وَ قَضَيْتَ وَ اَمَتَّ وَ اَحْيَيْتَ وَ اَمْرَضْتَ وَ شَفَيْتَ وَعَافَيْتَ وَ اَبْلَيْتَ وَ عَلَى الْعَرْشِ اسْتَوَيْتَ وَ عَلَى الْمُلْكِ احْتَوَيْتَ اَدْعُوْكَ دُعَاۤءَ مَنْ ضَعُفَتْ وَسِيْلَتُهٗ وَانْقَطَعَتْ حِيْلَتُهٗ وَاقْتَرَبَ اَجَلُهٗ...*

_"Parwardigar! Tera Shukr hai Tu ne Sahih o Salim paida kiya. Qaza o Qadar, Maut o Hayaat, Marz o Sahet o Aafiyyat o Balaa sab Tere Ikhtiyar mein hai. Tu Arsh ka Sahibe Ikhtiyar aur Mulk e Aalam ka Hakim hai. Manzile Dua mein meri haalat us shakhs ki hai jiske wasail kamzor, tadbeeren nakaam (ho chuki hain.)..."_

(Wednesday Dua -Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ _*MAQSAD-E-KHILQAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1440)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِلَیۡهِ مَرۡجِعُكُمۡ جَمِیعࣰاۖ وَعۡدَ ٱللَّهِ حَقًّاۚ إِنَّهُۥ یَبۡدَؤُا۟ ٱلۡخَلۡقَ ثُمَّ یُعِیدُهُۥ لِیَجۡزِیَ ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَعَمِلُوا۟ ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ بِٱلۡقِسۡطِۚ وَٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوا۟ لَهُمۡ شَرَابࣱ مِّنۡ حَمِیمࣲ وَعَذَابٌ أَلِیمُۢ بِمَا كَانُوا۟ یَكۡفُرُونَ.*

_"Uski taraf tum sab ko palat kar jaana hai. Ye Allah ka Sachcha Waada hai. Wohi Khilqat ka Aaghaz Karnewale hai aur phir use waapas le jaata hai taake jo log Imaan laye hain aur Nek Amal kiye hai unko Insaaf ke saath Jaza de aur Jinhone Kufr kiya hai to unke liye khaulte hue Paani ka Mashroob (Drinks) hai aur unke Kufr ki wajah se unke liye Dardnak Azaab hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 4)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Allah ne Guzishta aur is Ayat mein Apni Milkiyyat (Ownership) ka izhaar kiya hai. Allah ne hi ye poori Kaynat banayi aur Wohi ise manage karta hai. Sabhi Insaano ko Usne Khalq kiya aur phir Usi ki taraf wapas jaana hai. Ye hai Zindagi. Is Khilqat o Maut ke darmiyan mein hame Nek Amal karna hai taake ham iski Jaza paa saken. Aur jo log Allah ka Inkaar aur Nafarmani karenge unke liye khaulta hua Paani aur Dardnak Azaab hai.

🌎

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Shayad tum ye samajh rahe ho ke Allah Ta’ala ne sirf isi ek Aalam ko hi khalq kiya hai aur shayad ye samajhte ho ke usne tumhare alawa kisi aur ko Bashar (Insaan) banaya hi nahi. Nahi, Khuda ki qasam! Allah Jall Jalaalahu ne 10 Lakh Aalam paida kiya hain aur 10 Lakh Adam. Tum un Aalamo’n ke aakhri Aalam mein ho aur un Adamo’n ke aakhri Aadmiyo’n mein se ho."_

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p172)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Tu Akherat ke liye paida kiya gaya hai, lihaza isi ke liye kaam karte reh. Tu Duniya ke liye paida nahi kiya gaya, lihaza us se rukh pher le."_

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p83)

📖

Imam Sajjad (as):

_"Allah ne Apne Auliya mein se kisi ke liye Duniya ki Zeenat aur uski jald Fana hone wali cheezo'n ko pasand nahi farmaya. Aur na un mein se kisi ko khud Duniya aur uski khush karne waali cheezo'n ki taraf khwaish dilaayi hai. Balke Duniya aur Ahle Duniya ko sirf is liye paida kiya hai ke unki Aazmaish kare ke Duniya mein reh kar Akherat ke liye sabse zyada amal karne wala kaun hai."_

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p93)

🤲🏻

*وَبِكَلِمَتِكَ الَّتِيْ خَلَقْتَ بِهَا السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْاَرْضَ وَبِحِكْمَتِكَ الَّتِيْ صَنَعْتَ بِهَا الْعَجَاۤئِبَ، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا الظُّلْمَةَ وَجَعَلْتَهَا لَيْلًا وَجَعَلْتَ اللَّيْلَ سَكَنًا، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا النُّورَ وَجَعَلْتَهٗ نَهَارًا، وَجَعَلْتَ النَّهَارَ نُشُوْرًا مُبْصِرًا، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا الشَّمْسَ وَجَعَلْتَ الشَّمْسَ ضِيَاۤءً، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا الْقَمَرَ وَجَعَلْتَ الْقَمَرَ نُورًا، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا الْكَوَاكِبَ وَجَعَلْتَهَا نُجُوْمًا وَبُرُوْجًا وَمَصَابِيْحَ وَزِيْنَةً وَ رُجُوْمًا، وَجَعَلْتَ لَهَا مَشَارِقَ وَمَغَارِبَ، وَجَعَلْتَ لَهَا مَطَالِعَ وَمَجَارِيْ، وَجَعَلْتَ لَهَا فَلْكًا وَمَسَابِحَ،....*

_"Tere Kalemat se jisse Tu ne Aasmaano Zameen ko paida kiya, Teri Hikmat se jisse Tu ne Ajaeb banaye, Zulmat ko Paida kiya, Raat banayi, Raat ko Sukoon aur Araam qarar diya, Noor paida kiya, Din ko paida kiya, Din ko harkat o dekhne liye, Suraj aur iski Roshni paida ki, Chand aur iski Roshni paida ki,......"_

(Dua e Simaat (Dua e Shuboor) - Mafateeh

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

           *6th Shawwal 1441*

     *30th May 2020, Saturday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ _*MAQSAD-E-KHILQAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1440)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِلَیۡهِ مَرۡجِعُكُمۡ جَمِیعࣰاۖ وَعۡدَ ٱللَّهِ حَقًّاۚ إِنَّهُۥ یَبۡدَؤُا۟ ٱلۡخَلۡقَ ثُمَّ یُعِیدُهُۥ لِیَجۡزِیَ ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَعَمِلُوا۟ ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ بِٱلۡقِسۡطِۚ وَٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوا۟ لَهُمۡ شَرَابࣱ مِّنۡ حَمِیمࣲ وَعَذَابٌ أَلِیمُۢ بِمَا كَانُوا۟ یَكۡفُرُونَ.*

_"Uski taraf tum sab ko palat kar jaana hai. Ye Allah ka Sachcha Waada hai. Wohi Khilqat ka Aaghaz Karnewale hai aur phir use waapas le jaata hai taake jo log Imaan laye hain aur Nek Amal kiye hai unko Insaaf ke saath Jaza de aur Jinhone Kufr kiya hai to unke liye khaulte hue Paani ka Mashroob (Drinks) hai aur unke Kufr ki wajah se unke liye Dardnak Azaab hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 4)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Allah ne Guzishta aur is Ayat mein Apni Milkiyyat (Ownership) ka izhaar kiya hai. Allah ne hi ye poori Kaynat banayi aur Wohi ise manage karta hai. Sabhi Insaano ko Usne Khalq kiya aur phir Usi ki taraf wapas jaana hai. Ye hai Zindagi. Is Khilqat o Maut ke darmiyan mein hame Nek Amal karna hai taake ham iski Jaza paa saken. Aur jo log Allah ka Inkaar aur Nafarmani karenge unke liye khaulta hua Paani aur Dardnak Azaab hai.

🌎

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Shayad tum ye samajh rahe ho ke Allah Ta’ala ne sirf isi ek Aalam ko hi khalq kiya hai aur shayad ye samajhte ho ke usne tumhare alawa kisi aur ko Bashar (Insaan) banaya hi nahi. Nahi, Khuda ki qasam! Allah Jall Jalaalahu ne 10 Lakh Aalam paida kiya hain aur 10 Lakh Adam. Tum un Aalamo’n ke aakhri Aalam mein ho aur un Adamo’n ke aakhri Aadmiyo’n mein se ho."_

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p172)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Tu Akherat ke liye paida kiya gaya hai, lihaza isi ke liye kaam karte reh. Tu Duniya ke liye paida nahi kiya gaya, lihaza us se rukh pher le."_

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p83)

📖

Imam Sajjad (as):

_"Allah ne Apne Auliya mein se kisi ke liye Duniya ki Zeenat aur uski jald Fana hone wali cheezo'n ko pasand nahi farmaya. Aur na un mein se kisi ko khud Duniya aur uski khush karne waali cheezo'n ki taraf khwaish dilaayi hai. Balke Duniya aur Ahle Duniya ko sirf is liye paida kiya hai ke unki Aazmaish kare ke Duniya mein reh kar Akherat ke liye sabse zyada amal karne wala kaun hai."_

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p93)

🤲🏻

*وَبِكَلِمَتِكَ الَّتِيْ خَلَقْتَ بِهَا السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْاَرْضَ وَبِحِكْمَتِكَ الَّتِيْ صَنَعْتَ بِهَا الْعَجَاۤئِبَ، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا الظُّلْمَةَ وَجَعَلْتَهَا لَيْلًا وَجَعَلْتَ اللَّيْلَ سَكَنًا، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا النُّورَ وَجَعَلْتَهٗ نَهَارًا، وَجَعَلْتَ النَّهَارَ نُشُوْرًا مُبْصِرًا، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا الشَّمْسَ وَجَعَلْتَ الشَّمْسَ ضِيَاۤءً، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا الْقَمَرَ وَجَعَلْتَ الْقَمَرَ نُورًا، وَخَلَقْتَ بِهَا الْكَوَاكِبَ وَجَعَلْتَهَا نُجُوْمًا وَبُرُوْجًا وَمَصَابِيْحَ وَزِيْنَةً وَ رُجُوْمًا، وَجَعَلْتَ لَهَا مَشَارِقَ وَمَغَارِبَ، وَجَعَلْتَ لَهَا مَطَالِعَ وَمَجَارِيْ، وَجَعَلْتَ لَهَا فَلْكًا وَمَسَابِحَ،....*

_"Tere Kalemat se jisse Tu ne Aasmaano Zameen ko paida kiya, Teri Hikmat se jisse Tu ne Ajaeb banaye, Zulmat ko Paida kiya, Raat banayi, Raat ko Sukoon aur Araam qarar diya, Noor paida kiya, Din ko paida kiya, Din ko harkat o dekhne liye, Suraj aur iski Roshni paida ki, Chand aur iski Roshni paida ki,......"_

(Dua e Simaat (Dua e Shuboor) - Mafateeh

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ _*SHAMS O QAMAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1441)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هُوَ ٱلَّذِی جَعَلَ ٱلشَّمۡسَ ضِیَاۤءࣰ وَٱلۡقَمَرَ نُورࣰا وَقَدَّرَهُۥ مَنَازِلَ لِتَعۡلَمُوا۟ عَدَدَ ٱلسِّنِینَ وَٱلۡحِسَابَۚ مَا خَلَقَ ٱللَّهُ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ إِلَّا بِٱلۡحَقِّۚ یُفَصِّلُ ٱلۡـَٔایَـٰتِ لِقَوۡمࣲ یَعۡلَمُونَ.*

_"Usi ne hi Suraj (Sun)  ko Roshni di hai aur Chand (Moon) ko Noor banaya hai aur Chand ki Manzilen (Orbit) muqarrar kin, taake tum isse Barson aur Tarikh ke Hisaab (Lunar Year) maloom kar sako. Ye sab kuchh Allah ne Haq ke saath paida kiya hai. Woh Ilm rakhnewalon ke liye apni Nishaniyon ko khol khol kar bayan kar rah hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 5)

📚📖 ☀️🌙

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Allah Ta'ala Nabi e Akram (saww) ki misal Suraj se di hai aur unke Wasi Hazrat Ali (as) ki misal Chand se di hai aur farmaya hai (10:5). Maqsad ye hai ke Suraj ki Roshni zaati hai aur Chand Suraj ka Noor Munakas karta hai (Reflective Light). Usi tarah se Muhammad Mustafa (saww) par Qur'an nazil hua hai aur Hazrat Ali (as) ne unke Seene se Seena mila kar Ilm hasil kiya hai."_

(Roza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

☀️🌙

Abu Zar Ghafari ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) Suraj ghurub hote dekh sawal kiya ke ye kaha ghayab ho gaya?

Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

_"Ye Aasmaan mein ghurub (Set) hota hai. Phir ye ek se doosre Aasmaan ki taraf jata hai yahan tak ke Satven Aasman tak jaata hai. Wahan jaa kar Sajdah karta hai aur iske saath us par Mo'akkil Farishte bhi Sajdah karte hain. Phir Suraj arz karta hai. Khadaya! Mere liye kiya Hukm hai agar Hukm ho to mein Maghrib se tulu karun aur agar Hukm ho to apne Mashriq se tulu karun? Isi ke mutalliq Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: "Aur Suraj apne muqarrar Raaste par chalta rehta hai, ye Ghalib aur Dana ka muqarrar kiya hua andaza hai."(Yaseen: 38)."_

_"Iske baad Jibrael Ameen (as) uske Din ki Lambai ya Kami ke mutabiq Noor e Arsh se Roshni ki Khil'at le kar use pehnata hai aur woh is Noorani poshak ko yun pahenta hai jaisa ke tum mein se koi shakhs Libaas pahenta hai. Iske baad Suraj Aasmaani Fiza ka safar karke apne matlah (Rising place) se tulu karta hai."_

Phir AanHazrat (saww) ne farmaya:

_"Goya mehsoos kar raha hun ke Teen Raaton ki miqdar mein ise thehra liya gaya hai aur use Noor ki Khil'at nahi pehnai gayi aur use Hukm diya jaa raha hai ke woh simte Maghrib se tulu kare. Allah Ta'ala ne iske mutalliq farmaya: "Jab Suraj ki chadar ko lapet diya jayega aur Sitare bikhar jayenge."_

_" Chand ki bhi isi tarah ki manzilen tay karta hai...."_

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Jab dhoop mein baithho to Suraj ki taraf pusht (back) kar ke baithho kyun ki is se makhfi (hidden) Bimari duur hoti hai."_

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p598)

🤲🏻

 *يَا مَنْ يُقَلِّبُ اللَّيْلَ وَالنَّهَارَ، يَا مَنْ جَعَلَ الظُّلُمَاتِ وَالْاَنْوَارَ، يَا مَنْ خَلَقَ الظِّلَّ وَالْحَرُوْرَ، يَا مَنْ سَخَّرَ الشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ، يَا مَنْ قَدَّرَ الْخَيْرَ وَالشَّرَّ، يَا مَنْ خَلَقَ الْمَوْتَ وَالْحَيَاةَ، يَا مَنْ لَهُ الْخَلْقُ*

(Joshane Kabir No.62)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

**********************************

           *9th Shawwal 1441*

      *2nd June 2020, Tuesday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         ♦ _*RAAT AUR DIN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1442)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ فِی ٱخۡتِلَـٰفِ ٱلَّیۡلِ وَٱلنَّهَارِ وَمَا خَلَقَ ٱللَّهُ فِی ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ لَـَٔایَـٰتࣲ لِّقَوۡمࣲ یَتَّقُونَ.*

_"Yaqeenan Raat o Din ki amad o raft aur jo kuchh Allah ne Aasmaano aur Zameen mein paida kiya hai un sab mein Ahle Taqwa ke liye Nishaniyan paayi jaati hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 6)

📚📖 ☀️🎆

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Ye Ayat pichhli Ayat se paiwast hai. Guzishta Ayat mein Suraj aur Chand ka zikr tha. Is Ayat mein Raat o Din ka zikr hai. Earth Rotation aur Suraj ki Roshni ke zahir aur chhupne se Din wa Raat wujood mein aate hain. Earth Movement ki wajah se alternate Din wa Raat mein changes hote rehte hain. Agar aisa na hota to Zameen par Zindagi possible nahi thi. Zameen par hi Suraj ki jagah badalne se Mausam mein bhi tabdeeliya aati hain. Din Raat ke badalne se ham Dino ki ginti karte hain. Isi se Calendar chalta hai. Isi se Time badalta hai. Aur hamari Zindagi ki ghadi chal rahi hai. In par agar gaur karen to ye hamare liye Allah ko pehchanne ki Nishaniyan hain. Isi Allah jagah jagah Qur'an mein farmata hai ke Hamari Nishaniyon ko dekho aur ghaur karo.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Haalat e bimari ya Dard mein Ek Raat jaagna behtar hai ek saal ki Ibadat se."_

(Furoo e Kafi, v1, p272)

☀️🎆

Imam Ali (as):

_"Jis tarah Suraj aur Raat ikattha nahi ho sakte, isi tarah Allah ki Mohabbat aur Duniya ki mohabbat bhi ek saath nahi ho sakte."_

(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)

🤲🏻

*صَلَوَاتُ اللّٰهِ عَلَيْهِ وَ عَلٰى اٰبَاۤئِهِ الْاَئِمَّةِ الْهَادِيْنَ وَ الْقَادَةِ الْمَيَامِيْنِ مَا طَلَعَتْ كَوَاكِبُ الْاَسْحَارِ وَ اَوْرَقَتِ الْاَشْجَارُ وَ اَيْنَعَتِ الْاَثْمَارُ وَ اخْتَلَفَ اللَّيْلُ وَ النَّهَارُ وَ غَرَّدَتِ الْاَطْيَارُ اَللّٰهُمَّ انْفَعْنَا بِحُبِّهِ وَ احْشُرْنَا فِيْ زُمْرَتِهِ وَ تَحْتَ لِوَاۤئِهِ اِلٰهَ الْحَقِّ اٰمِيْنَ رَبَّ الْعَالَمِيْنَ۔*

(Ziyarat e Sahibul Amr (atfs) ke baad ki Dua - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

**********************************

           *10th Shawwal 1441*

     *3rd June 2020, Wednesday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               ♦ _*AAMAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1443)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ لَا یَرۡجُونَ لِقَاۤءَنَا وَرَضُوا۟ بِٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَٱطۡمَأَنُّوا۟ بِهَا وَٱلَّذِینَ هُمۡ عَنۡ ءَایَـٰتِنَا غَـٰفِلُونَ. * أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ مَأۡوَىٰهُمُ ٱلنَّارُ بِمَا كَانُوا۟ یَكۡسِبُونَ *  إِنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَعَمِلُوا۟ ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ یَهۡدِیهِمۡ رَبُّهُم بِإِیمَـٰنِهِمۡۖ تَجۡرِی مِن تَحۡتِهِمُ ٱلۡأَنۡهَـٰرُ فِی جَنَّـٰتِ ٱلنَّعِیمِ.*

_"Beshak woh log jo Hamse milne ki umeeden nahi rakhte aur Duniyavi Zindagi par qaane aur Mutmain ho chuke hain aur woh log jo hamari Ayaat se Ghafil hain. Ye sab woh hain jinke Aamaal ki bena par unka thikana Dozakh hai."_

_"Beshak jo log Imaan laye aur Nek Amal kiye unke Imaan ki badaulat unka Parwardigar unhe Hidayat dega. Ne'mat bhari Jannaton mein unke neeche Nehre beh rahi hongi."_

(Surah Yunus: 7 - 9)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Zahir hai ke is Ayat mein Mulaqat se murad hissi/physical meeting nahi hai hai kyonki Khuda ko dekhna mahal hai. Yahan isse murad Parwardigar ki Jaza wa Saza se mulaqat hai. Iske alawa Shuhood e Baatini hai yani Insaan Khuda ke Wujood/Huzoor ka ehsaas karega. Jo log is Duniya ki Muhabbat mein doobe hue hain, isiko Permanent Abode samajhte hain, woh is par raazi rehte hain. Ye log ghaflat mein hain, inhe nahi maloom marne ke baad kya hoga.

👉🏻

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Logo'n mein sabse zyada ghaafil (negligent) woh hai jo Duniya ke badalte haalaat se sabak (lesson) nahi leta."_

(Nahjul Fasaha)

👉🏻

Doosra giroh woh hai jo is Duniya ke bajai Akherat ko muqaddam rakhta hai. Apne pukhta Imaan ki wajah se woh Akherat ko hasil karta hai.

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Jab Momin apni Qabr se niklega to uske Aamaal ek pyari surat mein numaya honge aur usse kahenge ke mein tera Amal hun aur ek Noor sa aayega jo use Jannat ki taraf Hidayat karega."_

(Tafseer Fakhruddin Raazi, Vol 17, P-40)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Momin ke saaye ke alaawa Qayamat ki Zameen Aag hai. Beshak uska Sadqa  hi uska saayebaa'n (shade) hoga."_

(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aaamal)

📝

Imam Ali (as):

_"Maal Maut tak saath deta hai, Aulaad Qabr tak aur Aamaal Hashr tak."_

(Khisaal, Chapter3)

🤲🏻

_"Khudaya! Meri Musibat Azeem hai. Meri bad haali hadd se aage badhi hui hai. Mere Aamaal mein kotahi hai. Mujhe Kamzoriyon ki Zanjeeron ne jakad kar baitha diya hai aur mujhe door daraz umeedon ne fawaid se rok diya hai. Duniya ne dhoke mein mubtila rakha hai aur Nafs ne Khayanat aur tal matol mein mubtila rakha hai."_

(Dua-e-Kumail)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

**********************************

           *11th Shawwal 1441*

       *4th June 2020, Thursday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*AL HAMDO LILLAHE RABBIL AALAMIN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1444)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*دَعۡوَىٰهُمۡ فِیهَا سُبۡحَـٰنَكَ ٱللَّهُمَّ وَتَحِیَّتُهُمۡ فِیهَا سَلَـٰمࣱۚ وَءَاخِرُ دَعۡوَىٰهُمۡ أَنِ ٱلۡحَمۡدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ ٱلۡعَـٰلَمِینَ.*

_"Wahan unka qaul ye hoga ke Khudaya! Tu Paak hai aur unka Tohfa Salam hoga aur unka Akhari Bayan ye hoga ke tamam Tareefe Allah, Rabbul Aalamin, ke liye hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 10)

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Jab koi shakhs "Alhamdo Lillah" kehta hai to Khuda use Duniya o Akherat ki Ne'maat ata farmata hai aur uske liye Duniya o Akherat ki Ne'maat muttasil hoti hain. Jab Ahle Jannat, Jannat mein dakhil honge to unki pehli guftugu "Alhamdo Lillah" hogi. Unki Duniyavi Kalam unse munqata ho jayegi, lekin "Alhamdo Lillah" ke alfaaz unke saath rahenge jaisa ke Allah Ta'ala farmata hai (10:10)"_

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

🤦🏻‍♂️

Imam Sadiq (as) se "Subhanallah" ke mutalliq daryaft kiya to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

_"Wo Allah ke Naamo mein se ek Naam hai aur Ahle Jannat ka bayan hai."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤵🏻

Imam Sadiq (as) ne Shiyon ke mutalliq farmaya:

_"Tum woh Khush Naseeb ho jinhe Khuda ki taraf se Salam ka Tohfa diya jayega."_

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🙏🏻

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Jab Momin ko Jannat mein kisi cheez ki zaroorat hogi to woh " *َّسُبحٰانَكَ اللّٰهُم* Subhana kallahumma" kahega to Jannat ke Khuddam uski matlooba shay fauran uske saamne pesh kar denge. Use Munh se us cheez ke Naam lene ki zaroorat hi mehsoos nahi hogi aur jab woh Khaana, Sharaab e Tahoor aur Hooron se Jinsi Lazzat hasil karke farigh honge to us waqt woh 'Alhamdo Lillahe Rabbil Aalamin' kahenge. Isi cheez ko Allah Ta'ala ne in Alfaaz mein farmaya (10:10)."_

(Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Hazrat Ali (as):

_"Jannat ki sab se Lazzat Laziz tareen aur Pakeeza tareen cheez Allah se Muhabbat rakhna, Allah ki wajah se Muhabbat rakhna aur Allah ki Hamd baja laana hai. Jab Ne'maat e Ilahi ka Mushaheda karenge to unke Dilon mein Khuda ki Muhabbat mojezin hogi to us waqt woh kahenge: 'Alhamdo Lillahe Rabbil Aalamin'."_

(Misbahush Shari'a, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*قَدْ نَشَرْتَ لِوَاۤءَالنَّصْرِ تُرٰی اَتَرَانَا نَحُفُّ بِكَ وَ اَنْتَ تَاُمُّ الْمَلَاَ وَ قَدْ مَلَاْتَ الْاَرْضَ عَدْلًا وَ اَذَقْتَ اَعْدَاۤئَكَ ھَوَانًا وَ عِقَابًا وَ اَبَرْتَ الْعُتَاۃَ وَ جَحَدَۃِ الْحَقِّ وَ قَطَعْتَ دَابِرَ الْمُتَكَبِّرِیْنَ وَ اجْتَثَثْتَ اُصُوْلَ الظَّالِمِیْنَ وَ نَحْنُ نَقُوْلُ الْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِیْنَ.*

(Dua-e-Nudba)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

           *12th Shawwal 1441*

         *5th June 2020, Friday*

♦ _*GUNAHGARO KO MOHLAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1445)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوۡ یُعَجِّلُ ٱللَّهُ لِلنَّاسِ ٱلشَّرَّ ٱسۡتِعۡجَالَهُم بِٱلۡخَیۡرِ لَقُضِیَ إِلَیۡهِمۡ أَجَلُهُمۡۖ فَنَذَرُ ٱلَّذِینَ لَا یَرۡجُونَ لِقَاۤءَنَا فِی طُغۡیَـٰنِهِمۡ یَعۡمَهُونَ.*

_"Agar Allah logon ke liye Burai mein itni jaldi karta jitna ke woh Bhalai ki jaldi chahte hain to unki mohlate Amal kab ki khatm ho gayi hoti."_

(Surah Yunus: 11)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Allah apne Bande par bahut Meherban rehta hai. Jaise Baap apne Bete par. Agar Insaan koi Nek karta to usko turant Ajr de diya jaata hai lekin agar woh koi Gunah karta hai to usko mohlat deta hai ke shayad  woh pasheman ho aur Tauba kar le.

👉🏻

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Khuda Wande Kareem ne Machhli ke shikaar karne waalo'n ko Maskh kar diya to kya hoga un logo'n ka jinhone na-haq Aulaad e Rasool (saww) ko qatl kiya aur unki hurmat ki hatak ki? Khuda Wande Kareem ne Duniya mein chaahe un logo'n ko Sazaa e Maskh nahi di lekin Azaab e Akherat jo unke liye tayyar hai wo us Maskh hone se bahut zyada hai. Pus, ek shakhs ne Imam (as) ki khidmat mein arz ki, "Yabna Rasulallah (as)! Kuchh Naasibi hum par aiteraaz karte hain ke agar qatl e Husain (as) na-jaayez hota aur Bani Israil ke Machhli ke shikaar se uska jurm sangeen hota to phir qaatilaan e Husain (as) par Khuda ka ghazab kyun naazil nahi hua jaisa ke Bani Israel ke Machhli ke shikaariyo'n par naazil hua?" Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Un Naasibiyo'n se kaho ke Iblees ka Gunah un logo'n se sangeen hai jo uske behkaane se Gumraah hue, lekin woh gharq ho gaye jinka Gunah halka tha aur woh gharq nahi hua jiska Gunah sangeen tha. Pus, Khuda ne apni maslehat se sangeen jurm waale ko mohlat de di aur halke jurm waale ko Moazzab (Azaab mein mubtela) kar diya. Isi tarah Bani Israel ke shikaari jo halke jurm waale the wo Moazzab (Azaab mein mubtela) ho gaye aur Husain (as) ke qaatil ko Iblees ki tarah ek waqt tak mohlat di gayi halaa'nki unka jurm sangeen tha." Phir aap se sawaal hua, "Ye fe'l to guzishta zamane Bani Israil ka tha phir zamana e Islam ke Bani Israel ko is fe'l se kyun mukhatib kiya jaa raha hai?" To Imam (as) ne farmaya jiska ma-hasl (conclulsion) ye hai, "Ek shakhs ki qaum agar kisi ko qatl kar de ya kahi'n daaka daal de to us shakhs ko kaha jaa sakta hai ke tum ne fulaa'n ko qatl kiya ya fulaa'n par daaka daala, halaa'nki ye us qatl ya daake mein shareek nahi tha. Aur iske alaawa kyunki Bani Israel apne purvajo'n (forefathers) ke af'aal (actions) par raazi the, lihaaza unko unke fe'l ka shareek qaraar diya gaya. Aur unko taubeekh aur sarzanish (daa'nt fattkaar) ki gayi taaki apne faasid aqeede (corrupted belief) se baaz aa kar Islami taalimaat par amal karne ki koshish kare."

(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v2, p120)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Neki ke iraade par ek Sawaab aur Amal par 10 Sawaab hain; aur buraayi ke iraade par koi azaab nahi. (Bure) Amal ke baad 9 ghante ki mohlat milti hai ke agar Tauba kare to Nama e Amal mein na likha jaaye warna likh diya jaaye."_

(Khisaal, Chapter9)

🙏🏻

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Insaan ke 2 kaandho'n par 2 Farishte muqarrar hain. Daayen jaanib (right side) wala Farishta baayen jaanib (left side) waale par Haakim aur Ameer hai. Jab insaan koi bura amal anjaam deta hai to daayen jaanib wala baayen jaanib wale se kehta hai, "Likhne mein jaldi mat kar, usko 7 ghanto'n (7 hours) ki mohlat de'. Jab 7 ghanto'n ki mohlat khatm ho jaaye aur wo shakhs Tauba na kare to phir wo daayen jaanib wala kehta hai, "Likho, ye shakhs kitna be-hayaa aur be-sharm hai."_

(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v2, p154)

🙏🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Jab Banda e Momin Gunah karta hai to usko Mohlat di jaati hai Subah se Raat tak. Pus, agar woh Allah se Tauba o Astagfar karta hai to woh Gunah nahi likha jaata."_

(Al Kaafi, v5, p37)

🤲🏻

_"Meine Gunah ke naam par tezi se sabqat ki hai. Mein wohi hun jise Tu ne Mohlat di hai to mein sanbhla nahi. Pardah poshi ki hai to mein haya nahi ki. Gunah kiye hain to badhta hi chala gaya, aur Tu ne Apne Hilm se Mohlat di aur Apne Pardeh ki Aib poshi ki jaise ke Tujhe khud sharm aa gayi hai...."_

(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumali - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           *13th Shawwal 1441*

        *6th June 2020, Saturday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ _*KHUDGARZ INSAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1446)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا مَسَّ ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنَ ٱلضُّرُّ دَعَانَا لِجَنۢبِهِۦۤ أَوۡ قَاعِدًا أَوۡ قَاۤىِٕمࣰا فَلَمَّا كَشَفۡنَا عَنۡهُ ضُرَّهُۥ مَرَّ كَأَن لَّمۡ یَدۡعُنَاۤ إِلَىٰ ضُرࣲّ مَّسَّهُۥۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ زُیِّنَ لِلۡمُسۡرِفِینَ مَا كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ.*

_"Insaan par jab koi sakht lahma aata hai to woh khade baithe aur lete Hamko Sadayen deta hai magar jab Ham uski Musibat hata dete hain to woh aisa chal nikalta hai goya usne kabhi apne bure waqt mein Hamko pukara hi nahi tha. Isi tarah se had se guzarne walon ke liye unke Aamaal khush numa bana diye gaye hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 12)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Is Ayat mein Insaan ko Khud garz, matlabi bataya gaya hai. Jab woh mushkil mein padta hai, jab be sahara ho jata hai, uske haath kotah ho jate hain to apne Rab ki tarah haathon ko buland karta hai, pehlu ke bal, sote, baithe, khade ho kar Rab ko pukarta hai. Yehi Haadsaat, Mushkilaat, Balayen, Bimaariyan Insaani Fitrat ke Pardon ko khol kar rakh deti hain, saare Hijabaat uth jaate hain aur Mukhlis Bande ki tarah sirf Usi se lau lagata hai. Jaisa ke is Ayat mein bhi is baat ka zikr hai

*فَإِذَا رَكِبُوا۟ فِی ٱلۡفُلۡكِ دَعَوُا۟ ٱللَّهَ مُخۡلِصِینَ لَهُ ٱلدِّینَ فَلَمَّا نَجَّىٰهُمۡ إِلَى ٱلۡبَرِّ إِذَا هُمۡ یُشۡرِكُونَ*

_"Jab ye log Kashti par sawar hote hain to Allah Ta'ala ko hi pukarte hain, Uske ke liye Ibaadat ko khaalis kar ke. Phir jab Woh inhe bacha kar Khushki par le aata hai to yakayak ye Shirk karne lagte hain."_

(Surah Ankabut: 65)

Lekin jaise hi uska Maslah hal ho jata hai, Musibat o mushkelat door ho jati hain, Bimaari se Shifayab hota hai, apni Duniya mein mashgool ho jata hai, phir apne Rab ko aisa bhool jata hai jaise uska Usse kabhi rabta tha hi nahi. Kushaish, Comforts, Sukoon mein Insaan Maghroor o mutakabbir ho jata hai. Woh apne saamne kisi ko kuchh samajhta hi nahi.

Isliye har Insaan ko uski Zindagi mein kuchh jhatke diye jate hain taake woh Allah ki taraf palte.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Allah (swt):

_"Balaa o Musibat se maayus mat ho; Jaise Sona Aag mein pighla kar parkha jaata hai waise Momin Balaa'on mein parkha jaata hai."_

(Al-Hadith Al-Qudsi - ABISN, Nairobi, Kenya)

👉🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Allah ki sabse Mehboob Makhlooq woh hai jo kisi bhi Ne'mat ke ataa hone par Shukr kare aur Musibat ke waqt Sabr kare."_

(Miskhat ul Anwaar)

🤲🏻

*اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ ۟اِلْفُلْكِ الْجَارِيَةِ فِي اللُّجَجِ الْغَامِرَةِ يَأْمَنُ مَنْ رَكِبَهَا وَ يَغْرَقُ مَنْ تَرَكَهَا اَلْمُتَقَدِّمُ لَهُمْ مَارِقٌ وَ الْمُتَاَخِّرُ عَنْهُمْ زَاهِقٌ وَ اللَّازِمُ لَهُمْ لَاحِقٌ...*

(Salwat Nima Shaban -Mafateeh)

*يَا فُلْكَ النَّجَاةِ الَّذِيْ مَنْ رَكِبَهُ نَجَا وَ مَنْ تَاَخَّرَ عَنْهُ هَوٰى.*

_"Aye Safeena e Najaat, jo is mein chadh gaya Najaat paa gaya, jisne tark kiya halak hua."_

(Special Ziyarat on Wiladat of Rasoole Khuda (saww))

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          *7th June 2020, Sunday,*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ _*AZAAB-E-ILAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1447)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدۡ أَهۡلَكۡنَا ٱلۡقُرُونَ مِن قَبۡلِكُمۡ لَمَّا ظَلَمُوا۟ وَجَاۤءَتۡهُمۡ رُسُلُهُم بِٱلۡبَیِّنَـٰتِ وَمَا كَانُوا۟ لِیُؤۡمِنُوا۟ۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ نَجۡزِی ٱلۡقَوۡمَ ٱلۡمُجۡرِمِینَ *  ثُمَّ جَعَلۡنَـٰكُمۡ خَلَـٰۤىِٕفَ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ مِنۢ بَعۡدِهِمۡ لِنَنظُرَ كَیۡفَ تَعۡمَلُونَ.*

_"Hamne tumse pehli Aqwaam (Tribes, Groups) ko halaak kar diya jab unhone Zulm ki rawish apnayi aur unke Rasool unke paas khuli Nishaniyan le kar aaye magar woh Imaan laanewale na the. Ham isi tarah se Mujrim ko Badla diya karte hain. Iske baad Hamne tumko Zameen par unka Janasheen bana diya taake Ham ye dekhen ke tum kaise Amal karte ho?"_

(Surah Yunus: 13 - 14)

📚📖 🌵

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Isse milti julti doosri Ayat jiska zikr ham Dec, 2017 mein kar chuke hai. Mufhoom same hai isliye phir se repeat kar rahe hain:

*أَلَمْ يَرَوْا كَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا.........*

_"Kiya unhone nahi dekha ke Hamne unse qabl kitni aisi qaumon ko halak kiya hai jinhen Hamne Zameen mein aisa Aqdaar diya tha ke is jaisa Aqdaar tumhe nahi diya. Hamne un par Aasmaan se khoob Baarish barsayen aur Hamne unke neeche Nehren baha di thi. Akhirkar Hamne unhein Gunahon ki padaash mein halaak kar diya aur unki jagah doosri qaumon ko le aye."_

(Surah An'am: 6)

👥👉🏻

Zajaj ka kahna hai ke Qarn *قرن* ka itlaq us muddat ke logon par hota hai jin mein koi Nabi ho ya Ahle Ilm ka koi tabqa ho aur is mein kam saal ya zyada saal ho isse koi farq nahi padta kiyonki Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:

*خيركم قرني ثم الذين يلونهم.*

_"Mera daur sab se behtar hai. Phir un logon ka daur behtar hai jo iske baad ayenge."_

(Tafseer Majmaul Bayan)

🐲

Allah ne Guroor o Takabbur karne wale, Sarkash, Zalim logon par etaab ki barish barsa kar halaak kar diya. Ye sabaq ainda qaumon ke liye hai ke sarkashi ka natija kiya hota hai.

Aaj kal bhi aap log dekhte honge ke kahin Selaab, to kahin Zalzala to kahin bijli ka girna wa bhari barsat hona jiske natije mein sekdon ya hazaron log halaak ho jaate hain. Allah Zalim nahi, Woh zulm nahi karta lekin Zalim ko kadi se kadi saza bhi deta hai. Ye sab hadsaat o waqeat doosron logon ke liye sabaq hote hain taake woh hoshiyar ho jayen.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 🌵🐲

Ameerul Mo'meneen Imam Ali (as)

_"Tajjub hai aur mujhe kaise tajjub na ho un giroho'n ki khataao'n par jinhone apne Deen ki Hujjato'n mein ikhtelaaf paida kar rakhe hain. Jo na Nabi ke naqsh e qadam par chalte hain, na Wasi ke amal ki pairavi karte hain, na Gaib par Imaan laate hain, na Aib se daaman bachaate hain. Maskook (doubtful) cheezo'n par amal karte hain aur apni khwaisho'n (ki duniya) mein chalte phirte hain. Unke nazdeek bus wohi cheez achchi hai jisko wo achcha samajhte hain aur wohi cheez buri hai jisko wo bura jaante hain. Mushkil gutthiyo'n ko suljhaane ke liye unhone apne Nafso'n par etemaad kar liya hai aur mushtaba (Doubtful) cheezo'n mein apni raai par bharosa kar liya hai, goya unme se har shakhs apna Imam hai aur usne apni jagah jo faisla apni raai se kar liya hai uske baare mein ye khayaal karta hai ke ise qaabil e itminaan zariyo'n se haasil kiya hai."_

(Gorar ul Hakam, Vol 2, p494, Nahjul Balagah, Khutba 88 (Jisme Logo'n Ki Halaakat Ke Asbaab Bayaan Kiye Gaye Hain)

🤲🏻

Bare Ilaha hame un gunahon se Ma'af farma jo Tera Ghazab se qareeb karte hain aur hamari halakat ka sabab bante hain.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*QUR'AN MEIN TABDEELI KA MUTALBA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1448)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا تُتۡلَىٰ عَلَیۡهِمۡ ءَایَاتُنَا بَیِّنَـٰتࣲ قَالَ ٱلَّذِینَ لَا یَرۡجُونَ لِقَاۤءَنَا ٱئۡتِ بِقُرۡءَانٍ غَیۡرِ هَـٰذَاۤ أَوۡ بَدِّلۡهُۚ قُلۡ مَا یَكُونُ لِیۤ أَنۡ أُبَدِّلَهُۥ مِن تِلۡقَاۤىِٕ نَفۡسِیۤۖ إِنۡ أَتَّبِعُ إِلَّا مَا یُوحَىٰۤ إِلَیَّۖ إِنِّیۤ أَخَافُ إِنۡ عَصَیۡتُ رَبِّی عَذَابَ یَوۡمٍ عَظِیمࣲ.قُل لَّوۡ شَاۤءَ ٱللَّهُ مَا تَلَوۡتُهُۥ عَلَیۡكُمۡ وَلَاۤ أَدۡرَىٰكُم بِهِۦۖ فَقَدۡ لَبِثۡتُ فِیكُمۡ عُمُرࣰا مِّن قَبۡلِهِۦۤۚ أَفَلَا تَعۡقِلُونَ. * قُل لَّوۡ شَاۤءَ ٱللَّهُ مَا تَلَوۡتُهُۥ عَلَیۡكُمۡ وَلَاۤ أَدۡرَىٰكُم بِهِۦۖ فَقَدۡ لَبِثۡتُ فِیكُمۡ عُمُرࣰا مِّن قَبۡلِهِۦۤۚ أَفَلَا تَعۡقِلُونَ.*

_"Jab unke saamne Hamari wazeh Ayaat padhi jati hain to woh log jo Hamse milne ki umeed nahi rakhte, kehte hain ke iske bajaye koi aur Qur'an lao ya is mein tabdeeli karo. Aap keh den ke mujhe apni taraf se is mein tabdeeli karne ka koi ikhtiyar nahi hai. Mein to sirf is Amr ka itteba (follow) karta hun jiski meri taraf Wahy ki jati hai. Mein apne Parwardigar ki Nafarmani karun to mujhe Azeem Din ke Azaab ka khauf hai. Aap keh den ke agar Khuda ki Mashiyyat yehi hoti to mein tumhare saamne Qur'an ki tilawat na karta aur Allah tumhe iski khabar tak na deta. Aakhir mein isse pehle bhi tumhare tumhare darmiyan ek muddat tak reh chuka hun. Kya tum Aql se kaam nahi lete?"_

_"Aap keh den ke agar Khuda ki Mashiyyat  yehi hoti to mein tumhare saamne Qur'an ki tilawat na karta aur Allah tumhe iski khabar tak na deta. Aakhir mein isse pehle bhi tumhare tumhare darmiyan ek muddat tak reh chuka hun. Kya tum Aql se kaam nahi lete?"_

(Surah Yunus: 15 - 16)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Quresh ne AanHazrat (saww) se kaha tha ke jo Qur'an Aap pesh kar rahe hain use Aap (saww) ne Yahood o Nasaara ki zabani hasil kiya hai. Lehaza Aap (saww) iske bajai koi Quran pesh karen aur is mein tabdeeli layen. Is par AanHazrat (saww) ne jawab diya iski authority mujhe nahi hai. Aise bhi 40 Saal Rasoole Khuda (saww) Kuffar ke darmiyan rahe, bachpan dekha, ladakpan dekha, kabhi koi ghalti ya Jihalat dekhi? Balke Amanatdari aur Sadaqat ki sanad unse mili. To phir ye demand be matlab hai.

(Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Aaj bhi ye demand jahilon ki taraf se hota rehta hai jaise Tasleema Nasreen, ya Salman Rushdie. Kehte hain 1400 Saal se ek Kitab chali aa rahe hai, ye Purani aur farsooda ho chuki hai, ab Zamana badal gaya hai, ye sab purane logon ki baaten hain.

In logon ko ye nahi maloom ke ye Allah ka Kalam hai aur is par sirf Allah ki Authority hai. Qur'an Insaano ki banayi hui Kitab nahi. Allah Hakeem hai aur Usse behter koi Ilm nahi rakhta, Woh bakhubi Jaanta hai, ham nahi jaante. Isliye tabdeeli ka sawal hi paida nahi hota.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Kuffar e Makkah ke mutalba jaisa ek aur mutalba Fazail e Ali (as) ke Munkarin ne bhi kiya tha. Unhone bhi AanHazrat (saww) se kaha tha ke Aap (saww) Ali (as) ke Fazail mein kuchh kami karen. Magar AanHazrat (saww) ne aisa karne se inkaar kar diya tha."_

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*وَهُوَ شَهْرُ رَمَضَانَ، الَّذِيْ اَنْزَلْتَ فِيْهِ الْقُرْاٰنَ، هُدًى لِّلنَّاسِ وَبَيِّنَاتٍ مِنَ الْهُدىٰ وَالْفُرْقَانِ،..*

(Dua Ya Aliyyo Ya Azeem - Mafateeh)

                    ♦ _*SHIRK*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1449)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَمَنۡ أَظۡلَمُ مِمَّنِ ٱفۡتَرَىٰ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ كَذِبًا أَوۡ كَذَّبَ بِـَٔایَـٰتِهِۦۤۚ إِنَّهُۥ لَا یُفۡلِحُ ٱلۡمُجۡرِمُونَ*

_"Bhala isse badh kar Zalim aur kaun ho sakta hai jo Khuda par Jhoot tarashe ya Allah ki Ayaat ki Takzeeb kare. Yaqeenan Mujrim kabhi Falah nahi payenge."_

(Surah Yunus: 17)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Ham us Ayat ki Tafseer repeat kar rahe hain jo ham 27 Dec 2017 mein post kar chuke hain: Aaj ki Ayat aur ye Ayat same hai.

*وَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنِ افْتَرَىٰ عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا أَوْ كَذَّبَ بِآيَاتِهِ ۗ إِنَّهُ لَا يُفْلِحُ الظَّالِمُونَ*

_"Aur isse badh kar bhala koi Zalim kaun hoga jo Allah par jhoota Bohtan lagaye ya Allah ki nishaniyon ki takzeeb kare. Yaqeenan Zalim Nijaat nahi payenge."_

(Surah An'am 21)

Is Ayat mein Allah Mushrekin ke bare mein kinayatan sawal kar raha ke issa bada Zalim kaun ho sakta hai? *"ومن اظلم*" Qur'an mein 15 jaghon par mukhtalif maana mein aya hai. Jaise (Anaam: 21, A'raf:37, Zumar:32)

Shirk Zulm e Azeem hai jaisa ke H. Luqman ne Quran mein apne bete ko nasihat karte waqt farmaya. Zulm sangeen is liye hai kiyonki Zulm 3 par ho raha hai.

(1) Allah par Jhoota Bohtan sab se bada zulm.

(2) Apne aap par Zulm, kiyonki Parwardigar Buzurg o Bartar ke muqabile mein Patthar ya mitti ke buton ke samne apne aap ko gira kar pasti ki jaanib le jaata hai.

(3) Ma'ashere (Society) par zulm karta hai kiyonki uski bure asaraat Society par padte hain to society puraganda ho jaati hai.

Allah ko jhutla kar woh ek Azeem Gunah Karta hai. Gunah ka murtakib hona apne aap par zulm karna hai. Iske liye zaroori hai ke Jihad e Nafs kare.

Insaan ki Fitrat gawara nahi karti ke woh apne Khaaliq ko na pahchaane. Apne Paalnewale ko woh kaise bhula sakta hai ya tohmat laga sakta hai.

🍁

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Zulm 3 tarah ke hain: Ek Zulm aisa hai jise Allah Ta'ala baksh dega, aur ek zulm aisa hai jise Allah hargiz na bakhshega, aur ek zulm aisa hai jis se chashm-poshi (nazar-andaaz) nahi karega. *Pus, wo zulm jise Allah hargiz na bakhshega wo Shirk hai.* Wo zulm jise Allah baksh dega wo aisa hai jise bande ne khud apne hi upar kiya hoga. Aur wo zulm jis se Wo chashm-poshi na farmayega wo Haqqul Ibaad (bando'n ke haq) ke mutalliq hai."_

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p109)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Zulm karte waqt apne baare mein Khuda ke Adl ko yaad rakho aur taaqat o qudrat ke waqt ye yaad rakho ke tum Khuda ki Qudrat se baahar nahi ho."_

(Gorar ul Hakam, v2, p33)

🍁

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Mujhe 3 afraad ke alaawa Ummat ke tamaam afraad ki najaat ki ummeed hai jo hamare haq ki maarefat rakhte hun._

_(1) Zaalim Badshah,_

_(2) Khwaishaat ka ghulam,_

_(3) Jo khule aam bad-kaariyaa'n karta hai."_

(Khisaal, p76)

🤲🏻

*فَمَا تَنَاقَضَتْ اَفْعَالُكَ وَ لَا اخْتَلَفَتْ اَقْوَالُكَ وَ لَا تَقَلَّبَتْ اَحْوَالُكَ وَ لَا ادَّعَيْتَ وَ لَا افْتَرَيْتَ عَلَى اللّٰهِ كَذِبًا.......*

(Ziyarat Aminullah - Mafateeh)

♦ _*BUT-PARASTI (IDOL WORSHIP)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1450)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَیَعۡبُدُونَ مِن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ مَا لَا یَضُرُّهُمۡ وَلَا یَنفَعُهُمۡ وَیَقُولُونَ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ شُفَعَـٰۤؤُنَا عِندَ ٱللَّهِۚ قُلۡ أَتُنَبِّـُٔونَ ٱللَّهَ بِمَا لَا یَعۡلَمُ فِی ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَلَا فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِۚ سُبۡحَـٰنَهُۥ وَتَعَـٰلَىٰ عَمَّا یُشۡرِكُونَ.*

_"Ye log Khuda ki Pooja chod kar unki Pooja kar rahe hain jo na to unhe Nuqsaan pahuncha sakte hain aur na hi unhe Fayda de sakte hain aur woh kehte hain ke ye (But) Allah ke haan hamare Shifarihi hain. Aap keh den kya tum Allah ko is baat ki khabar dena chahte ho jise woh na to Aasmaano mein jaanta hai aur na Zameen mein? Woh har Nuqs (Defect) se Paak o Pakeeza hai aur Woh is Shirk se Buland o Bala hai jo woh kar rahe hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 18)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Quraish ye kehte the ke Allah ki Shaan Buland o Baala hai. Us tak hamari rasai nahi hai. Ham in Buton ko apne liye Khuda ke haan zariya e Taqarrub samajh kar poojte hain. Ye Khuda ki bargah mein hamare Shifareshi hain. Allah Ta'ala ne inki tardeed (reject) karte hue farmaya ke tumne kaise Shifareshi dhoondh liye hain, Khuda to inhe pahchanta tak nahi hai.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

💩

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko Hukm diya tha ke woh Hazrat Ismail (as) ko Makkah ki be Aab o gaya (Barren Land) mein chhod aayen. Chunanche Aap (as) ne Hukm e Khuda Wandi par Amal kiya tha aur Aap (as) ne apne aur apni Aulad ke mutalliq Khuda se ye Dua maangi:_

*وَٱجۡنُبۡنِی وَبَنِیَّ أَن نَّعۡبُدَ ٱلۡأَصۡنَامَ.*

_"Khudaya! Mujhe aur meri Aulad ko But Parasti se mehfooz rakhna."_(14:35)

_"Allah Ta'ala ne Aap (as) ki ye Dua qubool farmayi aur Aulad e Ismail (as) mein se koi bhi But Parast nahi tha, jabke Arab ke doosre Qabael But Parast the. Aulad e Ismail (as) ke afraad Buton ko Khuda maanne ke bajaye Khuda ki bargah mein Shafa'at karne wale maante the. Agarche is Aqeede ki wajah se woh Kafir zaroor ho gaye, lekin woh Sanam Parast (Idol Worshiper) hargiz nahi the."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_" Agar koi But-Parast (Idol-worshipper) bhi marte waqt mazhabe Shia ka aiteqaad aur Aimma e Masumeen (as) ki Imamat ka waaqai iqraar kar lega to aatish e Jahannum uske kisi jism ke hisse ko na chhuegi."_

Tehzeeb ul Islam, p318

🚩

Imam Ali (as):

_"Wallah! Na mere baap ne buuto'n ki parastish (idol-worship) ki, na mere dada Abdul Muttalib ne, na mere jadd e buzurg J. Haashim ne, na Abde Munaaf ne. Balke wo log Kaabe ki jaanib rukh kar ke Namaz padhte the aur Deen e Ibrahim (as) par qaayam the aur Rasule Khuda (saww) ke Deen se mutamassik rahe."_

(Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p67)

🤲🏻

*وَ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ كَمَاۤ اَضْعَفْتَ بِهِ الْاَمْوَالَ وَ اَحْرَزْتَ بِهِ مِنَ الْاَهْوَالِ وَ كَسَرْتَ بِهِ الْاَصْنَامَ وَ رَحِمْتَ بِهِ الْاَنَامَ.....*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     *11th June 2020, Thursday*

      ♦ _*TAUHEED E FITRAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1451)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا كَانَ ٱلنَّاسُ إِلَّاۤ أُمَّةࣰ وَ ٰ⁠حِدَةࣰ فَٱخۡتَلَفُوا۟ۚ وَلَوۡلَا كَلِمَةࣱ سَبَقَتۡ مِن رَّبِّكَ لَقُضِیَ بَیۡنَهُمۡ فِیمَا فِیهِ یَخۡتَلِفُونَ.*

_"Ibteda mein tamam log ek hi Ummat the baad mein unhone aapas mein ikhtelaf kiya aur agar tere Rab ki taraf se pehle se ek baat tai na kar li gayi hoti to jis cheez mein woh ikhtelaf kar rahe hain uska Faisla kar diya jata."_

(Surah Yunus: 19)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Is Ayat mein is baat ka zikr hai ke har Insaan Mowahhid (Tauheed) par paida hota hai. Insaani Fitrat mein Tauheed basa hua hai. Kyonki ye Insaan Duniya mein aane se pehle Aalam e Zar mein Tauheed ka iqrar kar chuka hai. Lekin jaise hi Insaan is Duniya mein dakhil hota hai, woh bhool jaata hai. Misal ke taur par jaise Insaan sote mein Asli Khwab dekhte hain lekin jaise hi Aankh khulti hai woh bhul jate hain. Lekin kisi ke yaad dilane par use yaad bhi aa jata hai.

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka farman hai:

*كُلُّ مَولُودٍ يُولَدُ عَلَى الفِطرَةِ.*

_"Har Paida honewala apni Fitrat par paida hota hai, baad mein woh Yahoodi ya Nasrani banta hai."_

Qur'an mein bhi hai:

*فِطۡرَتَ ٱللَّهِ ٱلَّتِی فَطَرَ ٱلنَّاسَ عَلَیۡهَاۚ لَا تَبۡدِیلَ لِخَلۡقِ ٱللَّهِۚ*

(30:30)

Lekin Insaan jab Duniya mein aata hai to uski Fitrat par Parde pad jate hain. Gunahon, Zulm, Lalach, Duniyavi Muhabbat ki gard us par jam jati hai. Isliye woh Haqeeqat ko nahi dekh pata. Anbiya (as) wa Aimma (as) Insaan ki Hidayat ke liye isliye bheje gaye taake ye Insaan ki Fitrat ko jaga saken.

Hazrat Ali (as) ne Nahjul Balagha mein Anbiya ke bhejne ka maqsad yehi bataya.

Ikhtelaf ki wajah yehi hai kyonki Fitrat par pardah hai aur woh Haqeeqat ko nahi samajh pa rahe hain.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Reza (as):

_"Dilo'n ki Fitrat ye hai ke jo unpe Ehsaan kare usse Mohabbat aur jo usse Bad-sulooki kare usse Nafrat kare."_

(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v4, p325)

🤲🏻

*يَا رَحِيْمُ يَا رَحْمٰنُ حَتّٰى اِذَا اسْتَهْلَلْتُ نَاطِقًا بِالْكَلَامِ، اَتْمَمْتَ عَلَىَّ سَوَابغَ الْاِ نْعَامِ وَرَبَّيْتَنِىْ زَاۤئِدًا فِى كُلِّ عَامٍ حَتّٰىۤ اِذَا اكْتَمَلَتْ فِطْرَتِىْ وَاعْتَدَلَتْ مِرَّتِىْۤ اَوْجَبْتَ عَلَىَّ حُجَّتَكَ....*

_"Aye Khuda e Rahim o Karim! Teri Hasti bahut Buland o Bartar hai. Iske baad jab mein bolne ke layeq hua to Tu ne aur mukammal Ne'maten di aur tarbiyat ke zariye har Saal mujhe aage badhaya yahan tak ke meri Fitrat kamil ho gayi aur meri quwwat mazboot ho gayi to Tu ne mujh par Apni Hujjat ko lazim qarar de diya..."_

(Dua e Imam Husain (as) on Arafa - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*AYATUL UZMA KA INTEZAAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1452)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَ يَقُوْلُوْنَ لَوْلاَ اُنْزِلَ عَلَيْهِ آيَاتٌ مِنْ رَّبِّهِ فَقُلْ اِنَّمَا الْغَيْبُ ِللهِ فَانْتَظِرُوا اِنِّىْ مَعَكُمْ مِنَ الْمُنْتَظِرِيْنَ.*

_"Aur woh kehte hain ke is Nabi par uske Rab ki taraf se koi *Ayat* (Nishani - Rehbar) kyon nahi nazil hui? Aap keh den ke *Ghaib* ka Malik Allah hai tum *Intezaar* karo aur mein bhi tumhare saath *Intezaar* karne walon mein se hun."_

(Surah Yunus: 20)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Jab aane wala ayega, Dushman to saza payega, beda hamara par ho jayega, Adl ka parcham lahrayega, kab woh din ayega,

khatm kab ye intezaar ho jayega.

📖

Isi tarah ki Qur'an mein 'Ayat' lafz bahut jagah istemal hua hai. Aam Tafseeron mein Ayat se murad Mojeza bhi liya gaya hai. Jaisa ke bata chuke hain Quran ki ek Ayat se 50 Baatin Maani bhi hote hain. Yahan par ham Ayat se Murad 'Ilahi Hadi e Barhaq' le rahe hain riwayaat ke mutabiq.

👉🏻

Ayatullah yani Allah ki Nishaniyan. Allah ki Nishaniyan sirf Allah ki taraf se hoti hain. Rivayaton mein Aimma e Masoomeen (as) ko Ayatullah ka khitab diya gaya hai. Jo Allah ki Nishaniyon ki itteba' karega usko Momin kahte hain.

🕌

🔰

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Imam Ayatullah (Allah ki Ayat) hota hai aur Naskh Ayat ke qanoon ke tehet jab bhi Khuda kisi Imam ko wafat deta hai ya uska zikr faramosh karata hai to isse behtar ya us jaisa Imam uski sulb se paida karta hai. "_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain) (Ayat Nasikh Mansookh ke zel mein)

🌎

Aaj Duniya isi Ayatullahil Uzma ke Intezaar mein hai. Har kisi ka yehi sawal hai kyon is Ayat ka zahoor nahi ho raha. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya ke Ghaib ka Ilm sirf Allah ko hai, koi zahoor ka waqt muayyan nahi kar sakta. Kyonki Imam (as) ne farmaya: *كَذَّبَ الوَقَّتُون* (Waqt muayyan karnewala jhoota hai). Jab Khuda chahega Zahoor hoga, jab tak Intezaar karen.

🚩

Imam Reza (as) se Sawaal kiya ke kushaysh (Faraj) kab hogi?Aap (as) ne farmaya:

_"Kushayesh ka Intezaar Kushayesh ka ek hissa nahi hai? Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:_ *فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ.*

_"Sabr aur Kushayesh ka Intezaar behtareen cheez hai. Kya tu ne Allah ka ye farman nahi suna:_

*وَٱرۡتَقِبُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُمۡ رَقِیبࣱ* (Hud: 93)

*فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ.*

 (7: 71)

_"Lehaza tumhe Sabr se kaam lena chahiye. Hamesha Mayusi ke Waqt hi Kushayesh utarti hai. (Kyonki Shab e Siyah ka khatema hamesha Subah par hua karta hai.)Tumse pehle log tumse bade Sabir the."_

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 🌦

Rasule Khuda (saww)

_"Aye Ali (as)! Roz e Qayamat main, tum aur Jibreel (as) Siraat par baithenge aur koi uspar se nahi guzrega magar woh jiske paas tumhari Wilayat ke sabab se aatish e Dozakh se Nijaat ka parwana hoga."_

(Isbaat e Imamat - Allamah Majlisi, p75, Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p52)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا وَصِيَّ الْاَوْصِيَاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا عِمَادَ الْاَتْقِيَاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا وَلِيَّ الْاَوْلِيَاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا سَيِّدَ الشُّهَدَاۤءِ *اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا اٰيَةَ اللّٰهِ الْعُظْمٰ* اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا خَامِسَ اَهْلِ الْعَبَاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا قَاۤئِدَ الْغُرِّ الْمُحَجَّلِيْنَ الْاَتْقِيَاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا عِصْمَةَ الْاَوْلِيَاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا زَيْنَ الْمُوَحِّدِيْنَ النُّجَبَاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا خَالِصَ الْاَخِلَّاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا وَالِدَ الْاَئِمَّةِ الْاُمَنَاۤءِ...

_"Salam ho Aap par aye Wasiyon ke Wasi. Salam ho Aap par Aye Shohada ke Sardar. *Salam ho Aap par Aye Allah ki Azeem tareen Nishani (Azeem Ayatullah).* Salam ho Aap par Aye Ahle Eba ki Panchvi Fard....."_

(Ziyarat Roze Wiladat Rasoole Khuda (saww) & Imam Sadiq (as) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             ♦ _*NA-SHUKRI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1453)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَاۤ أَذَقۡنَا ٱلنَّاسَ رَحۡمَةࣰ مِّنۢ بَعۡدِ ضَرَّاۤءَ مَسَّتۡهُمۡ إِذَا لَهُم مَّكۡرࣱ فِیۤ ءَایَاتِنَاۚ قُلِ ٱللَّهُ أَسۡرَعُ مَكۡرًاۚ إِنَّ رُسُلَنَا یَكۡتُبُونَ مَا تَمۡكُرُونَ.*

_"Aur jab Ham takleef ke baad logon ko Apni Rehmat ka Maza chakhate hain to woh Hamari Ayaat ke mutalliq chal baziyan karne lag jate hain. Aap keh den ke Khuda tumse Teztar Tadbeer Karnewale hai. Hamare Numainde tumhare Makr ko likh rahe hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 21)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Ye Tazkara Nashukri ka hai. Jab Allah takleef ke baad Rahat deta hai to log bajaye Khuda ka Shukr ada karne ke wapas But Parasti ki taraf chale jate hai. Baqaul unke, unke But Naraaz ho gaye to unka ghazab nazil ho gaya aur jab rahat mili to Buton ke zariye mili. Woh Khuda ki Nishaniyon ka mazaq udate aur Makro fareb karte.

Makr usko kehte hain jo khufiya taur par anjaam paya jata. Agar Kafir Khuda ke saath Makr kar sakte hain to Allah to sab se Tez Makr karnewale hai.

Is Ayat mein is baat ki taraf bhi ishaara hai ke Insaan ke har Aamaal do Farishte Munkir o Nakir kandhon par baithe likhte rehte hain. Har cheez Note ho rahi hai aur Qayamat ke Din ye Kitab sab ke saamne pesh kar di jayegi.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Musa (as) ko 4 baato'n ki Wasiyyat ki:_

_1) Jab tak tere Gunah Ma'af na ho, doosro'n ke Aib talaashne mein mashgool na hona,_

_2) Jab tak Mere khazaane khatm na ho, apni Rozi ki fikr mat karna,_

_3) Meri Haakimiyat (rule) ke hote hue kisi ghair ki haakimiyat ko tasleem na karna aur_

_4) *Jab tak Shaitan mar na jaye uske Makr o Fareb se ghaafil na rehna."*_

(Khisaal, p118)

☘️

Imam Taqi (as):

_"Jis Ne'mat ka *shukriya adaa na kiya jaye* wo us Gunah ke misl hai jo baksha na jaye."_

(Aqwaal 14 Masumeen (as), p207)

🤲🏻

*وَ كَيْدَ مَنْ اَخَافُ كَيْدَهُ وَ مَقْدُرَةَ مَنْ اَخَافُ [بَلَاۤءَ] مَقْدُرَتَهُ عَلَيَّ وَ تَرُدَّ عَنِّيْ كَيْدَ الْكَيَدَةِ وَ مَكْرَ الْمَكَرَةِ اَللّٰهُمَّ مَنْ اَرَادَنِيْ فَاَرِدْهُ وَ مَنْ كَادَنِيْ فَكِدْهُ وَ اصْرِفْ عَنِّيْ كَيْدَهُ وَ مَكْرَهُ وَ بَأْسَهُ وَ اَمَانِيَّهُ وَ امْنَعْهُ عَنِّيْ كَيْفَ شِئْتَ وَ اَنَّى شِئْتَ*

(Dua-e-Alqama - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*ALLAH SE BHAGHAWAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1454)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هُوَ ٱلَّذِی یُسَیِّرُكُمۡ فِی ٱلۡبَرِّ وَٱلۡبَحۡرِۖ حَتَّىٰۤ إِذَا كُنتُمۡ فِی ٱلۡفُلۡكِ وَجَرَیۡنَ بِهِم بِرِیحࣲ طَیِّبَةࣲ وَفَرِحُوا۟ بِهَا جَاۤءَتۡهَا رِیحٌ عَاصِفࣱ وَجَاۤءَهُمُ ٱلۡمَوۡجُ مِن كُلِّ مَكَانࣲ وَظَنُّوۤا۟ أَنَّهُمۡ أُحِیطَ بِهِمۡ دَعَوُا۟ ٱللَّهَ مُخۡلِصِینَ لَهُ ٱلدِّینَ لَىِٕنۡ أَنجَیۡتَنَا مِنۡ هَـٰذِهِۦ لَنَكُونَنَّ مِنَ ٱلشَّـٰكِرِینَ *  فَلَمَّاۤ أَنجَىٰهُمۡ إِذَا هُمۡ یَبۡغُونَ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ بِغَیۡرِ ٱلۡحَقِّۗ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ إِنَّمَا بَغۡیُكُمۡ عَلَىٰۤ أَنفُسِكُمۖ مَّتَـٰعَ ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَاۖ ثُمَّ إِلَیۡنَا مَرۡجِعُكُمۡ فَنُنَبِّئُكُم بِمَا كُنتُمۡ تَعۡمَلُونَ.*

_"Wohi to hai jo tumhe Khushki aur Samandar mein saer karata hai. Jab tum Kishtiyon mein sawar ho kar mawafiq Hawa par farhan o shadan safar kar rahe hote ho. Phir yakayak baad e mukhalif (opposite wind) ka zor hota hai aur har taraf se Maujon ke thapede lagte hain aur Musafir samajh lete hain ke woh Toofan mein ghir chuke hain to us waqt sab apne Deen ko Allah hi ke liye khalis karke Usse Duayen maangte hain ke agar Tu ne hamko isse bacha liya to ham Shukrguzar Bande ban kar rahenge._

_"Phir jab Khuda unhe Nijaat de deta hai to woh log Zameen mein Na-Haq Baghawat karne lag jate hain. Insaano! Tumhari ye Baghawat khud tumhare hi khilaf pad rahi hai. Ye Duniya ki Zindagi ke chand roza maze hain. Phir Hamari taraf tumhe palat kar aana hai. Phir Ham tumhe batayenge ke tum Duniya mein reh kar kya karte rahe the."_

(Surah Yunus: 22 - 23)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Jaisa ke guzishta Ayaat mein bhi zikr ho chuka hai ke Banda Musibat ke waqt Mukhlis ho jata hai aur jab Musibat tal jati hai phir waisa hi ho jata hai aur Baghawat karne lagta hai. Is Ayat mein ek misal ke zariye iski wazahat ki hai.

Isi tarah Qur'an mein doosri jagah Kashti sawar ki bhi misaal di hai.

🚩

Jab Talha Zubair ne Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ki Bai'at Shikni ki Aisha ko le kar Basra pahunche to Aap (as) ne apne Shiyon ko Khat likha:

_"Talha Zubair ki isse bade ghalti aur kya ho sakti hai ke unhone apni Biwiyon ko to ghar ki char diwariyon mein rakha, lekin Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki Zauja ko Maidan mein le aaye, un logon ne Khuda aur Rasool (saww) ke saath sakht Na-insaafi ki hai. In dono ne bek waqt Baghawat, chalbazi aur Bai'at Shikni ka irtekab kiya hai jabke Allah ko mazkoora teeno amal napasand hain. Allah ne farmaya: "Logo! Tumhari ye Baghawat khud tumhare hi khilaf hai."_

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Agar Imam Aakhiruz Zaman (atfs) ki Ghaibat ke baad Ulama Imamat ko saabit karne waale aur Shiyo'n ko Shayateen ke Makr o Fareb se bachane wale na hote, to tamaam Shia murtad ho jaate, magar unke haatho'n mein us giroh ki Mehaar is tarah hai jaise Mallah (Naavik) Kashti ke Langar ko sambhaale rehta hai. Is liye unka martaba Khuda ke nazdeek sab se behtar hai."_

(Roohul Hayaat, p243)

🤲🏻

Imam Musa Kazim (as): Agar koi Samandar/Darya mein doobne lage to ye Dua padhe:

*بِسمِ اللّٰه اسكُن بِسَكِينَةِ اللّٰه وَ قَرَّ بِوَقَارِ اللّٰه وَ اهدَا بِاِذنِ اللّٰه وَ لَا حَولَ وَلَا قُوَّةَ إلَّا بِاللّٰه العَلِيُّ الْعَظِيمِ.*

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        *15th June 2020, Monday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ _*🌾DUNIYAVI ZINDAGI🌾*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1455)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا مَثَلُ ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا كَمَاۤءٍ أَنزَلۡنَـٰهُ مِنَ ٱلسَّمَاۤءِ فَٱخۡتَلَطَ بِهِۦ نَبَاتُ ٱلۡأَرۡضِ مِمَّا یَأۡكُلُ ٱلنَّاسُ وَٱلۡأَنۡعَـٰمُ حَتَّىٰۤ إِذَاۤ أَخَذَتِ ٱلۡأَرۡضُ زُخۡرُفَهَا وَٱزَّیَّنَتۡ وَظَنَّ أَهۡلُهَاۤ أَنَّهُمۡ قَـٰدِرُونَ عَلَیۡهَاۤ أَتَىٰهَاۤ أَمۡرُنَا لَیۡلًا أَوۡ نَهَارࣰا فَجَعَلۡنَـٰهَا حَصِیدࣰا كَأَن لَّمۡ تَغۡنَ بِٱلۡأَمۡسِۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ نُفَصِّلُ ٱلۡـَٔایَـٰتِ لِقَوۡمࣲ یَتَفَكَّرُونَ.*

_"Duniya ki misal Barish ki si hai jise Hamne Aasmaan se nazil kiya phir isse mil kar Zameen se wo Nabatat (Veg) baramad huin jinko Insaan aur Jaanwar khaate hain yahan tak ke jab Zameen ne Sabzezar se apne ko araasta kar kiya aur Malik ye samajhne lage ke woh is Zameen ke Sahibe Ikhtiyar hain to achanak Raat ko ya Din ko Hamara Hukm aa gaya aur Hamne use bilkul kata hua khet bana diya goya is mein kal kuchh tha hi nahi. Sahibane Fikr ke liye Ham Apni Nishaniyon ko is tarah khol kar bayan karte hain. Allah Salamti ke Ghar ki Dawat deta hai aur jise chahta hai Seedhe Raaste ki Hidayat de deta hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 24)

📚📖 🌍 🌾

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Guzishta Ayat mein Kishti ke bhanvar mein phansne ki misal di thi, doosri misal is Ayat mein us Khet ki hai, ke jab Insaan ye samajhne lagta hai ke meine ugaya to doosre din wo usi Khet ko ujda hua pata hai, chahe Tiddiyon (Locust) ke zariye ya koi aur.

🌍

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as): (Khutba)

_"Logon! Poori koshish karke Duniya ke is chhote Din se Akherat ke Taveel Din ke liye Zade Raah talash karo. Duniya Amal ka Ghar hai aur Akherat Qarar aur Jaza ka Din hai. Lehaza Duniya mein apna daman samet kar raho. Woh shakhs dhoke mein mubtila hai jo Duniya par farefta ho jaye aur yaad rakho jab bhi Duniya Talab afraad ye mehsoos karte hain ke woh apni murad ko pahunchne ko hi hain to ye Duniya unke liye hare bhare Khet ki tarah se tabah o weraan ho jaati hai."_

(Noorus Saqlain)

👑

Imam Mohd Baqir (as): (Hukumat ke sawal par jawab)

_"Aale Jafar ki qismat mein iqtedar aur Hukumat naam ki koi cheez nahi hai albatta Aale Abbas ki qismat mein Hukumat o Saltanat hai jis mein woh door ke afraad ko qareeb karenge aur qareebon ko door karenge. Unki Hukumat bahut sakht hogi jis mein asaani o narmi nahi hogi. Aur jab woh Khuda ki pakad aur Uske Azaab se bekhauf ho jayenge to phir ek cheekh si buland hogi jo unki jami'at ko puraganda kar degi aur iqtedar unse chheen liya jayega aur woh Quran ki Ayat *حَتَّىٰۤ إِذَاۤ أَخَذَتِ ٱلۡأَرۡضُ* ka amali namuna ban jayenge."_

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

_"Logon! Khuda ne tumhe is Duniya se Zuhd ikhtiyar karne ka Hukm diya hai. Tum bhi isse Zuhd ikhtiyar karo aur apne aap ko Sahibane Fikr mein se banao."_

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*اَشْهَدُ يَا مَوْلَايَ اَنَّكَ وَ الْاَئِمَّةَ مِنْ اٰبَاۤئِكَ اَئِمَّتِيْ وَ مَوَالِيَّ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَ يَوْمَ يَقُوْمُ الْاَشْهَادُ اَسْاَلُكَ يَا مَوْلَايَ اَنْ تَسْاَلَ اللّٰهَ تَبَارَكَ وَ تَعَالٰى فِيْ صَلَاحِ شَأْنِيْ وَ قَضَاۤءِ حَوَاۤئِجِيْ وَ غُفْرَانِ ذُنُوْبِيْ وَ الْاَخْذِ بِيَدِيْ فِيْ دِيْنِيْ وَ دُنْيَايَ وَ اٰخِرَتِيْ لِيْ وَ لِاِخْوَانِيْ وَ اَخَوَاتِيَ الْمُؤْمِنِيْنَ وَ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ كَآفَّةً اِنَّهُ غَفُوْرٌ رَحِيْمٌ۔*

(Ziyarat Sahebul Amr اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَى الْحَقِّ الْجَدِيْدِ - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    *16th June 2020, Tuesday*

♦ _*DARUS SALAM KI DAWAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1456)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَٱللَّهُ یَدۡعُوۤا۟ إِلَىٰ دَارِ ٱلسَّلَـٰمِ وَیَهۡدِی مَن یَشَاۤءُ إِلَىٰ صِرَ ٰ⁠طࣲ مُّسۡتَقِیمࣲ.*

_"Allah Salamti ke Ghar (Darus Salam) ki Dawat deta hai aur jise chahta hai Seedhe Raaste ki Hidayat de deta hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 25)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

_"Salam' " *سلام*" Allah ka Naam hai aur "Ghar" se murad Uski Jannat hai, jo Usne Apne Auliya ke liye banayi hai aur Usne logon ko is Jannat ki Dawat dete hue farmaya (10:25) 'Allah Darus Salam ki taraf Dawat deta hai"_

(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Salam' Allah ke Naamo mein se ek hai. Sabse pehle Allah ne Apni Zaat ki taraf Insaano ko Dawat di hai aur unhe Apni Ita'at aur Farmabardari ki taraf bulaya hai aur Usne Apne Nafs se ibteda ki hai aur farmaya (10:25)"_

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Logo'n ko khair ki taraf baghair Zabaan se (yaani Kirdaar o Amal) se Daawat do, taaki wo tumhaari koshish aur sachchai aur Parhezgari ko (apni aa'nkho'n se) dekh sakein."_

(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p151)

🤲🏻

*اَللّٰهُمَّ اَنْتَ السَّلَامُ وَ مِنْكَ السَّلَامُ وَ اِلَيْكَ يَعُوْدُ السَّلَامُ وَ دَارُكَ دَارُ السَّلَامِ حَيِّنَا رَبَّنَا مِنْكَ بِالسَّلَامِ اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنِّيْ صَلَّيْتُ هٰذِهِ الصَّلَاةَ ابْتِغَاۤءَ رَحْمَتِكَ وَ رِضْوَانِكَ وَ مَغْفِرَتِكَ وَ تَعْظِيْمًا لِمَسْجِدِكَ اَللّٰهُمَّ فَصَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ ارْفَعْهَا فِيْ عِلِّيِّيْنَ وَ تَقَبَّلْهَا مِنِّيْ يَاۤ اَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِيْنَ۔*

(Aamaal Masjid e Kufa: Dua after Namaze Wasat e Masjid - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

♦ _*SIYAH AUR SAFED CHEHRE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1457)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لِّلَّذِینَ أَحۡسَنُوا۟ ٱلۡحُسۡنَىٰ وَزِیَادَةࣱۖ وَلَا یَرۡهَقُ وُجُوهَهُمۡ قَتَرࣱ وَلَا ذِلَّةٌۚ أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ أَصۡحَـٰبُ ٱلۡجَنَّةِۖ هُمۡ فِیهَا خَـٰلِدُونَ *  وَٱلَّذِینَ كَسَبُوا۟ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتِ جَزَاۤءُ سَیِّئَةِۭ بِمِثۡلِهَا وَتَرۡهَقُهُمۡ ذِلَّةࣱۖ مَّا لَهُم مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ مِنۡ عَاصِمࣲۖ كَأَنَّمَاۤ أُغۡشِیَتۡ وُجُوهُهُمۡ قِطَعࣰا مِّنَ ٱلَّیۡلِ مُظۡلِمًاۚ أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ أَصۡحَـٰبُ ٱلنَّارِۖ هُمۡ فِیهَا خَـٰلِدُونَ.*

_"Jin logon ne Bhalai ki Ravish apnai unke liye Bhalai hai aur mazeed izafa bhi hai. Unke Chehre par Siyahi aur Zillat taari na hogi. Wohi Jannat mein jaane wale hain woh us mein hamesha rahenge."_

_"Aur woh log jinhone Buraiyyan ki hain woh apni Buraiyyon ki miqdar mein hi Badla payenge aur un par Zillat taari hogi. Unhe Allah se koi bachanewala maujood na hoga. Unke Chehron par Raat ke Siyah Pardon jaisi Siyahi chhayi hogi. Woh Dozakh mein Jaanewale hain. Woh us mein hamesha rahenge."_

(Surah Yunus: 26 - 27)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Qayamat ke Din logon ke Chehre do tarah ke nazar aayenge Siyah (Dark) aur Safed (White).

👉🏻 🤵🏻🤵🏿

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne Ahle Bida'at  o Shahwaat (Innovators & Lustfuls) ka haal bayan kiya hai. Qayamat ke Din Khuda unke Chehron ko Siyah kar dega aur unhe Zillat o Ruswai ka Libaas pahnaiga."_

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤵🏿🤵🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Jis tarah se Siyah Raaton mein door se Makaan Siyah (Dark) dikhai deta hai usi tarah se Ahle Bida'at o Shahwaat ke Chehre bhi Akherat mein Siyah honge aur unki Ru Siyahi mein roz baroz izaafa hoga."_

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 🤵🏻

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Momin ki Nishaani ye hai ke jab uski Maut ka waqt aata hai to uske Chehre ka rang jitna safed tha us se zyada safed aur raushan ho jaata hai, pehsaani par paseena aane lagta hai, uski Aa'nkho’n se Aa'nsuo’n ki tarah Rutubat behne lagti hai; to yehi uski Rooh nikalne ki nishaani hai…"_

(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p100)

🤵🏿

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Zina ke 6 bure natije hote hain, 3 Duniya mein aur 3 Akherat mein: Duniya mein ye ke Chehre ki khubsoorati khatm ho jaati hai, Faqr (Ghareebi) aur tangdasti gher leti hain aur Umr kam ho jaati hai, Akherat mein ye ke Khuda ke Ghazab ka nishana banta hai, Hisaab mein sakhti hoti hai aur hamesha ke Azaab ka mustahaq hota hai."_

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p379)

🤲🏻

*...وَ اَنْتَ غَدًا عَلَی الْحَوْضِ خَلِیْفَتِیْ وَ اَنْتَ تَقْضِیْ دَیْنِیْ وَ تُنْجِزُ عِدَاتِیْ وَ شِیْعَتُكَ عَلٰی مَنَابِرَ مِنْ نُوْرٍ مُبْیَضَّۃً وُجُوْھُھُمْ حَوْلِیْ فِی الْجَنَّۃِ وَ ھُمْ جِیْرَانِیْ وَ لَوْلَاۤ اَنْتَ یَا عَلِیُّ لَمْ یُعْرَفِ الْمُؤْمِنُوْنَ بَعْدِیْ وَ كَانَ بَعْدَهٗ ھُدًی مِنَ الضَّلَالِ وَ نُوْرًا مِّنَ الْعَمٰی وَ حَبْلَ ﷲِ الْمَتِیْنَ وَ صِرَاطَهُ الْمُسْتَقِیْمَ...*

_"Aur (Ay Ali) tum kal Hauze Kausar par mere Janashin honge aur tum mere Qarz ko ada karoge. Aur mere Waadon ko poora karoge. Aur tumhare Shia Noor ke Minbar par honge. Unke Chehre chamkte honge. Woh mere Giroh Jannat mein mere hamsaya (Neighbour) honge. Aur Aye Ali agar tum na hote to mere baad Mo'meneen ki shanakht kabhi na ho sakti aur woh Paighambar ke baad Gumrahi mein Hidayat aur Tareeki mein Noorullah ki Mazboot Hidayat ki Rassi aur Seedha Raasta the."_

(Dua-e-Nudba - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

**********************************

           *25th Shawwal 1441*

   *18th June 2020, Wednesday*

(Shahadat Imam Sadiq (as) by other Riwayat)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ _*BUT PARASTI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1458)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَیَوۡمَ نَحۡشُرُهُمۡ جَمِیعࣰا ثُمَّ نَقُولُ لِلَّذِینَ أَشۡرَكُوا۟ مَكَانَكُمۡ أَنتُمۡ وَشُرَكَاۤؤُكُمۡۚ فَزَیَّلۡنَا بَیۡنَهُمۡۖ وَقَالَ شُرَكَاۤؤُهُم مَّا كُنتُمۡ إِیَّانَا تَعۡبُدُونَ *  فَكَفَىٰ بِٱللَّهِ شَهِیدَۢا بَیۡنَنَا وَبَیۡنَكُمۡ إِن كُنَّا عَنۡ عِبَادَتِكُمۡ لَغَـٰفِلِینَ *  هُنَالِكَ تَبۡلُوا۟ كُلُّ نَفۡسࣲ مَّاۤ أَسۡلَفَتۡۚ وَرُدُّوۤا۟ إِلَى ٱللَّهِ مَوۡلَىٰهُمُ ٱلۡحَقِّۖ وَضَلَّ عَنۡهُم مَّا كَانُوا۟ یَفۡتَرُونَ.*

_"Jis Din Ham sab ko mehshoor (gather) karenge phir Ham Mushrekin se kahenge ke tum bhi apni jagah par thaher jao aur tumhare Sharik bhi thaher jayen. Ham unke darmiyan se pardeh hata denge aur unke Sharik kahenge ke tum hamari Ibaadat nahi kiya karte the. Hamare aur tumhare darmiyan Allah Ta'ala ki Gawahi Kafi hai. Ham to tumhari us Ibaadat se bilkul bekhabar the. Us waqt har Shakhs apne kiye ka zayqa chakh sakega. Sabko unke Haqeeqi Parwardigar ki taraf lautaya jayega aur saare jhoot jinhe woh ghada karte the gum ho jayenge."_

(Surah Yunus: 28 - 30)

📚📖 💩

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Is Ayat mein Qayamat ke Din wo manzarkashi ki hai jahan Butparast aur unke sharik jin ki woh pooja karte the jama honge aur haqeeqat unke saamne zahir hogi. But sirf Patthar ke hi nahi hote balke har cheez jinki Insaan jhooti pooja karne lagta hai. Dua Sanam e Quraish mein bhi Do Buton par La'anat bheji gaye hai. Mansab, Jaa o hasham, ghamand, Daulat, Aurat, Malaika etc. sab ki Insaan pooja karta hai. Us Din inke Dev aur khud yakja jama honge aur unka Dev kahega meine to apni pooja karne ko nahi kaha tha. Allah ko apna Gawah banayenge.

👹

Riwayat:

"Jab Shaitan ne Sone aur Chaandi se banaye gaye Sikke (Gold aur Silver Coins) is Duniya mein pehli bar dekhe to unhe utha kar seene se lagaya aur kaha, "Tum dono mere Noor e Nazar ho, mere Dil ka Mewa ho" aur phir un Sikko'n se kaha ke, "Main iske alawa koi aur gharz nahi rakhta ke Bani Adam (Adam (as) ki Aulaad) ek But bana kar uski parastish karen aur use dost rakhen aur doosra ye ke woh tumhe dost aur azeez rakhen."

(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p197)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Taqi (as):

_"Jo bolne waale ki baat kaan dharke sune usne (goya) uski parastish / Ibaadat ki. Pus, agar bolne wala Khuda ki baat keh raha hai to usne Khuda ki ibaadat ki aur agar bolne waala Shaitan ki zabaan bol raha hai to usne Shaitan ki parastish ki."_

(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205)

🚩

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Agar koi But-parast (idol-worshipper) bhi marte waqt Mazhabe Shia ka eteqaad aur Aimma e Masoomeen (as) ki Imamat ka waqai iqraar kar lega to Aatish e Jahannum uske kisi jism ke hisse ko na chhuegi."_

(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p318)

🤲🏻

*وَ حَشَرَكَ مَعَ النَّبِيِّيْنَ وَ الصِّدِّيْقِيْنَ وَ الشُّهَدَاۤءِ وَ الصَّالِحِيْنَ وَ حَسُنَ اُوْلٰۤئِكَ رَفِيْقًا....*

(Ziyarat Muslim bin Aqeel - Mafateeh)

*فَبِحُرْمَةِ هٰذَا الْمَكَانِ الْمُنِيْفِ، صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ آلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، وَاحْشُرْنِيْ فِيْ زُمْرَتِهِمْ، وَ اَدْخِلْنِي الْجَنَّةَ بِشَفَاعَتِهِمْ،....*

(Ziyarat e Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*HAMARA HAQEEQI RAB: ALLAH!*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1459)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلۡ مَن یَرۡزُقُكُم مِّنَ ٱلسَّمَاۤءِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ أَمَّن یَمۡلِكُ ٱلسَّمۡعَ وَٱلۡأَبۡصَـٰرَ وَمَن یُخۡرِجُ ٱلۡحَیَّ مِنَ ٱلۡمَیِّتِ وَیُخۡرِجُ ٱلۡمَیِّتَ مِنَ ٱلۡحَیِّ وَمَن یُدَبِّرُ ٱلۡأَمۡرَۚ فَسَیَقُولُونَ ٱللَّهُۚ فَقُلۡ أَفَلَا تَتَّقُونَ *  فَذَ ٰ⁠لِكُمُ ٱللَّهُ رَبُّكُمُ ٱلۡحَقُّۖ فَمَاذَا بَعۡدَ ٱلۡحَقِّ إِلَّا ٱلضَّلَـٰلُۖ فَأَنَّىٰ تُصۡرَفُونَ.*

_"Inse poochho! Tumhe Aasmaano Zameen se Rizq kaun faraham karta hai? Aur Sama'at (Hearing) o Basaarat (Sight) ki quwwaten kis ke ikhtiyar mein hain aur be-Jaan se Jaandar aur Jaandar se be-Jaan ko kaun nikalta hai? Aur is Nazme Jahan (Universal System) ki tadbeer kaun kar raha hai? Woh zaroor kahenge ke 'Allah'! Pas Aap keh dijiye phir tum Usse darte kyon nahi ho? Woh Allah tumhara Haqeeqi Rab hai aur Haq ke baad gumrahi ke siwa aur kya hai? Akhir tum kidhar phiraye jaa rahe ho?_

_Is tarah se Fisq ikhtiyar karnewalo par tumhare Rab ki baat Sadiq aa gayi ke woh Imaan nahi layenge."_

(Surah Yunus: 31 - 32)

📚📖 🕌

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Is Ayat mein Allah ne Insaan ki Fitrat ko jhanjhod kar kai Sawal kiye jiske Jawab mein usse besakhta yehi Mu'nh se niklenge: 'Allah'. Poore zikr ka mafhoom yehi hai ke hamara Rab, Palnewala, Dekh bhal karnewala, Parwarish Karnewala Allah hi hai. Jab ham ye baat samajh lenge to kyon kisi aur saamne haath phailayenge. Kyon kisi ghair ki pooja karenge. Kyon kisiko Allah ka Sharik banayenge. Lekin jo hatdharmi par hain woh manne wale nahi, woh idhar udhar bhatakte phirenge.

Allah ne Apni tarah bulane liye Apne Numainde muqarrar kiye. Nabi Rasool aur Aimma ka intekhab kiya. Ab jo inse door bhage yani Allah se farar ikhtiyar ki.

🕌

Allah Ta'ala:

_"Aye Adam ke bete! Agar Allah ne tujhe Rizq dene ki zimmedaari le li hai tab kyun teri tamaam koshishen Usi ki taraf hai."_

(Al-Hadith Al-Qudsi - ABISN, Nairobi, Kenya)

🍽️

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Allah ne Bani Adam (Aadmi) ko jumla makhluqaat par fazilat di hai aur unhe khushki aur tari mein uthaya aur har qism ke pakeeza phalo'n se use Rizq diya. Har haiwaan aur parinda ye taaqat nahi rakhta ke apna khana aur paani apne haatho'n se utha kar apne mu'nh mein daale. Ye fazilat sirf Bani Adam (Aadmi) hi ko hai ke wo apna khana apne haatho'n se apne Mu'nh mein daalta hai aur ye bahut badi fazilat hai."_

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p92)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 🕌

Imam Ali (as):

_"Jab Khaaliq se daro to Usi ki taraf faraar karo aur jab makhlooq se daro to usse faraar karo."_

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p340)

🍪🥣

Imam Ali (as):

_"Rizq ki 2 qismein hain: Ek talaash karnewala aur doosra jise talaash kiya jaye. Lihaza, jo shakhs Duniya ka taalib hai, Maut uski taalib hoti hai yahan tak ke woh is Duniya se baahar nikal jaye. Aur jo shakhs Akherat ka khwahishmand hota hai, use Duniya roke rakhegi, yahan tak ke woh apna pura Rizq haasil kar le."_

(Adaab e Islami, v2, p142)

🤲🏻

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Tu Khaaliq hai aur main makhlooq hun. Tu Maalik hai aur main mamlook hun. Tu Parwardigar hai aur main Tera banda hun. Tu Raaziq hai aur main Rizq paanewala hoo'n. Tu ataa karne waala hai aur main maangnewala hun. Tu Sakhawat karnewala aur main kanjoos hun. Tu Quwwatwala aur main kamzor hun…"_

(Dua e Yastasheer)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
