♦ _*HAMARA HAQEEQI HADI: ALLAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1460)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلۡ هَلۡ مِن شُرَكَاۤىِٕكُم مَّن یَبۡدَؤُا۟ ٱلۡخَلۡقَ ثُمَّ یُعِیدُهُۥۚ قُلِ ٱللَّهُ یَبۡدَؤُا۟ ٱلۡخَلۡقَ ثُمَّ یُعِیدُهُۥۖ فَأَنَّىٰ تُؤۡفَكُونَ *  قُلۡ هَلۡ مِن شُرَكَاۤىِٕكُم مَّن یَهۡدِیۤ إِلَى ٱلۡحَقِّۚ قُلِ ٱللَّهُ یَهۡدِی لِلۡحَقِّۗ أَفَمَن یَهۡدِیۤ إِلَى ٱلۡحَقِّ أَحَقُّ أَن یُتَّبَعَ أَمَّن لَّا یَهِدِّیۤ إِلَّاۤ أَن یُهۡدَىٰۖ فَمَا لَكُمۡ كَیۡفَ تَحۡكُمُونَ.*

_"Aap kahen ke kya tumhare Shuraka mein se koi aisa bhi hai jo Khilqat ki ibteda (start) kare aur phir dobara use palat sake? Kahen ke Woh sirf Allah hai jo Takhleeq (Creation) ki ibteda bhi karta hai aur Wohi inhe paltata bhi hai. Akhir tum kis ulti raah par chalaye jaa rahe ho? Aap kahe kya tumhare Shuraka mein se koi aisa bhi hai jo Haq ki Hidayat kar sake? Aap keh den ke Allah hi Haq ki Hidayat karta hai. Phir bhala batao ke jo Haq ki taraf Rahnumayi karta hai Woh iska zyada mustahaq hai ke Uski Pairavi ki jaye ya jo khud raah nahi pata siwai iske uski Rahnumayi ki jaye? Akhir tumhe kya ho gaya hai, tum kaise faisle karte ho?"_

(Surah Yunus: 34 - 35)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Hidayat e Mutlaq Allah ki hoti hai lekin Allah ne is Aalam mein Apni Numainde logon ki Hidayat ke liye bheje.

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Is Ayat ke misdaq Hazrat Ali (as) hain."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

_"Muhammad wa Aale Muhammad (as) Haq ki Hidayat karnewale hain jabke hamare Mukhalefin woh hain jinhe Raahe Haq ka Ilm hi nahi hai, jab tak unki Rahnumayi na ki jaye."_

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Imam Ali Reza (as):

_"Allah Ta'ala Anbiya aur Aimma (as) ko khusoosi Taufeeq se nawazta hai aur unhe Apne Poshida Ilm o Hikmat se Woh kuchh ata karta hai jo doosron ko ata nahi karta. Isiliye Woh Apne zamane ke tamam afraad se zyada Aalim hote hain. Allah Ta'ala farmata hai (10:35)."_

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ek shakhs Abu Bakr ke paas aaya jo Sharab mein dhut tha. Khalifa ne kaha Tu ne Sharab pee hai, maloom nahi Sharab Haram hai. Usne kaha mein chand roz pahle hi Musalman hua hun aur jahan mein rehta hun wahan sab log Sharab peete hain. Mujhe nahi maloom tha Islam mein Sharab Haram hai. Umar se poochha gaya ke kya faisla karen. Usne kaha Ali (as) ko bulao wohi faisla kar sakte hain. Imam Ali (as) ne kaha isko kisi shakhs ke saath Muhajir o Ansaar ki mehfil mein bhejo aur unse poochho kya kisi ne isko Sharab ki Hurmat ki Ayat padhte suna hai. Kisi ne is baat ki gawahi nahi di. Ali (as) ne farmaya: "Isko bari kar do."

Janab Salman Farsi ne kaha aapne khub faisla kiya. To Aap (as) ne is Ayat (10:35) ki taraf mutawajjah kiya."

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

_"Logo! Jab mein tumse kuchh kahun to meri baat suno, Khuda tumhe Hidayat dega aur jab mein tumhe koi hukm dun to tum meri ita'at karo, gumrahi se mehfooz rahoge. Aur agar tumne meri Nafarmani ki to gumrahi mein mubtila ho jaoge. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya (10:35)."_

(Kashful Mahajjah Syed Ibne Taus, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*وَ صَلِّ عَلَى الْخَلَفِ الْهَادِي الْمَهْدِيِّ اِمَامِ الْمُؤْمِنِيْنَ وَ وَارِثِ الْمُرْسَلِيْنَ وَ حُجَّةِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِيْنَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اَهْلِ بَيْتِهِ الْاَئِمَّةِ الْهَادِيْنَ الْعُلَمَاۤءِ الصَّادِقِيْنَ الْاَبْرَارِ الْمُتَّقِيْنَ دَعَاۤئِمِ دِيْنِكَ وَ اَرْكَانِ تَوْحِيْدِكَ وَ تَرَاجِمَةِ وَحْيِكَ وَ حُجَجِكَ عَلٰى خَلْقِكَ.....*

(Salwat Abul Hasan Zarab Al Isfahani - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ _*IDOL: FALSE IMAGES*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1461)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا یَتَّبِعُ أَكۡثَرُهُمۡ إِلَّا ظَنًّاۚ إِنَّ ٱلظَّنَّ لَا یُغۡنِی مِنَ ٱلۡحَقِّ شَیۡـًٔاۚ إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ عَلِیمُۢ بِمَا یَفۡعَلُونَ.*

_"Unki Aksariyat mehez Guman ki Pairavi kar rahi hai jabke Guman Haq ke bare mein koi bhi fayda nahi pahuncha sakta. Jo kuchh ye kar rahe hain Allah usko khoob jaanta hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 36)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Guzishta Ayat mein zikr hua ke Hidayat mutalaqan Allah ke zimme hai. Lekin ye Uski Shaan hai ke Usne Apne Karzaar ke liye zaraye moayyan kiye hain. Jaise Farishte. Hidayat ke liye Usne Anbiya (as) wa Aimma (as) ka intekhab kiya. Yehi Haq ka raasta hai, jisko hamne guzishta tafseer mein bayan kiya.

Aaj ki Ayat mein But Parasti ka sabab bayan kiya gaya hai.

Logon ki Aksariyat Jahil hoti hai. Jahilon ko Ilm hasil karne mein koi interest nahi hota. Lekin ye Insaani Fitrat hai ke jab usko koi kuchh deta hai ye uska Shukriya ada karta hai, uska ka Ehsaan maanta hai. Shukriye ki hadd aage badhti hai to woh uski Ibaadat karne lagta hai. Uska Ghulam ban jata warna woh musibat mein pada rahta. La Ilmi ki bena par jis jis se use fayda pahuchta rehta hai, uska Ghulam (Banda) banta jata hai. Ilm na hone ki wajah se woh nahi samajh pata kya sahi, kya ghalat. Isliye apne taur par woh Guman, Khayalon ka sahara leta hai. Uske Dimagh mein jo images, Suraten nazar aati hain, unhi ki Pooja karne lagta hai. Uski aql un images mein mehdood ho jati hai aur usi ko physical shape de kar But tayyar karta hai. But do tarah ke hote hain Zehni wa Khayali But, aur Jismani But. Fitrat ke taqazon ko woh apne Guman se poora karta hai. Guman kabhi bhi Haq nahi ho sakta. Ye Assumption hai. Ham kisi cheez ko assume karen, ya ye sahi niklegi ya ghalat.

Pas Khuda ne is pehlu ko is Ayat mein bayan kiya. Guman ki pairavi na karo. Haq ki pairavi karo. Ye Khayali But ki koi Haqeeqat nahi hai, Allah is sab cheezon se Paak hai. Allah ki Haqeeqat o Ma'arefat hasil karne ke liye hame unhi ke paas jana hoga jinko Allah ne apna Numainda bana kar bheja hai. Aap koi Company ka product kharidte hain to uske bare mein usi ke agent se contact karenge na ke kis aur company ke. Allah ka product hai Tauheed. Ye sirf Allah ke hi Numainde se milega, na ke logon ke banaye hue khud sakhta numaindon se. Quran ne bahut si misalen pesh ki hain jahan ek hi shakhs ne poori Qaum ko gumrah kiya aur apne Guman par amal kiya jaise Samari ne Gau Pooja shuru ki. Ka'abe mein Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Statues the jin ki log pooja karte the waghaira. Aur aaj bhi Duniya mein But Parasti jaari hai. Ye sirf Guman hai, Haq nahi.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Roz e Qayamat ek bande ko Dozakh mein jaane ka Hukm diya jayega. Pus, woh Khuda ki taraf mutawajjeh hoga. Khuda farmayega, "Use lauta lao". Phir poochhega, "Aye Mere bande, tu kyun mutawajjeh hua?" Wo kahega, "Aye mere Parwardigar, kya mera Guman Teri taraf aisa na tha?" Khuda poochhega, "Kaisa?" Wo kahega, "Mera Guman Teri nisbat ye tha ke Tu meri khata ko bakhsh dega aur mujhe Jannat mein jagah dega." Khuda kahega, "Aye Mere Malaaika, Qasam hai Apne Izzat o Jalaal ki isne Mere mutalliq kabhi Neki ka Guman nahi kiya? Agarche ab khauf e Naar (Jahannum ki aag ke darr) se usne ye Guman kiya, magar use Ajr do aur Jannat mein daakhil kar do."_

(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p171)

🤲🏻

*ھَیْھَاتَ مَا ذٰلِكَ الظَّنُّ بِكَ وَ لَا الْمَعْرُوْفُ مِنْ فَضْلِكَ وَ لَا مُشْبِہٌ لِمَا عَامَلْتَ بِہِ الْمُوَحِّدِیْنَ مِنْ بِرِّكَ وَ اِحْسَانِكَ..*

_"Jabke woh Tere Fazlo Karam ka umeedwar hoga. Hargiz Tere bare mein Khayal aur Tere Ehsaan ka ye andaza nahi hai. Tu ne jis tarah Ahle Tauheed ke saath Nek Bartao kiya iski koi misaal nahi hai."_

(Dua-e-Kumail)

  ♦ _*CHALLENGE OF QUR'AN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: 📖

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا كَانَ هَـٰذَا ٱلۡقُرۡءَانُ أَن یُفۡتَرَىٰ مِن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ وَلَـٰكِن تَصۡدِیقَ ٱلَّذِی بَیۡنَ یَدَیۡهِ وَتَفۡصِیلَ ٱلۡكِتَـٰبِ لَا رَیۡبَ فِیهِ مِن رَّبِّ ٱلۡعَـٰلَمِینَ *  أَمۡ یَقُولُونَ ٱفۡتَرَىٰهُۖ قُلۡ فَأۡتُوا۟ بِسُورَةࣲ مِّثۡلِهِۦ وَٱدۡعُوا۟ مَنِ ٱسۡتَطَعۡتُم مِّن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ إِن كُنتُمۡ صَـٰدِقِینَ.*

_"Qur'an aisi cheez nahi hai jise Allah ki Wahy o Taleem ke baghair tasneef (write) kar liye jaye balke apni guzishta Kitabon ki tasdeeq aur Tafseel hai jis mein kisi ko Shak ki gunjayish nahi hai. Ye Rabbul Aalamin ki taraf se nazil kardah hai._

_Kya ye log kehte hain ke Paighambar ne ise khud hi tasneef kar liya hai? Aap keh den ke agar tum sachche ho to is jaisi ek Surah apni taraf se tasneef kar lao aur Allah ko chhod kar jis jis ko bula sakte ho madad ke liye bula lo."_

(Surat Yunus: 37 - 38)

*قُلْ لَئِنِ اجْتَمَعَتِ الْإِنْسُ وَالْجِنُّ عَلَىٰ أَنْ يَأْتُوا بِمِثْلِ هَٰذَا الْقُرْآنِ لَا يَأْتُونَ بِمِثْلِهِ وَلَوْ كَانَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ ظَهِيرًا*

*وَلَقَدْ صَرَّفْنَا لِلنَّاسِ فِي هَٰذَا الْقُرْآنِ مِنْ كُلِّ مَثَلٍ فَأَبَىٰ أَكْثَرُ النَّاسِ إِلَّا كُفُورًا.*

_"Keh do: agar Insaan aur Jin mil kar is Qur'an ki misl (similar) laana chahen to is ki misaal nahi laa sakenge agarche is kaam mein ek doosre ki madad bhi karen."_

_"Is Qur'an mein Hamne logon ke saamne tarah tarah ki misaalen aur namoone (examples) pesh kiye hain lekin log inkaare Haq ke siwa kuchh nahi karte."_

(Surat Al-Isra: 88 - 89)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

(Repeat Message)

Allah ne Challenge kiya hai ke is Qur'an ki ek ayat ki bhi misl koi nahi laa sakta chaahe sab Jinn o Ins ekathha hokar ek doosre ki madad karen. Ye permanent challenge har zamaane ke liye hai. Ye ek hamare Nabi e Karim (sa) ka permanent mo'jeza hai. Aur aaj tak iski misl koi laa nahi saka na laa sakega.

Detail ki yahan gunjaaish nahi hai,

Readers can read in detail in following links:

_*The Challenge of the Qur'an:*_

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/challenge-quran

_*The Scientific Miracle of the Qur'an:*_

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/scientific-miracle-quran

_*Some Brief Examples​ of Scientific Data in the Qur'an*_

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/some-brief-examples-scientific-data-quran

_*Accuracy of Historical Records in the Qur'an:*_

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/accuracy-historical-records-quran

_*Predictions in Qur'an:*_

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/predictions-quran

_*Lack of Contradictions in the Qur'an:*_

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/lack-contradictions-quran

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 📖

Imam Reza (as):

_"Jo koi Mahe Ramazan mein Allah ki Kitaab (Quran) mein se EK ayat padhega, wo uske misl hai jisne aur Mahino'n mein pura Quran padha."_

(40 Hadith - Quran)

🤲🏻

*اَللّٰهُمَّ بِحَقِّ هَذَا الْقُرْاٰنِ، وَبِحَقِّ مَنْ اَرْسَلْتَهُ بِهِ، وَبِحَقِّ كُلِّ مُؤْمِنٍ مَدَحْتَهُ فِيْهِ، وَبِحَقِّكَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَلَا اَحَدَ اَعْرَفُ بِحَقِّكَ مِنْكَ.*

(Shabe Qadr Aamaal e Qur'an - Mafateeh)

Bare Ilaha bawaste is ke Qur'an hamare saare Gunah Ma'af farma.

♦ _*LA ILMI, JIHAALAT KUFR HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1463)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*بَلۡ كَذَّبُوا۟ بِمَا لَمۡ یُحِیطُوا۟ بِعِلۡمِهِۦ وَلَمَّا یَأۡتِهِمۡ تَأۡوِیلُهُۥۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ كَذَّبَ ٱلَّذِینَ مِن قَبۡلِهِمۡۖ فَٱنظُرۡ كَیۡفَ كَانَ عَـٰقِبَةُ ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ.*

_"Dar asl un logon ne us cheez takzeeb ki (denied) hai jiska unhe mukammal Ilm nahi hai aur iski Taweel abhi tal unke saamne nahi aayi hai. Is tarah unke pehle walon ne bhi takzeeb ki thi. Ab dekho Zulm karne walon ka Anjaam kya hua."_

(Surah Yunus: 39)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Kuchh Allah ki Nishaniyan hain jo baad mein zahoor pazeer hongi lekin hame iska Ilm na hone ki wajah se iska inkaar nahi kar sakte.

Imam Mahdi (atfs) ka zahoor hatmi hai aur woh Zinda hain, lekin hamari la ilmi ki wajah se ham unka inkaar nahi kar sakte. Ye Jahel hai. Aur Jahel Kufr hai.

✒️

Imam Sadiq (as) se mustaqbil mein aane wale waqeat ke mutalliq sawal kiya gaya to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

_"Abhi unke Zahoor Pazeer hone ka waqt nahi aaya aur woh waqeat is Ayat ke zimn mein shamil hain."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

📝

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Allah Ta'ala ne Apne Bandon ko do khusoosi Ahkam diye hain. Pehla Hukm ye hai ke jab tak unhe kisi baat ka Ilm na ho us waqt tak iske mutalliq kuchh na kahen jaisa ke Farman e Qudrat hai. (7:169)._

_Doosra Hukm ye hai ke Ilm baghair kisi baat ko radd na karen jaisa ke Farman e Ilahi hai (10:39)"_

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Jisne Zamana e Ghaibat mein mere Farzand Qaim (atfs) ka inkaar kiya aur woh mar gaya to uski Maut Jahiliyyat ki Maut hai."_

(Falsafa e Gaibat e Mahdi (atfs) , p206)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Aalim wohi hai jo apne Ilm par Amal kare, chaahe uska Ilm kam hi kyun na ho."_

(Adaab e Islami, v2, p62)

✒️

Imam Ali (as):

_"Aalim ki Jihaalat (ignorance) ke liye itni baat kaafi hai ke uske Aamaal uske Ilm ke virudh / bar khilaaf (opposite) hon."_

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)

🤲🏻

*لَعَنَ اللّٰهُ مَنْ قَتَلَكَ وَ لَعَنَ اللّٰهُ مَنْ اَمَرَ بِقَتْلِكَ وَ لَعَنَ اللّٰهُ مَنْ ظَلَمَكَ، وَ لَعَنَ اللّٰهُ مَنِ افْتَرٰى عَلَيْكَ وَ لَعَنَ اللّٰهُ مَنْ جَهِلَ حَقَّكَ وَ اسْتَخَفَّ بِحُرْمَتِكَ وَ لَعَنَ اللّٰهُ مَنْ بَايَعَكَ وَ غَشَّكَ وَ خَذَلَكَ وَ اَسْلَمَكَ....*

(Ziyarat Hazrat Muslim bin Aqeel - Mafateeh)

♦ _*MUNKIR KO USKE HAAL PAR CHHOD DO*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1464)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمِنۡهُم مَّن یُؤۡمِنُ بِهِۦ وَمِنۡهُم مَّن لَّا یُؤۡمِنُ بِهِۦۚ وَرَبُّكَ أَعۡلَمُ بِٱلۡمُفۡسِدِینَ *  وَإِن كَذَّبُوكَ فَقُل لِّی عَمَلِی وَلَكُمۡ عَمَلُكُمۡۖ أَنتُم بَرِیۤـُٔونَ مِمَّاۤ أَعۡمَلُ وَأَنَا۠ بَرِیۤءࣱ مِّمَّا تَعۡمَلُونَ *  وَمِنۡهُم مَّن یَسۡتَمِعُونَ إِلَیۡكَۚ أَفَأَنتَ تُسۡمِعُ ٱلصُّمَّ وَلَوۡ كَانُوا۟ لَا یَعۡقِلُونَ *  وَمِنۡهُم مَّن یَنظُرُ إِلَیۡكَۚ أَفَأَنتَ تَهۡدِی ٱلۡعُمۡیَ وَلَوۡ كَانُوا۟ لَا یُبۡصِرُونَ.*

_"Un mein se kuchh Imaan layenge aur kuchh Imaan nahi layenge aur Aapka Parwardigar Fasaad karnewalon ko khoob Jaanta hai. Aur agar ye Aaki takzeeb karen to keh den ke mere liye mera Amal hai aur  tumhare liye tumhara Amal hai. Tum mere Amal se bari aur mein tumhare Amal se Bezaar hun. Aur in mein se kuchh aise hain jo bazahir Kaan laga kar Aapki baaten sunte hain to kya Aap Behron ko sunayenge jabke woh kuchh bhi na samajhte hon? In mein se baaz woh hain jo tumhe dekhte hain to kya Aap Andhon ko bhi Hidayat de sakte hain chahe woh kuchh na dekh pate hon?"_

(Surah Yunus: 40 - 43)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Guzishta Ayat se pewast in Ayat mein bhi tazkara jaari hai. Ayaat Self Explanatory hai. Allah Ta'ala Paighambar (saww) se farma raha hai ke Aap apni Hujjat tamam karen, kuchh maanenge to kuchh nahi maanenge. Unke Aamaal Allah dekh raha raha hai, Aap unse Bezaari (Tabarrah) ka izhaar karen. Yehi Non-Muslim se ittehaad hai. Jaisa ke Surah Kafiroon mein bhi hai: 'Tumhare liye tumhara Deen, mere liye mera Deen.' Yani ye Social ittehaad hai, jabke ham unke Aqeede se ittefaq nahi rakhte. Kyonki Tableegh o Hidayat ki bhi ek Hadd hoti hai. Agar koi Sun Behra ho to usko sunana be matlab hai, agar koi dekhta to hai lekin Baseerat na ho to usko dekhane se kya fayda. Isliye use uske haal par chhod do. Allah usse niptega. Allah sabko Jaanta hai.

📚

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Muhammad wa Aale Muhammad (as) ke Dushman *وَمِنۡهُم مَّن لَّا یُؤۡمِنُ بِهِۦۚ* ke misdaq hain. *وَرَبُّكَ أَعۡلَمُ بِٱلۡمُفۡسِدِینَ.* Fasaad se Allah aur uske Rasool ki Nafarmani murad hai."_

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Aakhri Zamane mein meri Ummat mein kuchh aise log bhi honge jo Masjid mein aa kar halqa baandh (circle / group banaa) kar baithha karenge aur Duniya aur Hubbe Duniya ka zikr karenge. Tum unke paas na baithhna kyunki Allah ko unki koi haajat nahi hai."_

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p14)

🤲🏻

Ankhon ke Dard ke liye ye Dua baad Namaz e Fajr aur Maghrib padhe. - Mafateeh:

*اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنِّي اَسْاَلُكَ بِحَقِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ عَلَيْكَ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اجْعَلِ النُّوْرَ فِي بَصَرِيْ وَ الْبَصِيْرَةَ فِي دِيْنِيْ وَ الْيَقِيْنَ فِي قَلْبِيْ وَ الْاِخْلَاصَ فِي عَمَلِيْ وَ السَّلَامَةَ فِي نَفْسِيْ وَ السَّعَةَ فِي رِزْقِي وَ الشُّكْرَ لَكَ اَبَدًا مَا اَبْقَيْتَنِيْ.*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*DUNIYA KI MUKHTASAR ZINDAGI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1465)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَا یَظۡلِمُ ٱلنَّاسَ شَیۡـࣰٔا وَلَـٰكِنَّ ٱلنَّاسَ أَنفُسَهُمۡ یَظۡلِمُونَ *  وَیَوۡمَ یَحۡشُرُهُمۡ كَأَن لَّمۡ یَلۡبَثُوۤا۟ إِلَّا سَاعَةࣰ مِّنَ ٱلنَّهَارِ یَتَعَارَفُونَ بَیۡنَهُمۡۚ قَدۡ خَسِرَ ٱلَّذِینَ كَذَّبُوا۟ بِلِقَاۤءِ ٱللَّهِ وَمَا كَانُوا۟ مُهۡتَدِینَ *  وَإِمَّا نُرِیَنَّكَ بَعۡضَ ٱلَّذِی نَعِدُهُمۡ أَوۡ نَتَوَفَّیَنَّكَ فَإِلَیۡنَا مَرۡجِعُهُمۡ ثُمَّ ٱللَّهُ شَهِیدٌ عَلَىٰ مَا یَفۡعَلُونَ.*

_"Yaqeenan Allah Insaano par kuchh bhi Zulm nahi karta. Log khud hi apne upar Zulm karte hain aur jis Din Khuda un sab ko mehshoor (gather) karega to unhe yun mehsoos hoga ke woh Duniya mein mehez ghadhi bhar jaan pehchan ke liye thehre the. Woh log khasare mein rahe jinhone Allah se mulaqat ko jhutlaya aur woh Hidayat yafta na the. Jin bure nataij se Ham unhe dara rahe hain unka kuchh hissa tere jeete ji dikha den ya tujhe isse pehle hi utha len, unhe har qeemat par Hamari taraf hi aana hai aur ye jo kuchh kar rahe hain us par Allah Gawah hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 44 - 46)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Allah Adil hai, Woh kisi par Zulm nahi karta. Balke Insaan Gunah karke khud apne upar zulm karta hai. Jab Insaan Duniya mein Zindagi basar karta hai to use lagta yehi Asl Zindagi hai. Lekin sab log Qayamat ke Din Roze Mehshar jama kiye jayenge aur apna Hisaab Kitab chukana hoga. Jabke Insaan is Duniya ki ek arsa Zindagi guzar chuka hoga aur ek arsa Barzakh ka safar tai kar chuka hoga tab bhi use itna bada waqt ek lamhe ka mehsoos hoga. Kyonki tab use Akhirat ki la mehdood Zindagi dikhayi degi. Yehi zikr Quran mein (Surah Rum:55-56) mein hua hai. Khasare mein woh hoga jisne ye kabhi nahi socha ke use kabhi to apne Parwardigar se mulaqat karna hai. Ye baat bulkul wazeh hai jo Insaan roz kisi na kisi ki Maut ko dekhta rehta hai phir bhi sabaq hasil nahi karta.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Sabse zyada khasaara (nuqsaan) uthanewala wo shakhs hai jo Haq baat kehne par qudrat rakhne ke bawajood Haq baat nahi kehta."_

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p83

🤲🏻

Imam Sajjad (as):

_"Aye mere Sardaar!...Aye Paalne wale! Main Tujhe pukaarta hoo'n lekin sehma hua, dara hua, chahta hua, ummeed rakhta hua. Aye mere Maula! Jab main apne Gunaho'n ko dekhta hun, to ghabraata hun aur Tere karam par nigaah daalta hun, to aarzu badhti hai. Pus, agar Tu mujhe Ma'af kare to Tu behtareen Rahem Karnewala hai aur Azaab de to bhi Zulm Karnewala nahi."_

(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             *5th Zilqad 1441*

   *27th June 2020, Saturday*

♦ _*HAR UMMAT MEIN RASOOL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1465)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلِكُلِّ أُمَّةࣲ رَّسُولࣱۖ فَإِذَا جَاۤءَ رَسُولُهُمۡ قُضِیَ بَیۡنَهُم بِٱلۡقِسۡطِ وَهُمۡ لَا یُظۡلَمُونَ.*

_"Aur har Ummat ke liye ek Rasool hai jabke kisi Ummat ke paas uska Rasool aa jata hai to unke darmiyan Insaaf se Faisla chuka diya jata hai aur unse koi Na-Insaafi nahi ki jati."_

(Surah Yunus: 47)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Is Ayat se ye sabit hai ke tamam pichhli Aqwam mein mein Rasool aaye the. Kisi Qaum ko yun hi rayga nahi chhoda jaisa ke is Ayat mein hai: "Koi Qarya (Town) aisa nahi hai jahan Nazir na aaya ho." (Fatir:24).

Albatta ye zaroori nahi ke woh Qaum mein har waqt maujood ho, jaisa ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) aaj hamare saamne maujood nahi, unki rehlat ho chuki hai lekin unki Risaalat baqi hai. Isliye Zamana Fatrat mein agarche koi Rasool nahi aaya tha, magar unki Risaalat maujood thi.

Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne Apna ye Qanoon banaya hai ke jab kisi Qaum mein Rasool jata hai wahan Deen ki Tableegh karta hai to log do hisson mein bat jate hain. Ek Nabi ki Tasdeeq karta hai to doosra Takzeeb karta hai. Allah ki taraf se inke darmiyan Faisla kar diya jata hai.

Rasool bhej kar Allah Ta'ala ne itmam Hujjat kar diya. Ab jo inkar karega Akherat mein Azaab ka Haqdar hoga jiske asbaab khud usi ne paida kiye. Qayamat ke Deen khud Rasool apni Ummat ke Amaal ke Gawah banege.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Parwardigaar ne har Nabi aur Rasool ko kaamil Aql ke saath bheja aur use Ummat ke saare saahibaan e Aql se afzal qaraar diya."_

(Ijtehaad Ke Jalway, p67)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Rasulullah (saww) ne farmaya - Meri Ummat mein Jannat mein daakhil hone waale zyadatar log Muttaqi (parhez-gaar) aur Achche Akhlaaq (manners / morals) waale honge."_

(Al Kaafi, v3, p354)

🤲🏻

*وَ بِبَرَكَاتِكَ الَّتِىْ بَارَكْتَ فِيْهَا عَلىٰ اِبْرَاهِيْمَ خَلِيْلِكَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فِىْ اُمَّةِ مُحَمَّدٍ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَ اٰلِهِ وَ بَارَكْتَ لِاِسْحَاقَ صَفِيِّكَ فِىْ اُمَّةِ عِيْسىٰ عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ وَ بَارَكْتَ لِيَعْقُوْبَ اِسْرَاۤئِيْلِكَ فِىْ اُمَّةِ مُوْسىٰ عَلَيْهِمَاالسَّلَامُ وَ بَارَكْتَ لِحَبِيْبِكَ مُحَمَّدٍ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَ اٰلِهِ فِىْ عِتْرَتِهِ وَ ذُرِّيَّتِهِ وَ اُمَّتِهِ.*

(Dua-e-Simat - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

       *28th June 2020, Sunday*

♦ _*MUNKARIN KI AZAAB KI KHWAHISH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1466)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَیَقُولُونَ مَتَىٰ هَـٰذَا ٱلۡوَعۡدُ إِن كُنتُمۡ صَـٰدِقِینَ *  قُل لَّاۤ أَمۡلِكُ لِنَفۡسِی ضَرࣰّا وَلَا نَفۡعًا إِلَّا مَا شَاۤءَ ٱللَّهُۗ لِكُلِّ أُمَّةٍ أَجَلٌۚ إِذَا جَاۤءَ أَجَلُهُمۡ فَلَا یَسۡتَـٔۡخِرُونَ سَاعَةࣰ وَلَا یَسۡتَقۡدِمُونَ *  قُلۡ أَرَءَیۡتُمۡ إِنۡ أَتَىٰكُمۡ عَذَابُهُۥ بَیَـٰتًا أَوۡ نَهَارࣰا مَّاذَا یَسۡتَعۡجِلُ مِنۡهُ ٱلۡمُجۡرِمُونَ *  أَثُمَّ إِذَا مَا وَقَعَ ءَامَنتُم بِهِۦۤۚ ءَاۤلۡـَٔـٰنَ وَقَدۡ كُنتُم بِهِۦ تَسۡتَعۡجِلُونَ.*

_"Aur woh kehte hain ke agar tum sachche ho to ye batao ke ye Wada (Azaab) kab poora hoga? Aap keh den ke mein apne liye Nafa Nuqsaan ka Maalik nahi hun jab tak Khuda na chahe har Qaum ke liye ek muddat moayyan hai jisse ek ghadi na takhir ho sakti hai aur na taqdeem (precede). Aap kahen bhala socho to sahi agar tum uska Azaab Raat ke waqt ya Din mein aa jaye to tum kya karoge? Akhir in Mujrimon ko kis baat ki jaldi hai. To kya tum Azaab nazil hone ke baad Imaan laoge? Ab bachna chahte ho? Halanke tum khud iske jaldi aane ka taqaza kar rahe the."_

(Surah Yunus: 48 - 51)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Ayat ka zikr bilkul wazeh hai. Allah Munkarin ka kinayatan zikr kar raha hai. Unki Jihalat ko zahir kar raha hai. Chunke woh log Khuda ki Qudrat se hi inkar kar rahe hain isliye aisa sawal kar rahe hain. Rasool ya Paighambar ke ikhtiyar mein kisi ko Azaab mein mubtila karna nahi hai, iska ikhtiyar sirf Allah ko hai. Allah ne Azaab ki muddat tai kar rakhi hai, uska time fix hai. Is time ke na pehle aayega na baad mein. Phir unke salahiyat par sawal uthta hai, Allah ka Azaab aa bhi gaya to woh kya kar payenge, kya woh apne aap ko bacha payenge? Kya Azaab ke baad woh Imaan le aayenge? Yani woh log sirf aur sirf Rasool (saww) ka mazaq uda rahe hain. Haan ek Munkir e Ali (as) ne bhi Azaab ka taqaza kiya ke agar Wilayat Ali (as) Haq hai to mujh par Azaab nazil ho jaye. Turant Aasmaan se ek Patthar aa ke us par gira aur woh wahi dher ho gaya (Surah Ma'arij:1-2) Yani Allah Apne Wali ke Inkar par turant Azaab nazil kar deta hai, jabke Khud ke Inkaar par kuchh mohlat de deta.

⏱️

Imam Sadiq (as): (Ayat (10:49) ke zel mein)

_"Isse wo muddat murad hai jo Shabe Qadr mein Malakul Maut ko batayi jati hai."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⏱️

Imam Baqir (as): (Ayat (10:50) zel mein)

_"Ye wo Azaab hai jo Akheri Zamane mein Fasiq Ahle Qibla par nazil hoga aur woh isse qabl Azaab aane ka inkar kar rahe honge."_

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 🤲🏻

*يَوْمَ يَعَضُّ الظَّالِمُ عَلٰى يَدَيْهِ يَقُوْلُ يَا لَيْتَنِيْ اتَّخَذْتُ مَعَ الرَّسُوْلِ سَبِيْلًا وَ اَسْاَلُكَ الْاَمَانَ يَوْمَ يُعْرَفُ الْمُجْرِمُوْنَ بِسِيْمَاهُمْ فَيُؤْخَذُ بِالنَّوَاصِيْ وَ الْاَقْدَامِ وَ اَسْاَلُكَ الْاَمَانَ يَوْمَ لَا يَجْزِيْ وَالِدٌ عَنْ وَلَدِهِ وَ لَا مَوْلُوْدٌ هُوَ جَازٍ عَنْ وَالِدِهِ شَيْئًا اِنَّ وَعْدَ اللّٰهِ حَقٌّ وَ اَسْاَلُكَ الْاَمَانَ يَوْمَ لَا يَنْفَعُ الظَّالِمِيْنَ مَعْذِرَتُهُمْ وَ لَهُمُ اللَّعْنَةُ وَ لَهُمْ سُوۤءُ الدَّارِ...*

(Munajat e Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ _*MUNKARIN E HAQ KO SAZA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1467)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ثُمَّ قِیلَ لِلَّذِینَ ظَلَمُوا۟ ذُوقُوا۟ عَذَابَ ٱلۡخُلۡدِ هَلۡ تُجۡزَوۡنَ إِلَّا بِمَا كُنتُمۡ تَكۡسِبُونَ * وَیَسۡتَنۢبِـُٔونَكَ أَحَقٌّ هُوَۖ قُلۡ إِی وَرَبِّیۤ إِنَّهُۥ لَحَقࣱّۖ وَمَاۤ أَنتُم بِمُعۡجِزِینَ.*

_"Phir Zalimon se kaha jayega ke ab hamesha ka Azaab chakho. Tumhe tumhare Aamaal ko Reward ke baghair tumhe aur kya badla diya ja sakta hai? Woh Aap se daryaft karte hain ke kya waqai woh Haq hai? Aap keh den ke ji haan mujhe mere Rab ki Qasam! Ye bilkul Haq hai tum ise zahoor pazeer hone se aajiz nahi kar sakte."_

(Surah Yunus: 52 - 53)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Guzishta Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne unke Azaab ki khwahish ka zikr kiya tha jabke woh Munkarin aisi demand karke Allah aur Uske Rasool ka mazaq uda rahe the. Pas Allah ne Qayamat ke Din ki yaad delaate hue farmata hai ke bahut Azaab ki maang kar rahe the, lo ab chakho Azaab!

Allah Apni Nabi se farma raha hai ke Aap Qasam kha ke kahen ye Haq hai. Haq ke inkar karne walon ke saath aisa hi hoga. Baarha Rasoole Khuda (saww) Hazrat Ali (as) ka tarruf karaya ke Ali (as) Haq hain.

👉🏻

Imam Baqir (as) is Ayat ke zel mein farmate hain:

_"Ayat ka Maqsad ye hai ke Ahle Makkah Aap (saww) se Ali Ibne Abi Talib (as) ke mutalliq poochhte hain ke kya wohi Imam hai? Aap (saww) keh den ke ji haan mujhe mere Rab ki Qasam! wohi Imam hain."_

(Amaali Shaikh Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Log Aap (saww) se poochhte hain ke Aap (saww) Ali (as) ke jo Fazail bayan karte hain kya waqai woh Haq hai? Aap (saww) keh den ke ji haan mujhe mere Rab ki Qasam! Woh Fazail Haq hain."_

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Aisi Aag (Jahannum) se bacho jiski cheekh o pukaar sakht hogi, jikse sholay (flames) shadeed (extreme) honge aur jiska Azaab hamesha naya hoga."_ 

(Gorar ul Hakam, Meezan ul Hikmah , Vol 2)

🚩

Imam Ali (as):

_"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki Ma'arefat hai aur badtareen Andhapan hamare Fazl se Aa'nkhen band kar lena hai."_

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)

🤲🏻

*اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا مَوْلَايَ اَنَا مَوْلَاكَ عَارِفٌ بِاُوْلَاكَ وَ اُخْرَاكَ اَتَقَرَّبُ اِلَى اللّٰهِ تَعَالٰى بِكَ وَ بِاٰلِ بَيْتِكَ وَ اَنْتَظِرُ ظُهُوْرَكَ وَ ظُهُوْرَ الْحَقِّ عَلٰى يَدَيْكَ، وَ اَسْاَلُ اللهَ اَنْ يُصَلِّيَ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ...*

(Ziyarat Sahibe Amr (as) Roze Juma - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ _*MUNKARIN KI NIDAMAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1468)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوۡ أَنَّ لِكُلِّ نَفۡسࣲ ظَلَمَتۡ مَا فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ لَٱفۡتَدَتۡ بِهِۦۗ وَأَسَرُّوا۟ ٱلنَّدَامَةَ لَمَّا رَأَوُا۟ ٱلۡعَذَابَۖ وَقُضِیَ بَیۡنَهُم بِٱلۡقِسۡطِ وَهُمۡ لَا یُظۡلَمُونَ *  أَلَاۤ إِنَّ لِلَّهِ مَا فِی ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِۗ أَلَاۤ إِنَّ وَعۡدَ ٱللَّهِ حَقࣱّ وَلَـٰكِنَّ أَكۡثَرَهُمۡ لَا یَعۡلَمُونَ *  هُوَ یُحۡیِۦ وَیُمِیتُ وَإِلَیۡهِ تُرۡجَعُونَ*

_"Agar har Zulm karnewale ke paas rue Zameen ki Daulat bhi ho to woh is Azaab se bachne ke liye Fidye mein dene par amaada ho jayega (Rishwat). Aur jab woh Azaab ko dekhenge to Dil mein nidamat mehsoos karenge. Magar unke darmiyan Insaaf ke mutabiq Faisla kar diya jayega aur un par Zulm nahi kiya jayega."_

_"Agah ho jao ke Aasmaano aur Zameen mein jo kuchh bhi hai wo Allah ki Milkiyat hai. Agah raho ke Allah ka Waada Sachcha hai magar aksar logon ko Ilm nahi hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 54 - 56)

📚📖 😔

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Allah Ta'ala Munkarin Zalimeen ke tassurat ka zikr kar raha hai. Ye Duniyadar log ke samajhte hain ke jaise Duniya mein Police ko rishwat de kar setting kar ke Saza khatm ya kam karai jati hai aur aksar Daulatmand Mujrimon ka yehi dastoor hai. Allah ke Darbar mein ye sab kuch nahi chalega. Tum chahe kitne kyon ka Amir shakhs ho, poore Aalam ki Milkiyat Allah ki hai. Insaan ke liye koi farar ki raah nahi, bas jab woh Azaab ka saamna karega woh Nidamat ke siwa kuchh mehsoos nahi karega.

🕌

Agarche ye Ayat tamam Zalimon ke liye hai magar Aale Muhammad (as) ke Ghasib iske misdaq e khaas hain. Jab woh "Raja'at" mein uthaye jayenge to woh hasrat se kahenge ke kaash saari rue Zameen Hamari Milkiyat hoti aur ham ise Fidye mein de kar Azaab se mehfooz ho jate lekin us Din ki nidamat unhe koi fayda na degi.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

😔

Ek Shakhs ne Hazrat Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) se arz kiya (ye Ayat padhi 10:54 aur kaha:) bhala jo shakhs Azaab mein mubtila hua use Dil mein Sharmindgi ki kya zaroorat hai, use to khil kar nidamat ka izhaar karna chahiye?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

_"Woh Dushmano ko Ilzaam (blame) se bachne ke liye Dil hi Dil mein nidamat mehsoos karenge."_

(Noorus Saqlain)

😔

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Roze Qayamat ki Nidamat Badtareen Nidamat hai."_

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Kazim (as):

_"Jab bhi Momin se koi Gunah sarzad hota hai to use wo bura mehsoos hota hai aur woh us par Naadim (sharminda) hota hai, kyunki Nabi Akram (saww) ka farmaan hai ke Tauba ke liye Nidamat (sharmindagi) kaafi hai. Jise Neki kar ke khushi mehsoos ho to wo Momin hai. Jo shakhs Gunah kar ke sharminda nahi hota to woh Momin nahi hai aur woh shafa'at ka haqdar nahi hai. Aisa shakhs Zaalim hai aur Allah Ta'ala ka farmaan hai, "Zaalimon ka na koi mushfiq Dost hoga aur na hi koi Shafa'at karnewala hoga ke jiski Shafa'at qubool ki jaaye (Surah Momin:18)."_

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p401)

🤲🏻

*اِلٰهِيْ لَئِنْ اَعْطَيْتُ نَفْسِيَ سُؤْلَهَا فَهَاۤ اَنَا فِيْ رَوْضِ النَّدَامَةِ اَرْتَعُ*

_"Bare Ilaha! Agarche meine apne Nafs ko jo chaha karne diya, ab mein yahan Pachhtave ki sar Zameen par palat raha hun."_

(Munajat e Ameerul Momeni - Sahifa e Alaviyah)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             *9th Zilqad 1441*

    *1st July 2020, Wednesday*

     ♦ _*QUR'AN SHIFA HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1469)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ قَدۡ جَاۤءَتۡكُم مَّوۡعِظَةࣱ مِّن رَّبِّكُمۡ وَشِفَاۤءࣱ لِّمَا فِی ٱلصُّدُورِ وَهُدࣰى وَرَحۡمَةࣱ لِّلۡمُؤۡمِنِینَ.*

_"Aye logo! Tumhare paas tumhare Rab ki taraf se Nasihat aur Dilon ko Shifa dene wali cheez aa chuki hai jo Ahle Imaan ke liye Hidayat aur Rehmat hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 57)

 ----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

📚📖 🙇

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Guzishta Ayat mein Allah ne un Munkarin par Azaab nazil kiya jinhone Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Nasihat nahi maani jabke Nasihat ke liye Allah ne Qur'an ko nazil kiya jo ke Insaan ke liye Shafee hai.

📚

Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):

_"Allah ne tum par aisi Kitab  nazil ki hai jo Shukook o Shubhhaat se Dilon ko Shifa bakhashti hai."_

(Kitab Ahleelja, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Ek Shakhs ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se Seene mein Dard ki ki to Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

_"Qur'an ke zariye Shifa talab karo, kyonki Allah Ta'ala farmata hai (10:57)"_

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Musa (as) se farmaya:

_"Mein Muhammad (saww) ko Duniya mein bhejunga aur us par Qur'an nazil karunga jo Haq o Baatil mein Faisla karnewala hoga aur wo Shaitaani Waswason se Seeno ko Shifa bakhshega."_

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

_"Qur'an ki taleem hasil karo, Qur'an Dilon ki Bahar hai aur iske Noor se Shifa talab karo, wo Seeno ke liye Shifa hai."_

(Nahjul Balagha, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*يَا وَصِىَّ الْحَسَنِ وَالْخَلَفَ الْحُجَّةَ اَيُّهَا الْقَاۤئِمُ الْمُنْتَظَرُ الْمَهْدِىُّ يَا بْنَ رَسُوْلِ اللهِ يَا حُجَّةَ اللهِ عَلٰى خَلْقِهِ يَا سَيِّدَنَا وَمَوْلٰينَا اِنَّا تَوَجَّهْنَا وَاسْتَشْفَعْنَا وَتَوَسَّلْنَا بِكَ اِلَى اللهِ وَقَدَّمْنَاكَ بَيْنَ يَدَىْ حَاجَاتِنَا يَا وَجِيْهًا عِنْدَ اللهِ اِشْفَعْ لَنَا عِنْدَ اللهِ.*

(Dua e Tawassul - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        *2nd July 2020, Thursday*

     ♦ _*MOMIN KI KHUSHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1470)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلۡ بِفَضۡلِ ٱللَّهِ وَبِرَحۡمَتِهِۦ فَبِذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ فَلۡیَفۡرَحُوا۟ هُوَ خَیۡرࣱ مِّمَّا یَجۡمَعُونَ.*

_"Aap keh den ke inhe Khuda ka Fazl o Rehmat (Qur'an) paa kar khushiyan manani chahiye. Ye unki Daulat se kahin behtar hai jise woh jama kar rahe hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 58)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Guzishta Ayat se ye paiwast hai. Jisko Shifa denewali cheez mil jaye usko to bahut khush hona chahiye.

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Jisko Khuda Islam ki Hidayat de de aur Qur'an ki taleem ata kar de phir woh Faqr o Faqa ki shikayat kare to Allah uski Aankhon ke darmiyan Qayamat tak Faqr likh deta hai."_ Phir AanHazrat (saww) ne ye Ayat padhi. (10:58)

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

Allah ne jis Ne'mat ka yaha zikr kiya wo Hidayat, Rehmat, Nasihat o Maueza hai. Jis tarah Qur'an logon ke liye Hidayat aur Shafee hai, us tarah Qur'an e Natiq. Qur'an e Samit Qur'an Natiq ke baghair samajh mein nahi aayega.

📚

Is silsile mein rivayaat mulaheza farmayen.

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Fazl se Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) aur Rehmat se Hazrat Ali Murtaza (as) murad hain. Maqsad ye hai ke jinhe Muhammad (saww) wa Ali (as) mil jayen unhe khush hona chahiye. Isiliye hamare Shiyon ko chahiye ke woh in do Buzurgwar Shakhsiyat ko hasil karke khush ho jayen, kyonki inka mil jana Sone Chandi ke milne se kahin behtar hai jise hamare Dushman jama karne mein masroof hain."_

(Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) se farmaya:

_"Us Zaat ki Qasam! Jisne Muhammad (saww) ko bar Haq Nabi bana kar bheja hai woh Shakhs mujh par Imaan nahi laya jisne tera Inkaar kiya aur jisne tera Inkaar kiya hai usne mera iqraar nahi kiya. Tere Munkir ka to Khuda par bhi Imaan nahi hai. Teri Fazilat meri Fazilat ka ek juz hai aur meri Fazilat dar asl Khuda ki Fazilat hai aur Allah ka farman hai: (10:58)"_

_"Logon! Allah ke Fazl se tumhare Nabi ki Nabuwwat aur Allah ki Rehmat se Ali Ibne Abi Talib (as) ki Wilayat murad hai aur hamare Shiyon ko Nabuwwat o Wilayat par khush hona chahiye aur ye Azeem Daulat Mukhalefin ki Aulad aur Duniyadari ki Daulat se kahin behtar hai."_

(Amaali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"…Aye Misma! Jab se Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) qatl kiye gaye, Zameen o Aasmaan girya kar raha hai aur Farishto'n se zyada hum par koi nahi roya aur unke Aa'nsuo'n ka silsila jaari hai, tootne waala nahi hai. Jo koi hamara Haq samajh kar hamare masaaib par rota hai to Allah Ta'ala uspar Rehmat ki nazar daalta hai aur jab uski Aa'nkh ka Aa'nsu uske rukhsar par jaari ho to agar uske ek Aa'nsu ka ek qatra bhi Jahannum mein gir jaye to Jahannum ki Aag ki garmi khatm ho jayegi aur wo sard (thandi) ho jayegi. Aur jis dil mein hamare liye dard hoga, wo us din khush hoga jab humen apni Maut ke waqt dekhega aur uski ye khushi uske dil ke liye na khatm hone waali hogi yahan tak ke woh hamare paas Hauz e Kausar par pahunchega aur Hauz e Kausar bhi hamare mohib ko dekh kar khushi mehsoos karega…"_

(Kaamiluz Ziyaraat, ch32, p156, Nafsul Mahmoom, p15, h4, Azadari - Ahlebait (as) Ki Nazar Mein, p183)

🤲🏻

*اَنْ تُصَلِّيَ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ ۟اِلطَّيِّبِيْنَ وَ اَنْ تَجْعَلَنِيْ مِنَ الْمُطْمَئِنِّيْنَ الْفَاۤئِزِيْنَ الْفَرِحِيْنَ الْمُسْتَبْشِرِيْنَ الَّذِيْنَ لَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَ لَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُوْنَ.*

(Ziyarat Janabe Narjis Khatoon (sa) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

              *12th Zilqad 1441*

      *4th July 2020, Saturday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ _*MUSHREKIN KA IFTERA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1471)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلۡ أَرَءَیۡتُم مَّاۤ أَنزَلَ ٱللَّهُ لَكُم مِّن رِّزۡقࣲ فَجَعَلۡتُم مِّنۡهُ حَرَامࣰا وَحَلَـٰلࣰا قُلۡ ءَاۤللَّهُ أَذِنَ لَكُمۡۖ أَمۡ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ تَفۡتَرُونَ *  وَمَا ظَنُّ ٱلَّذِینَ یَفۡتَرُونَ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ ٱلۡكَذِبَ یَوۡمَ ٱلۡقِیَـٰمَةِۗ إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَذُو فَضۡلٍ عَلَى ٱلنَّاسِ وَلَـٰكِنَّ أَكۡثَرَهُمۡ لَا یَشۡكُرُونَ.*

_"Aap kahen ke tum logon ne kabhi ye bhi socha ke jo Rizq Allah ne tumhare liye utara hai us mein tumne khud hi kisi ko Haram aur kisi ko Halal thehra liya. Inse poochho ke kya Allah ne tumhe iski ijazat di hai ye tum Allah par iftara kar rahe ho (tohmat bandhte)? Aur jo log Khuda par Iftrapardazi (invent) kar rahe hain unka kiya guman hai ke Qayamat ke Din unse kya sulook kiya jayega. Allah to logon par Fazl Karnewala hai lekin logon ki aksariyat Shukr karnewali nahi hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 59 - 60)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Ye Zikr guzishta Ayaat mein bhi aa chuka. Surah Maeda:103 aur Surah An'am: 138-139. Jisko ham Nov 2017 mein post kar chuke hain. Phir se repeat kar rahe hain:

📚👉🏻

_"Tumse pahle ek giroh ne isi qism ke sawal kiye the. Phir un baton ke Munkir ban gaye the."_

_"Allah ne na koi "Bahira" muqarrar kiya hai aur na "Sayba" na "Wasila" aur na "Haam". Lekin Kafiron ka ye watira hai ke woh Khuda par jhooti baatein taraashten hain aur unki aksariyat be Aql hai."_ (5:102 - 103)

Zamana Jahiliyyat mein But parasti aam thi aur Buton ke alag naam se yaad kiya jata tha. India mein ye aaj tak jaari hai. Arab mein jin Buton ke bahut sare naam the, un mein se kuchh naam is Ayat mein diye hain.

🐪

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Zamana Jahiliyyat mein jab koi Oontni yake baad deegar do Nar (male) paida karti to woh kahte the ke usne _"Naron ka Wasaal"_ kiya hai. Use zabah karna Halaal nahi samajhte the aur use khaana jaez nahi jaante the. Jab koi Oontni 10 bachche janti to use "Sayba" ka naam dete the. Us par sawari karne aur uske gosht khane ko Haraam samajhte the. Aur "Haam" Oontni ke saand ko kahte the. Woh uska gosht khaana bhi jaez na samajhte the. Allah Ta'ala ne Ailan kiya ke Usne is tarah ka koi hukm nazil nahi kiya."

(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar)

🐪

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Amr bin Yahya bin Qama' bin Khandaf ki Makkah par Hukomat qayem hui thi. Deen e Islam ko sab se pahle usi ne tabdeel kiya tha. Usi ne But aur Moortiyan nasb ki thi aur usi ne "Bahira", "Sayba", "Wasila" aur "Haam" ka tasawwur diya tha. Meine dekha ke woh Dozakh mein jal raha tha aur uski badboo se Ahle Dozakh ko aziyyat mahsoos ho rahi thi."_

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 🕌

Imam Ali (as)

_"Wallah! Na mere baap ne buto'n ki parastish (idol-worship) ki, na mere dada Abdul Muttalib ne, na mere jadd e buzurg Janabe Hashim ne, na Abde Munaaf ne. Balke wo log Ka'abe ki jaanib rukh kar ke Namaz padhte the aur Deen e Ibrahim (as) par qaayam the aur Rasule Khuda (saww) ke Deen se mutamassik rahe."_

(Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p67)

🤲🏻

*فَمَا تَنَاقَضَتْ اَفْعَالُكَ وَ لَا اخْتَلَفَتْ اَقْوَالُكَ وَ لَا تَقَلَّبَتْ اَحْوَالُكَ وَ لَا ادَّعَيْتَ وَ لَا افْتَرَيْتَ عَلَى اللّٰهِ كَذِبًا.......*

(Ziyarat Aminullah - Mafateeh)

 ♦ _*ALLAH DEKH RAHA HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1472)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا تَكُونُ فِی شَأۡنࣲ وَمَا تَتۡلُوا۟ مِنۡهُ مِن قُرۡءَانࣲ وَلَا تَعۡمَلُونَ مِنۡ عَمَلٍ إِلَّا كُنَّا عَلَیۡكُمۡ شُهُودًا إِذۡ تُفِیضُونَ فِیهِۚ وَمَا یَعۡزُبُ عَن رَّبِّكَ مِن مِّثۡقَالِ ذَرَّةࣲ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَلَا فِی ٱلسَّمَاۤءِ وَلَاۤ أَصۡغَرَ مِن ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ وَلَاۤ أَكۡبَرَ إِلَّا فِی كِتَـٰبࣲ مُّبِینٍ.*

_"Aye Nabi (saww)! Tum jis haal mein bhi hote ho aur Qur'an mein se jo kuchh bhi sunate ho aur Aye logon! Tum jo kuchh bhi karte ho un sab ke dauran Ham tum par Gawah hote hain. Jab bhi tum koi Amal karte ho aur tumhare Parwardigar se Zameen o Aasmaan ka koi zarrah makhfi (hidden) nahi hai aur zarreh se koi cheez chhoti ya badi aisi nahi hai magar ye sab Kitab e Mubeen mein hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 61)

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Allah har Insaan ke Amal ko dekh raha hai. Poori Kainaat par Allah ki Nazar hai.

👁️

Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):

_"AanHazrat (saww) jab bhi is Ayat ko padhte the to Aap (saww) bahut zyada rote the."_

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

👀

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

_"Hamare Rab se koi cheez poshida nahi hai aur ye kaise mumkin hai ke Khaliq (Creator) ko Apni Makhlooq (Creatures) ka Ilm na ho, jabke Woh Khaliq o Aleem hai aur Uske Ilm ki Shaan ye hai (10:61)"_

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

👀

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Allah tumhari surato'n aur tumhare aamaal ki taraf nahi dekhta balke wo tumhaare quloob (dil) aur tumhari niyyato'n ko dekhta hai."_

(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p173)

👁️

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Jo shakhs ye baat samajh lega ke jo kuchh uske Mu'nh se nikalta hai Allah Ta'ala sunta hai aur jo Nek aur Bad Amal karta hai Allah use dekhta aur Jaanta hai. To us shakhs ka ye samajh lena use bahut si buraaiyo'n se baaz rakhega."_

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p121)

🤲🏻

 *يَا مَوْضِعَ كُلِّ شَكْوٰى، وَيَا شَاهِدَ كُلِّ نَجْوٰى، وَيَا عَالِمَ كُلِّ خَفِيَّةِ،....*

(Dua 1st Day Ramazan -Mafateeh)

             *18th Zilqad 1441*

       *10th July 2020, Friday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        ♦ _*AULIYA E KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1473)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَلَاۤ إِنَّ أَوۡلِیَاۤءَ ٱللَّهِ لَا خَوۡفٌ عَلَیۡهِمۡ وَلَا هُمۡ یَحۡزَنُونَ *  ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَكَانُوا۟ یَتَّقُونَ.*

_"Agah ho jao! ke Auliya e Khuda par na to Khauf taari hota hai aur na hi ghamgeen wa Ranjeeda hote hain. Ye woh log hain jo Imaan laye aur Khuda se darte rahe."_

(Surah Yunus: 62 - 63)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne is Ayat ko padhne ke baad farmaya:

_"Jaante ho woh Auliya e Khuda kaun hain?"_

_"Woh ham hain aur woh log hain jo hamare baad hamari Pairavi karenge. Hamare liye bhi Khush Khabri hai aur ham se zyada Khush Khabri unke liye hai."_

Logo ne poochha unke liya zyada kyon?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

_"Nahi, woh itni takleef uthayenge jo tumne nahi uthayi aur woh us taqat ka muzahera karenge jiska muzahera tumne nahi kiya."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sajjad (as) & Imam Baqir (as):

_"(10:62) Lekin ye zaroori hai ke woh Allah ke faraez ada karen aur Rasool e Khuda (saww) ki Sunnaton ki pairavi karen aur Maharim e Ilahi se kinara kashi ikhtiyar karen aur Duniya ke dil farebiyon se juda rahe aur jo kuchh Khuda ke haan Ajr o Sawab hai uski taraf raghbat rakhen aur Paak o Pakeeza Rizq e Khuda wandi talash karen aur phir kisi ke fakhr o kasrat ke izhar ka iraada na karen aur Wajib Huqooq ke liye Daulat kharch karen. Ye woh log hain jinki kamai mein Khuda Barkat rakhi hai aur jo kuchh unhone apni Akherat ke liye aage bheja hai uska unhe Sawab diya jayega."_

(Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Hazrat Ali (as):

_"Allah ne 4 cheezon ko 4 cheezon mein makhfi (hidden) rakha hai. Allah ne Apni Wali ko Apne Bandon mein makhfi rakha hai lehaza Khuda ke Bando mein se kisi ko bhi haqeer na samajhna jisko tum haqeer samajh rahe ho ain mumkin hai ke woh Khuda ka Wali ho aur tumhe uska Ilm na ho."_

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Abu Baseer! Khush khabri hai hamare Qaem ke Shiyon ke liye jo unki Ghaibat ke zamane mein unka Intezar karenge aur unke Zahoor ke waqt unki ita'at karenge. Woh log Khuda ke aise Wali hain jin par na to koi khauf hai aur na woh ghamgeen honge."_

(Kitab Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*فَاِنَّكُمْ وَسِيْلَتِىْ اِلَى اللهِ وَبِحُبِّكُمْ وَبِقُرْبِكُمْ اَرْجُوْ نَجَاةً مِنَ اللهِ فَكُوْنُوْا عِنْدَ اللهِ رَجَاۤئِىْ يَا سَادَتِىْ يَا اَوْلِيَاۤءَ اللهِ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِمْ اَجْمَعِيْنَ وَلَعَنَ اللهُ اَعْدَاۤءَ اللهِ ظَالِمِيْهِمْ مِنَ الْاَوَّلِيْنَ وَالْاٰخِرِيْنَ اٰمِيْنَ رَبَّ الْعَالَمِيْنَ۔*

(Dua e Tawassul - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        *11th July 2020, Saturday*

♦ _*MOMIN O MUTTAQI KE LIYE BASHAARAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1474)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَكَانُوا۟ یَتَّقُونَ *  لَهُمُ ٱلۡبُشۡرَىٰ فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَفِی ٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۚ لَا تَبۡدِیلَ لِكَلِمَـٰتِ ٱللَّهِۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ هُوَ ٱلۡفَوۡزُ ٱلۡعَظِیمُ*

_"Ye woh log hain jo Imaan laye aur Khuda se darte rahe. Unke liye Zindagani e Duniya aur Akherat dono maqamat par Bashaarat aur Khush Khabri hai aur Kalamaat e Khuda mein koi tabdeeli waqe nahi ho sakti aur yehi dar Haqeeqat Azeem Kamyabi hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 63 - 64)

📚📖 🍁

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

_"Duniyavi Khush Khabri se woh Nek aur achhe Khwab murad hain jo Momin ko dikhai dete hain aur Akherat ki Khush Khabri se wo Khush Khabri murad hai jo Maut ke waqt Momin ko di jati hai ke Khuda ne tujhe Bakhsh diya hai aur jo teri Mayyat utha kar teri Qabr par layenge unhe bhi Ma'af kar diya jayega."_

(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

🍁

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Jab tum mein se kisi ki Jaan Halq tak pahunchti dekho to us par Malakul Maut nazil hota hai aur usse kaha jata hai ke tujhe jis cheez ki umeed thi wo tujhe mil chuki hai aur jis cheez se tu khaufzada tha ab tu usse mutmain ho chuka hai.' Phir uske liye Jannat ke Ghar ka Darwaza khol diya jata hai aur usse kaha jata hai ke Jannat mein apna Makan dekho aur nigah karo Rasoole Khuda (saww), Ali Murtaza (as) aur Hasan o Husain (as) tere Rafeeq hain. Allah ka farman hai (10:63-64)."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🍁

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Duniyavi Bashaarat se wo Bashaarat murad hai jo unhe Imam e Qiyam e Qayem (atfs) aur unke Zahoor aur Dushmano ke Qatl ki dhamki deta hai aur Akherat ki Khush Khabri se Akherat ki Najaat aur Muhammad o Aale Muhammad (as) ke paas Hauz par warid hona murad hai."_

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 🍁

Imam Reza (as):

_"Jo Aaj (Ghadeer) ke Din kisi Momin ko milne jayega, Allah 70 kism ke Noor uski qabr mein bhejega aur rozana 70000 Farishte uski Qabr mein milne aayenge aur Jannat ki Bashaarat denge."_

(40 Hadith - Ghadeer)

📝

Imam Kazim (as):

_"Allah Ta'ala ne Apni Kitaab mein Ahle Aql o Fahem ko Bashaarat (khush-khabari) di hai. Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya, "Ye Khush-khabari un bando'n se mutalliq hai jo Hadees ko gaur se sunen aur jaisi sunen waisi hi bayaan karen, na kuch badhayen aur na ghatayen."_

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p115)

🤲🏻

*الَّذِيْنَ اٰمَنُوْا وَ هَاجَرُوْا وَ جَاهَدُوْا فِيْ سَبِيْلِ اللّٰهِ بِاَمْوَالِهِمْ وَ اَنْفُسِهِمْ اَعْظَمُ دَرَجَةً عِنْدَ اللّٰهِ وَ اُوْلٰۤئِكَ هُمُ الْفَاۤئِزُوْنَ يُبَشِّرُهُمْ رَبُّهُمْ بِرَحْمَةٍ مِنْهُ وَ رِضْوَانٍ وَ جَنَّاتٍ فِيْهَا نَعِيْمٌ مُقِيمٌ خَالِدِيْنَ فِيْهَا اَبَدًا اِنَّ اللّٰهَ عِنْدَهُ اَجْرٌ عَظِيْمٌ.*

(Ziyarat e Roze Ghadeer - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

              *20th Zilqad 1441*

         *12th July 2020, Sunday*

♦ _*QABR MEIN DEEDAR E  NOOR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1475)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَكَانُوا۟ یَتَّقُونَ *  لَهُمُ ٱلۡبُشۡرَىٰ فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَفِی ٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۚ لَا تَبۡدِیلَ لِكَلِمَـٰتِ ٱللَّهِۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ هُوَ ٱلۡفَوۡزُ ٱلۡعَظِیمُ.*

_"Ye woh log hain jo Imaan laye aur Khuda se darte rahe. Unke liye Zindagani e Duniya aur Akherat dono maqamat par Bashaarat aur Khush Khabri hai aur Kalamaat e Khuda mein koi tabdeeli waqe nahi ho sakti aur yehi dar Haqeeqat Azeem Kamyabi hai."_

(Surah Yunus: 63 - 64)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_ (Cont'd...)

Mo'meneen o Muttaqeen ke liye ye Bashaarat hai ke woh Rasoole Khuda (saww) wa Hazrat Ali (as) ka Deedar Qabr mein jaate hi karenge.

⚰️ 👉🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Aqba! Qayamat ke Din Allah bas usi ke Amal aur Aqeede ko qubool karega jo is Aqeede ka karband hoga jiske tum karband ho. Tumhari Aankhon ki thandak mein bas yahi der hai ke iska Saans Halq tak pahunch jaye. Phir woh inhe dekh lega."_

Aqba ne sawal kiya halat e Niza mein marne wala kis cheez ko dekhega?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

_"Khuda ki Qasam! Woh un dono ko dekhega. Marnewala Hazrat Rasoole Khuda (saww) aur Hazrat Ali (as) ko dekhta hai aur koi Momin unhe dekhe baghair nahi mar sakta. Rasoole Khuda (saww) marnewale ki Sar ki janib baithte hain aur Hazrat Ali (as) uski payeti ki janib (leg side) baithte hain. Rasoole Khuda (saww) usse farmate hain: 'Tujhe Bashaarat ho, mein Allah ka Rasool hun, tu ne Duniya ka jo tarka chhoda hai, mein tere liye usse behtar hun.' Phir Hazrat Ali (as) usse farmate hain: 'Aye Wali e Khuda! Tujhe Bashaarat ho! Mein wohi Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) hun jinse tu Mohabbat rakhta tha. Aaj mein zaroor tujhe fayda pahunchaonga. Ye baat Allah ki Kitab mein maujood hai (10:63-64)"_

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚰️

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Abu Hamza! Jab woh waqt aata hai (Maut), to Rasoole Khuda (saww) aur Hazrat Ali (as) marnewale ke paas tashreef laate hain phir woh marnewale ke sarhane baith jate hain. Us waqt Rasoole Khuda (saww) farmate hai: Kya tu mujhe nahi jaanta? Mein Allah ka Rasool hun. Tu hamare paas aa ja, tere aage isse kahin zyada bhalai hai jise tu chhod raha hai. Tujhe jo khauf tha ab tu mutmain ho chuka hai aur tujhe jiski umeed thi woh tere paas aa chuki hai. Aaye Rooh! Iske Badan se nikal kar Allah ki Rehmat o Raza ki taraf chali aa.' Us waqt Hazrat Ali (as) bhi usse wohi kuchh kehte hain jo Rasoole Khuda (saww) kehte hain."_

_"Ye woh log hain jo Imaan laye aur Khuda se darte rahe."_

(Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Jo hamare Masaaeb par Aah o Nalaa karte hain aur hamari Khushi mein Khush hote hain aur hamare Gham mein Ghamgeen hote ho, beshak ke tum marte waqt hamare Aaba o Ajdaad (as) ko apne paas haazir dekhoge aur wo tumhare baare mein Malekul Maut se sifaarish karenge aur tumhe aisi bashaarat denge ke marne se pehle tumhari aa'nkhein munawwar ho jaayengi aur Malekul Maut tum par bachche ki nisbat Maa se bhi zyada meherbaan ho jayega."_

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p121)

🤲🏻

*وَقَدْ دَنَا يَوْمَهُ مِنْ حَتْفِهِ وَاَحْدَقَ بِهِ مَلَكُ الْمَوْتِ فِىْ اَعْوَانِهِ يُعَالِجُ سَكَرَاتِ الْمَوْتِ وَحِيَاضَهُ تَدُوْرُ عَيْنَاهُ يَمِيْنًا وَشِمَالًا يَنْظُرُ اِلٰى اَحِبَّاۤئِهِ وَاَوِدَّاۤئِهِ واَخِلَّاۤئِهِ قَدْ مُنِعَ مِنَ الْكَلَا مِ وَحُجِبَ عَنِ الْخِطَابِ يَنْظُرُ اِلٰى نَفْسِهِ حَسْرَةً لَايَسْتَطِيْعُ لَهَا ضَرًّا وَلَا نَفْعًا وَاَنَا خِلْوٌ مِنْ ذٰلِكَكُلِّهِ بِجُوْدِكَ وَكَرَمِكَ فَلَاۤ اِلٰهَ اِلَّا اَنْتَ سُبْحَانَكَ مِنْ مُقْتَدِرٍ لَا يُغْلَبُ وَذِىْ اَنَاةٍ لَا يَعْجَلُ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَاٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَاجْعَلْنِىْ لِنَعْمَاۤئِكَ مِنَ الشَّاكِرِيْنَ*

(Dua e Joshane Sagheer - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

             *21st Zilqad 1441*

       *13th July 2020, Monday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ _*ALLAH MAALIK HAI.*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1476)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا یَحۡزُنكَ قَوۡلُهُمۡۘ إِنَّ ٱلۡعِزَّةَ لِلَّهِ جَمِیعًاۚ هُوَ ٱلسَّمِیعُ ٱلۡعَلِیمُ *  أَلَاۤ إِنَّ لِلَّهِ مَن فِی ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَمَن فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِۗ وَمَا یَتَّبِعُ ٱلَّذِینَ یَدۡعُونَ مِن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ شُرَكَاۤءَۚ إِن یَتَّبِعُونَ إِلَّا ٱلظَّنَّ وَإِنۡ هُمۡ إِلَّا یَخۡرُصُونَ.*

_"Aye Nabi (saww)! In logon ki baten Aap (saww) ko ranjeeda na karen. Izzat saari ki saari Allah ke ikhtiyar mein hai. Woh Sunnewala, Jannewala hai. Agah raho ke Aasmaano ke basne wale hon ya Zameen ke rehne wale hon, sab Allah ke mamlook (parja) hain. Aur jo log Khuda ko chhod kar (apne khud sakhta) Sharikon ko pukarte hain woh sirf is wahem o zan ki pairavi kar rahe hain aur woh mehez Qayas arai (guess) kar rahe hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 65 - 66)

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Is Ayat mein is Allah Apne Habib (saww) ko dilasa de raha ke Kuffar ki in baaton par ranjeeda na hon, ye to bhonkte hi rahenge. Inke bolne se Allah par koi farq nahi padta. Allah Malekul Mulk hai.

Isi tarah ki do Ayaat Qur'an mein aa chuki hain aur ham unki Tafseer bayan kar chuke hain. (Surah

 Ale Imran:176, Surah Maeda: 41)

Jahan Qur'an ki Ayaat Tauheed e Ilahi ka Zikr kar rahi hain, wahin hamare Aimma ne Dua ke zariye Tauheed e Ilahi ki hame taleem di hai. Malaheza farmayen:

🤲🏻

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Tu Khaaliq hai aur main makhlooq hun. Tu Maalik hai aur main mamlook hun. Tu Parwardigar hai aur main Tera Banda hun. Tu Raaziq hai aur main Rizq paane waala hun. Tu Ataa Karnewala hai aur main maangne wala hun. Tu Sakhawat Karnewala aur main kanjoos hun. Tu Quwwatwala aur main kamzor hun…"_

(Dua e Yastasheer)

🤲🏻

Imam Ali (as):

_"…Aye meri Ghulami ke Maalik! Aye Wo ke jiske haath mein meri Taqdeer hai. Aye mere Nuqsaan aur meri Miskeeni ki haalat Jannewale! Aye mere Rab! Aye mere Rab! Aye mere Rab!....."_

(Dua e Kumail)

🤲🏻

Imam Husain (as):

_"Aye mere Maalik! Aaya apne Kaan, ya apni Aankh, ya apni Zabaan, ya apne Haath , ya apne Paaon ke saath? Kya ye sab mere paas Teri Ne'mat nahi hai? Aur in sab ke saath maine Teri Nafarmani ki. Aye mere Maula! Pus Tere paas mere khilaaf hujjat aur daleel hai."_

(Dua e Arafa)

Isi tarah Dua e Abu Hamza aur doosre Duayen aur Ziyarat. Duaon ke tarjume padhe to apke Ilm mein izaafa hoga.

             *22nd Zilqad 1441*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        ♦ _*NEEND - SLEEP*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1477)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هُوَ ٱلَّذِی جَعَلَ لَكُمُ ٱلَّیۡلَ لِتَسۡكُنُوا۟ فِیهِ وَٱلنَّهَارَ مُبۡصِرًاۚ إِنَّ فِی ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لَـَٔایَـٰتࣲ لِّقَوۡمࣲ یَسۡمَعُونَ.*

_"Usne hi tumhare liye Raat banayi taake tum is mein Sukoon hasil kar sako aur Din ko Roshan banaya hai. Is mein logon ke liye Nishaniyan hain jo (Paighame Haq) sunte hain. "_

(Surah Yunus: 67)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Is Ayat mein us Raat ka zikr hai jis mein har shakhs Araam, sukoon pata hai. Qur'an mein in Ayat mein bhi isi baat ka zikr hai:

(Ale Imran: 96) (Qasas: 73) (Naml: 86) (Ghafir: 61)

Insaan Din bhar thak har kar Raat ko so jata hai aur araam mehsoos karta hai. Agar usko sahi Neend mili to agle Din phir mehnat ke liye tayyar/fresh ho jata hai. Agar kisi ko poori Neend na mile to woh Din bhar pareshan o bechain rehta hai aur kisi kaam mein uska man nahi lagta. Kuchh log tension ki wajah se so nahi pate, woh is Ne'mat ko khoya hua mehsoos karte hain. Waqae ye bhi Allah ki Ne'mat hai ke Usne Raat hamare Sukoon ke liye banayi. Yahan Allah ne ye nahi farmaya ke Raat sone ke liye banayi. Kyonki Raat mein Fitri taur par sirf sone se hi sukoon hasil nahi hota. Sona bhi araam ka ek zariya hai. Muttaqeen Raat ko Namaz-e-Shab padh kar bhi sukoon hasil karte hai. Kuchh Raat bhar Ilmi tehsil mein guzar dete hain aur sukoon hasil kar lete hain.

Kuchh log Raat ko Haraam kaam mein bhi waqt guzaar kar sukoon haasil karte hain. Kuchh bachche Raat bhar Games ya film dekhne mein Time Past kar dete hain jiski wajah se woh Din mein sote hain, ye un-natural hai, sehet ke liye bhi nuqsandeh hai. Jabke Shabbedari Ibaadat ke liye hai na ke fuzool kamon ke liye.

Raat ko taarik rakha taake Insaan so jaye, Din ko Roshan rakha taake Din mein Insaan apni Rozi talaash kare. Allah ne ye Duniya ka is tarah Nizam qayem kiya hai.

😴

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Neend Badan ki Raahat hai, guftagu Rooh ki Raahat hai aur Khamoshi Aql ki Raahat hai."_

(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p413)

😴

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"5 logo'n ko Neend nahi aati:_

_(1) Wo shakhs jisne kisi ka Khoon bahaya ho,_ (Qatil)

_(2) Wo shakhs jiske paas Maal bahut ho magar uske paas koi ameen (amanatdar) na ho,_ (Rich)

_(3) Wo shakhs jisne Maal e Duniya ke liye logo'n se Jhoot aur Fareb ki baaten ki ho'n,_  (Fraud)

_(4) Wo shakhs jis par logo'n ka Qarz bahut zyada ho magar uske paas kuchh Maal na ho,_ (Indebted)

_(5) Wo shakhs jo kisi se Mohabbat kare aur uski judaai mutawaqqe (expected) ho."_ (Lover)

(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p318)

😴

Neend ke bare mein mazeed Scientific maloomat is link mein padhen:

👉🏻

*Sleep* accounts for one-quarter to one-third of the human lifespan. But what exactly happens when you sleep?

*The Science of Sleep: Understanding What Happens When You Sleep:*

https://www.hopkinsmedicine.org/health/wellness-and-prevention/the-science-of-sleep-understanding-what-happens-when-you-sleep

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Raat ki taariki (darkness) mein padhi gayi 2 Rakat Namaz mujhe is Duniya se aur isme jo kuch hai, in sab se zyada pasand hai."_

(Salaatul Layl)

😴

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Jo shakhs Neend mein darta ho use chahiye ke sote waqt Mauzatain (Surah Falaq aur Surah Naas) aur Ayatul Kursi padhh le."_

Tehzeeb ul Islam, p186

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Jise neend na aati ho woh ye Dua padhe:_

*سُبحٰانَ اللّٰهِ دَائَمَ السُّلطَانِ كُلَّ يَومٍ هُوَ فِي الشَّان*

(Tehzibul Islam)

🤲🏻

*اَلْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ الَّذِىْ جَعَلَ اللَّيْلَ لِبَاسًا وَّالنَّوْمَ سُبًاتًا وَّ جَعَلَ النَّهَارَ نُشُوْرًا لَكَ*

(Wednesday Dua - Mafateeh)

♦ _*KHUDA KA BETA (SON OF GOD)*_ ♦

.

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1478)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالُوا۟ ٱتَّخَذَ ٱللَّهُ وَلَدࣰاۗ سُبۡحَـٰنَهُۥۖ هُوَ ٱلۡغَنِیُّۖ لَهُۥ مَا فِی ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَمَا فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِۚ إِنۡ عِندَكُم مِّن سُلۡطَـٰنِۭ بِهَـٰذَاۤۚ أَتَقُولُونَ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعۡلَمُونَ *  قُلۡ إِنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ یَفۡتَرُونَ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ ٱلۡكَذِبَ لَا یُفۡلِحُونَ.*

_"Unhone kaha ke Allah ne kisi ko beta banaya hai (Son of God) halanke woh isse Paak o Munazzah hai, Woh Be-Niyaz hai. Aasmaano aur Zameen ki tamam ashya Usi ki Milkiyat hai. Tumhare paas iski koi daleel nahi hai to kya tum Khuda ke mutalliq wo baaten kehte ho jiska tumhe Ilm nahi hai. Aap keh den ke woh log jo Allah par Jhoota Iftera bandhte hain (jhoota ilzam lagate hai) woh kabhi kamyab na honge."_

(Surah Yunus: 68 - 69)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Is Topic par Zikr ho chuka hai. Aur in Ayaat mein yehi Zikr repeat hua hai: (2:116), (Nisa:171), (Anaam:101), (Bani Israel: 111), (Kahf: 4), (Maryam: 35, 88), (Momenoon: 91), (Zumar: 4), (Surah Tauheed)

Same message dobara repeat kar rahe hain:

*وَقَالَتِ ٱلۡیَهُودُ عُزَیۡرٌ ٱبۡنُ ٱللَّهِ وَقَالَتِ ٱلنَّصَـٰرَى ٱلۡمَسِیحُ ٱبۡنُ ٱللَّهِۖ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ قَوۡلُهُم بِأَفۡوَ ٰ⁠هِهِمۡۖ یُضَـٰهِـُٔونَ قَوۡلَ ٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوا۟ مِن قَبۡلُۚ قَـٰتَلَهُمُ ٱللَّهُۖ أَنَّىٰ یُؤۡفَكُونَ*

_"Yahoodiyon (Jews) ne kaha ke Uzair Allah ka Beta hai aur Esai (Christian) kahte hain ke Maseeh Allah ka Farzand hai. Ye Sab be-Haqeeqat baaten hain jo woh apne Munh se nikal rahe hain. In baton mein ye unki misl hain jo unse pahle Kuffar kaha karte the. Un par Khuda ki Maar pade, ye kahan bahke chale jaa rahe hain."_

(Surah Taubah: 30)

Rasoole Khuda (saww) Jews ko jawab dene ke baad Christians se mukhatib hue:

_"Tumhara dawa hai ke Allah jo ke "Qadeem (Everlasting)" hai, Usne ek "Haadis (Created)" se ittehad (unity) kar liya hai. Is dawe se tumhari kya murad hai? Kya isse ye murad hai ke jab Qadeem ne Haadis se ittehad kiya to Woh Qadeem Apni Sifat e Qadamat se dastbardar hokar Haadis ban gaya ya basurat deegar Us Ittehad ki wajah se Qadeem ho gaya? Ya tumhare kahne ka matlab ye hai ke Allah ne use khusoosi Karamaat se sarfraz karte hue Apna Beta bana liya? Agar tum samajhte ho ke Qadeem Haadis ban gaya (Creator became Created) to ye mahaal (impossible) hai, isi tarah se Haadis ka Qadeem ban jana mahaal hai."_

Phir unhone bhi yehi kaha ke real mein nahi mazaji taur par kahte hain, to iska jawab wohi jo Yahoodiyon ko pahle de chuke hain.

Phir unhone kaha jaise Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko Khaleelullah kahte hain waise hi Hazrat Esa (as) ko Ibnullah.

Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

_"Tumne ghalat samjha. Ye sach hai Hazrat Ibrahim (as) Khaleelullah hain._

_1. Khullat yani Faqr o Faqa. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) sirf Allah se madad talab karte the. Yahan tak ke Jibrael (as) ki bhi madad nahi li jab Namrood ne unhe Aag mein dala. Makhlooq ki Beniyazi ki wajah se "Khaleelullah" kahlaye._

_2. Khaleel hone ki doosri wajah ye thi ke Hazrat Ibrahim (as) aise Asraar o Ma’arif (Secrets & Recognition) se aagah the jin se aur log waaqif nahi the._

_Hazrat Ibrahim (as) mein Khullat ke dono maani paye jaate hain lekin Khaleelullah aur Ibnullah mein kafi farq hai. Agar koi shakhs Raazon se waqif ho to Khaleel kahlayega, agar wohi shakhs gharz o ghayat doosron se karne lage aur Asraar o Ma'arif faramosh kar de to Lafz "Khaleel" salb ho jayega. Yani ye temporary Sifat hai jo lag bhi sakti hai aur juda bhi ho sakti hai. Jabke Farzand hona ye ek atoot Rishta hai. Beta apne Walid ka kitna hi nafarman kyon na ho khwah Walid ghar se nikal bhi de tab bhi woh uska beta hi kahlaya jayega._

_Agar Hazrat Esa (as) ke Mo'jezat ki wajah se kahte ho to Hazrat Musa (as) bhi Mo'jezat mein kam nahi the. To phir unko bhi Khuda ka Beta kaho!"_

Unhone kaha ke ye Aasmaani Kitabon mein likha hai.

Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

_"Ye Daleel khud tumhare Nazarye ko Baatil karne wali hai kyonki Hazrat Esa (as) ne tamam hazerin se kaha tha to ab tumhara kya khayal hai ke woh tamam hazerin bhi Khuda ke Farzand the? Aur agar bilfarz un sab ko farzand maan liya jaye to phir sawal uthega ke Maseeh to Allah ke khaas Bande the, Allah ne unhe apna farzand bana liya lekin us mehfil mein bhi Sahib e Mo'jezat afraad the jinhe khitab karke farmaya: "Mein apne aur tumhare Baap ke paas jaa raha hun?"_

_Asl baat ye hai ke tumne Maseeh ke qaul ka matlab nahi samjha. Is Jumle ka matlab ye ho sakta hai ke "Ab mein tumse juda ho raha hun, ab mein apne aur tumhare Baap Adam (as) wa Nooh (as) ki taraf jaa raha hun."_

AanHazrat (saww) ka ye jawab sun kar Christians khamosh ho gaye.

(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Hazrat Ali (as):

_"Jab Yahoodiyon ne Uzair (as) ko Allah ka Beta kaha to un par Khuda ko bahut Ghussa aaya aur jab Nasaara (Christians) ne Maseeh bin Maryam ko Allah ka Beta kaha to un par Allah ka sakht Azaab nazil hua aur Allah ka us par sakht Azaab nazil hoga jo mera Khoon bahayega aur mujhe meri Itrat ke mutalliq aziyyat dega."_

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*وَ الْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ الَّذِىْ لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ وَلَدًا وَ لَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ شَرِيْكٌ فِى الْمُلْكِ وَ لَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ وَلِىٌّ مِّنَ الذُّلِّ وَ كَبِّرْهُ تَكْبِيْرًا۔*

(Taqeebaat e Mushtarka ki ek Dua - Mafateeh)

♦ _*KAFIR AZAAB CHAKHENGE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1479)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَتَـٰعࣱ فِی ٱلدُّنۡیَا ثُمَّ إِلَیۡنَا مَرۡجِعُهُمۡ ثُمَّ نُذِیقُهُمُ ٱلۡعَذَابَ ٱلشَّدِیدَ بِمَا كَانُوا۟ یَكۡفُرُونَ.*

_"Duniya mein chand roza fayde hain. Phir Hamari taraf unko palatna hai. Phir is Kufr ke badle jiska woh irtekab (commit) kar rahe hain Ham unhe sakht Azaab ka maza chakhayenge."_

(Surah Yunus: 70)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Ayat ke maani bilkul wazeh hain. Guzishta Ayaton mein Kuffar o Munkarin ka zikr hua. Jab woh apni hatdharmi mein pade rahe to Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya to ab Azaab chakho. Gunehgar Azaab ko taste karenge. Taste jab hota hai jab hamari zabaan sahi mehsoos karti hai. Agar zaban senseless ho jaye to ham taste nahi kar payenge. Iska matlab ye hai ke har shakhs Azaab ko mehsoos karega, yani use wohi takleef ka ehsaas hoga jo woh is Duniya mein karta tha.

Duniya ki Zindagi to bahut chhoti hai. Yahan use Akherat ke liye Zaade raah mohayya karna hai. Ye to har Insaan apni Aankhon se dekhta hai ke Insaan is Duniya mein paida hota hai phir kuchh Din ke baad chala jata hai. Allah ki taraf se aata hai, phir palat kar Allah ki taraf jata hai. To phir kyon Insaan apne upar ghamand karta hai, akadta hai. Apne Khaliq ka Munkir hota hai. Akhirkar jana to Usi ke paas hai Jise woh chhod raha hai.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

_"Duniya mein reh kar Akherat ke liye Zaad e Raah jamaa karo aur behtareen Zaad e Raah Taqwa hai."_

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p620)

🌍

Imam Ali (as):

_"Duniya Momin ka Qaid-khana, Maut uska tohfa aur Jannat uski manzil hai. Duniya Kafiro'n ki Jannat hoti hai aur Maut use is (Jannat) se juda karnewali  aur Aag uski manzil hoti hai."_

(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)

🌍

Allah Ta'ala:

_"Duniya mein zyada aarzuein na banao, kyunki isse tera Dil sakht ho jayega aur jiska bhi Dil sakht ho jaata hai wo Mujh se door ho jata hai."_

(Al Kaafi, Ahaadis e Qudsi, Aastaan e Quds Razawi)

🤲🏻

*یَا اِلٰھِیْ وَ بِحَمْدِكَ تَسْمَعُ فِیْھَا صَوْتَ عَبْدٍ مُّسْلِمٍ سُجِنَ فِیْھَا بِمُخَالَفَتِہٖ وَ ذَاقَ طَعْمَ عَذَابِھَا بِمَعْصِیَتِہٖ وَ حُبِسَ بَیْنَ اَطْبَاقِھَا بِجُرْمِہٖ وَ جَرِیْرَتِہٖ وَ ھُوَ یَضِجُّ اِلَیْكَ ضَجِیْجَ مُؤَمِّلٍ لِرَحْمَتِكَ.*

_"Aye Qabil e Hamd o Sana Parwardigar! Kya ye mumkin hai ke Tu Banda e Musalman ko uski mukhalifat ki bena par Jahannum mein giraftar aur Ma'siyyat ki bena par Azaab ka maza chakhne wala aur Jurm o Khata ki bena par Jahannum ke Tabaqat ke darmiyan karwate badalne wala bana de aur phir ye dekhe ke woh Ummeedwar e Rehmat ki tarah pukarnewala hai."_

(Dua - e - Kumail)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ _*HAZRAT NOOH (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1480)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَٱتۡلُ عَلَیۡهِمۡ نَبَأَ نُوحٍ إِذۡ قَالَ لِقَوۡمِهِۦ یَـٰقَوۡمِ إِن كَانَ كَبُرَ عَلَیۡكُم مَّقَامِی وَتَذۡكِیرِی بِـَٔایَـٰتِ ٱللَّهِ فَعَلَى ٱللَّهِ تَوَكَّلۡتُ فَأَجۡمِعُوۤا۟ أَمۡرَكُمۡ وَشُرَكَاۤءَكُمۡ ثُمَّ لَا یَكُنۡ أَمۡرُكُمۡ عَلَیۡكُمۡ غُمَّةࣰ ثُمَّ ٱقۡضُوۤا۟ إِلَیَّ وَلَا تُنظِرُونِ *  فَإِن تَوَلَّیۡتُمۡ فَمَا سَأَلۡتُكُم مِّنۡ أَجۡرٍۖ إِنۡ أَجۡرِیَ إِلَّا عَلَى ٱللَّهِۖ وَأُمِرۡتُ أَنۡ أَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُسۡلِمِینَ.*

_"Unke saamne Nooh (as) ka Qissa bayan karo. Jab unhone apni Qaum se kaha tha ke aye meri Qaum! Mera tumhare darmiyan rehna aur Ayat e Ilahi ke zariye se tumhe Ghaflat se bedaar karna tumhare liye na-qabile bardasht ho chuka hai to meine Allah par Tawakkal (rely) kiya hai. Tum apna muttafeqa faisla kar lo aur apne Shariko ko bhi is mein shamil kar lo aur jo mansooba tumhare peshe nazar ho usko khoob soch samajh lo taake iska koi pehlu tumhari nigah se poshida na rahe. Phir mere khilaf amal mein le aao aur mujhe koi mohlat na do. Agar tumne mu'nh mod liya to meine tumse kaunsi Ujrat talab ki thi. Mera Ajr to sirf Allah ke zimme hai. Mujhe Hukm diya gaya hai ke mein farmanbardaron mein shamil rahun."_

(Surah Yunus: 71 - 72)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Yahan se Hazrat Nooh (as) ke qissa bayan ho raha hai. Hazrat Nooh (as) ka apni Qaum ko ye paigham tha ke woh usko Ghaflat se badaar karne ke liye bheje gaye hain, ab woh maane ya na maane unko isse koi farq nahi padta, woh Allah par bharosa karte hain. Balke unki Qaum ko challenge kiya ke woh apni poori taqat se jo karna chahe kar len, woh unka kuchh bhi nahi bigad sakte, kyonki inko Allah par Bharosa tha.

Yehi tamam Anbiya (as) ka mission bhi tha, jaisa ke Hazrat Ali (as) ne farmaya:

*فبعث فيهم رسله وواتر إليهم أنبياءه, ليستأدوهم ميثاق فطرته, ويذكروهم منسي نعمته. ويحتجوا عليهم بالتبليغ. ويثيروا لهم دفائن العقول.*

_"Unke darmiyan Anbiya wa Rasool bheje, taake unki Fitri Ahd ko poora karen, bhooli hui Ne'mato'n ka zikr kare, Tableegh se Hujjat tamam karen, unki madfoon Aqlon ko jhanjhod den."_

(Khutba Nahjul Balagha)

Anbiya (as) ki is Duniya mein aane ka maqsad yehi tha ke woh Insaan mein uski soyi hui Fitrat ko jagayen.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Imam Ali (as)

_"Rooh ki hayaat Ilm hai, Rooh ki Maut uski Jihaalat hai, Rooh ki Bimari shak hai, Rooh ki sehet Yaqeen hai, Rooh ki neend ghaflat hai, Rooh ki bedaari uski nigehbaani hai."_

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p373)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

_"Logo'n mein us shakhs ka Imaan zyada qawi (strong) hai jo Khuda par zyada tawakkul (bharosa) karta hai."_

(Gorar ul Hakam, v1, p115)

🕌

Imam Taqi (as):

_"Allah par bharosa har bulandi tak pahunchne ka zariya hai."_

(Tanzeemul Makatib, 38322)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

_"Allah par Tawakkul (bharosa) karo, Woh tumhari kifaalat karega."_

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p45)

🤲🏻

Imam Ali (as):

_"Aye mere Sardaar! Ab main Tujhe Teri izzat ka waasta de kar sawaal karta hun ke meri bad-amali aur bad-kirdaari, meri Dua ko Teri bargaah tak pahunchne se na roke. Aur Tu mujhe mere un poshida raazo'n ke sabab se jinse Tu waaqif hai, ruswa na karna. Aur main chhup chhup kar jo buraiyan aur bad-kaariyan kar chuka hun aur meri daymi kotaahi, meri Jihaalat, meri Khwaisho'n ki zyadati, meri Ghaflat ki wajah se mujhe saza dene mein jaldi na karna."_

(Dua e Kumail)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             *26th Zilqad 1441*

       *18th July 2020, Saturday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ _*SAFEENATUN NAJAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1481)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَكَذَّبُوهُ فَنَجَّیۡنَـٰهُ وَمَن مَّعَهُۥ فِی ٱلۡفُلۡكِ وَجَعَلۡنَـٰهُمۡ خَلَـٰۤىِٕفَ وَأَغۡرَقۡنَا ٱلَّذِینَ كَذَّبُوا۟ بِـَٔایَـٰتِنَاۖ فَٱنظُرۡ كَیۡفَ كَانَ عَـٰقِبَةُ ٱلۡمُنذَرِینَ.*

_"Qaum ne unki takzeeb (deny) ki, Hamne usko aur uske logon ko jo uske saath Kashti mein the Najaat di aur unhe Zameen Janasheen banaya aur un logon ko gharq kar diya jinhone Hamari Ayaat ko jhutlaya tha. Pas dekh lo ke jinhe mutanabba kiya gaya tha unka kiya anjam hua."_

(Surah Yunus: 73)

📚📖 ⛵

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Hazrat Nooh (as) ne apni Qaum mein 950 Saal Tableegh ki lekin kuchh log maane aur aksariyat ne takzeeb ki aur unko jhutlaya. Pas Hazrat Nooh (as) Allah se un par Azaab ki darkhwast ki. Lekin Allah Rehman o Rahim ne kaafi mohlat di. Pehle ek Darakht lagwaya, kuchh Saal mein wo bada hua, phir use kaatne ka Hukm hua. Usse Lakdiyan kaati gayi. Usse Kashti banane ka Hukm hua. Kashti dekh kar logon ne mazaq bhi udayi. Akhirkar Azaab ka Din aa gaya. Hazrat Nooh (as) ne apne Saathiyon, Chahnewalon ko Kashti mein sawaar karwaya. Yahan tak ke Janwaron ko bhi Kashti mein sawar kiya. Sabhi Imaanwale Kashti mein sawar hue aur Azaab se Najat payi. Ek bada Selaab (Flood) aya aur sabhi Dushman e Deen is mein gharq ho gaye aur sab halak ho gaye siwai Ahle Kashti wale. Isliye ise Safeena e Najaat kaha gaya. (Safeena = Boat)

Ahle Bait (as) bhi Safeena Najaat hain. Jo is Wilayat ki Kashti mein sawaar ho gaya Najaat paa gaya. Dushman e Ahle Bait (as) ko ye Safeena naseeb na hua.

Safeena e Najaat aaj bhi Samandar ki lehron mein Safar karti badhti chali jaa rahi hai. Aaj bhi Dushman e Ahle Bait ghairon ka daman pakde Pahado par chadhe chale jaa rahe hain lekin woh jahan bhi rahen ye Qudrati Azaab ki Maujen unhe chho leti hain aur unhe ghaseet kar apne mein gharq kar leti hain chahe woh kitne hi upar hon.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇 🚣

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Ya Ali (as)! Tumhari aur tumhari Aulaad ki misaal Safeena e Nooh (as) ki hai ke jo us Safeene par sawaar ho gaya Najaat pa gaya aur jo usse alag reh gaya woh halaak ho gaya aur phir tumhari misaal Aasmaan ke Sitaaro'n ki hai ke jab ek Sitara ghaayab hota hai to doosra tulu (rise) ho jata hai aur ye silsila Qayamat tak jaari rahega."_

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p168)

⛵

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Hazrat Nooh (as) ne apni Kashti mein Kutte aur Khinzeer (Pig /Suwwar) tak ko sawaar kiya, lekin Haraam-zaade ko na bithhaya. Aur Dushman e Ahlebait (as) to Haraam-zaade se badhkar hai."_

(Iqaabul Aamaal, p-455)

🤲🏻

*اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا سَفِيْنَةَ النَّجَاةِ*

(Ziyarat Roze Juma aur mutaddid Ziyarat mein yehi alfaaz hain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

**********************************

            *27th Zilqad 1441*

     *19th July 2020, Sunday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ _*ANBIYA (as) KI AAMAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1482)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ثُمَّ بَعَثۡنَا مِنۢ بَعۡدِهِۦ رُسُلًا إِلَىٰ قَوۡمِهِمۡ فَجَاۤءُوهُم بِٱلۡبَیِّنَـٰتِ فَمَا كَانُوا۟ لِیُؤۡمِنُوا۟ بِمَا كَذَّبُوا۟ بِهِۦ مِن قَبۡلُۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ نَطۡبَعُ عَلَىٰ قُلُوبِ ٱلۡمُعۡتَدِینَ.*

_"Phir Nooh (as) ke baad Hamne mukhtalif Paighambaron ko unki Qaumon ki taraf bheja. Woh unke paas khuli hui Nishaniyan le kar aaye magar jis cheez ko unhone pehle jhutla diya tha uski tasdeeq na kar sake. Is tarah se Ham hadd se tajawuz karne walon ke Dilon par Mohr laga dete hain."_

(Surah Yunus: 74)

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_

Guzishta Topic se paiwast hai.

Hazrat Nooh (as) aur unki Qaum ke baad bhi Anbiya (as) ka silsila jari raha. Toofan e H. Nooh (as) ke baad jo log bache the, jaise jaise arsa guzarta gaya, log phir gumrah hone lage, usi tarah jis tarah Qaum e Nooh (as) gumrah hui thi, agli Qaum bhi gumrah hui. Hazrat Hud (as) aaye aur unhone bhi apni Qaum mein Tableegh ki aur Ayah Bayyanah yani Mo'ajze bataye. Is tarah baqi Anbiya (as) ne Hidayat ka Silsila jari rakha.

Allah ne unki hatdharmi ki wajah se Unke Dilon par Mohr laga di.

Unke Dilon ka seal hona unhi ke Aamaal ki wajah se tha, ye Allah ki taraf se Jabr nahi hai. Woh log khud aise sakht Dil ho gaye ke un par Hidayat ka koi asar nahi hota. Jab Insaan sakht ho jata hai aap chahe kitna hi us par Dil nichhawar kar de, us par koi asar nahi hoga.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Allah Azz wa Jall ne 1,24,000 Nabi khalq kiye ke Allah ke nazdeek unme sabse zyada Saaheb e Ikraam main hun aur (mujhe) koi fakhr nahi aur Allah Azz wa Jall ne 1,24,000 Wasi khalq kiye ke unme Allah ke nazdeek Ali (as) sab se zyada Saaheb e Ikraam hai aur sab se Afzal bhi."_

(Khisaal, p427)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww):

_"Parwardigaar ne har Nabi aur Rasool ko kaamil Aql ke saath bheja aur use Ummat ke saare Saahibaan e Aql se Afzal qaraar diya."_

(Ijtehaad Ke Jalway, p67)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

_"Parwardigaar e Aalam ne kisi Nabi ko mab'oos nahi kiya magar sachchai aur amaanat-daari ke saath."_

(Adaab e Islami, v1, p327)

🤲🏻

*اِنِّىْ اُشْهِدُكَ وَ كَفٰى بِكَ شَهِيْدًا وَّ اُشْهِدُ جَمِيْعَ مَلَاۤئِكَتِكَ وَ سُكَّانَ سَمٰوَاتِكَ وَ حَمَلَةَ عَرْشِكَ وَ مَنْ بَعَثْتَ مِنْ اَنْبِيَاۤئِكَ وَ رُسُلِكَ وَ اَنْشَاْتَ مِنْ اَصْنَافِ خَلْقِكَ اَنِّىْ اَشْهَدُ اَنَّكَ اَنْتَ اللهُ لَاۤ اِلٰهَ اِلَّا اَنْتَ وَحْدَكَ لَا شَرِيْكَ لَكَ وَ لَا عَدِيْلَ وَ لَا خُلْفَ لِقَوْلِكَ وَ لَا تَبْدِيْلَ وَ اَنَّ مُحَمَّدً صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَ اٰلِهٖ عَبْدُكَ وَ رَسُوْلُكَ اَدّٰى مَا حَمَّلْتَهٗ اِلَى الْعِبَادِ وَجَاهَدَ فِىْ اللهِ عَزَّ وَ جَلَّ حَقَّ الْجِهَادِ وَ اَنَّهٗ بَشَّرَ بِمَا هُوَ حَقٌّ مِنَ الثَّوَابِ وَ اَنْذَرَ بِمَا هُوَ صِدْقٌ.*

(Dua e Roze Juma - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*

**********************************

            *27th Zilqad 1441*

     *19th July 2020, Sunday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ AALAM-E-ARWAAH KA IQRAAR ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1483)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ثُمَّ بَعَثۡنَا مِنۢ بَعۡدِهِۦ رُسُلًا إِلَىٰ قَوۡمِهِمۡ فَجَاۤءُوهُم بِٱلۡبَیِّنَـٰتِ فَمَا كَانُوا۟ لِیُؤۡمِنُوا۟ بِمَا كَذَّبُوا۟ بِهِۦ مِن قَبۡلُۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ نَطۡبَعُ عَلَىٰ قُلُوبِ ٱلۡمُعۡتَدِینَ.

"Phir Nooh (as) ke baad Hamne mukhtalif Paighambaron ko unki Qaumon ki taraf bheja. Woh unke paas khuli hui Nishaniyan le kar aaye *magar jis cheez ko unhone pehle jhutla diya tha uski tasdeeq na kar sake.* Is tarah se Ham hadd se tajawuz karne walon ke Dilon par Mohr laga dete hain."

(Surah Yunus: 74)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Guzishta message mein is Ayat ke zel mein Rasool ki amad ka zikr hua.

Is Ayat ki doosri Tafseer Imam ki zabani mulaheza ho.

👉🏻

Imam Baqir (as):

"Allah ne Apni Makhlooq ko paida kiya, Allah ne Apni pyari Makhlooq ko Teenat e Jannat se paida kiya aur Apni Na-pasandida Makhlooq ko Teenat e Dozakh se paida kiya. Phir unhe saye mein khada kiya."

Raavi ne Saaye ke bare mein sawal kiya to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Kya tumne kabhi dhoop mein apna saya nahi dekha jo ke kuchh bhi nahi hota. Phir Allah ne unki taraf Anbiya rawana kiye, unhone unko Khuda ki Tauheed ke iqraar ki dawat di. Logon ne iska iqraar kiya. Yahi wajah hai ke Tauheed ka iqraar Insaani Fitrat mein shamil hai. Allah Ta'ala ne Mushrekin o Kuffar ke mutalliq farmaya: ("Aur agar Aap unse poochhe ke unhe kisne paida kiya to woh jawab mein zaroor ye kahenge ke 'Allah' ne.") Phir Anbiya (as) ne unhe Anbiya ki Nabuwwat ke iqraar ki dawat di. Kuchh logon ne Aqeeda e Nabuwwat ka iqraar kiya. Phir Anbiya (as) ne unhe hamari Wilayat ke Aqeede ko qabool karne ki dawat di. Khuda ki pyari Makhlooq ne iska iqraar kiya aur Khuda ki  Na-pasandida Makhlooq ne iska inkaar kiya. Isi Masle ko Allah ne is Ayat mein is Alfaaz mein bayan kiya hai. فَمَا كَانُوا۟ لِیُؤۡمِنُوا۟ بِمَا كَذَّبُوا۟ بِهِ مِن قَبۡلُ"

(Usoole Kaafi, Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Aye Ali (as)! Main aur Aap dono ek Teenat (Mitti) se khalq kiye gaye hain. Aur jo Mitti us Mitti se bach gayi usse hamare Shiyo'n ko khalq kiya gaya hai aur jab Qayamat ka Din hoga to logo'n ko unki Maa ke naam se pukara jayega siwaye Aapke Shiyo'n ke. Pus unko unke Baap ke naam se pukara jayega, kyunki unki Wiladat paak hai."

(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p208)

🤲🏻

اَنَّ هٰذَا سَابِقٌ لَكُمْ فِيْمَا مَضٰى وَ جَارٍ لَكُمْ فِيْمَا بَقِيَ وَ اَنَّ اَرْوَاحَكُمْ وَ نُوْرَكُمْ وَ طِيْنَتَكُمْ وَاحِدَةٌ طَابَتْ وَ طَهُرَتْ بَعْضُهَا مِنْ بَعْضٍ خَلَقَكُمُ اللّٰهُ اَنْوَارًا....

(Ziyarat Jamiah Kabeerah - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
