              29th Zilqad 1441

      21st July 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ JADU v/s MO'JEZA ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1484)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ثُمَّ بَعَثۡنَا مِنۢ بَعۡدِهِم مُّوسَىٰ وَهَـٰرُونَ إِلَىٰ فِرۡعَوۡنَ وَمَلَإِی۟هِۦ بِـَٔایَـٰتِنَا فَٱسۡتَكۡبَرُوا۟ وَكَانُوا۟ قَوۡمࣰا مُّجۡرِمِینَ *  فَلَمَّا جَاۤءَهُمُ ٱلۡحَقُّ مِنۡ عِندِنَا قَالُوۤا۟ إِنَّ هَـٰذَا لَسِحۡرࣱ مُّبِینࣱ * قَالَ مُوسَىٰۤ أَتَقُولُونَ لِلۡحَقِّ لَمَّا جَاۤءَكُمۡۖ أَسِحۡرٌ هَـٰذَا وَلَا یُفۡلِحُ ٱلسَّـٰحِرُونَ *  قَالُوۤا۟ أَجِئۡتَنَا لِتَلۡفِتَنَا عَمَّا وَجَدۡنَا عَلَیۡهِ ءَابَاۤءَنَا وَتَكُونَ لَكُمَا ٱلۡكِبۡرِیَاۤءُ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَمَا نَحۡنُ لَكُمَا بِمُؤۡمِنِینَ *  وَقَالَ فِرۡعَوۡنُ ٱئۡتُونِی بِكُلِّ سَـٰحِرٍ عَلِیمࣲ *  فَلَمَّا جَاۤءَ ٱلسَّحَرَةُ قَالَ لَهُم مُّوسَىٰۤ أَلۡقُوا۟ مَاۤ أَنتُم مُّلۡقُونَ *  فَلَمَّاۤ أَلۡقَوۡا۟ قَالَ مُوسَىٰ مَا جِئۡتُم بِهِ ٱلسِّحۡرُۖ إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ سَیُبۡطِلُهُۥۤ إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَا یُصۡلِحُ عَمَلَ ٱلۡمُفۡسِدِینَ *  وَیُحِقُّ ٱللَّهُ ٱلۡحَقَّ بِكَلِمَـٰتِهِۦ وَلَوۡ كَرِهَ ٱلۡمُجۡرِمُونَ

"Phir Hamne in Rasoolon ke baad Firaun aur uske Sardaron ki taraf Musa (as) o Haroon (as) ko Apni Nishaniyan de kar bheja magar unhone apni badai ka ghamand kiya, woh Mujrim log the.

Pas jab unke paas Hamari taraf se Haq pahunch gaya to unhone kaha ke ye to zahir ba zahir Jadu hai.

Musa (as) ne kaha tum Haq ko ye kehte ho jabke wo tumhare paas aa gaya? Kya ye Jadu hai? Jabke Jadugar kabhi kamyabi hasil nahi karte.

Unhone (jawab mein) kaha ke kya tu hamare paas isliye aaya hai ke hame us Raaste se pher de jis par hamne apne Baap Dada ko paya hai aur Zameen mein tum dono ki badayi qaem ho jaye? (Sun lo) ham tum dono par Imaan laane wale nahi hain. Aur Firaun ne (apne Darbariyon se) kaha tum har mahir e fan Jadugar ko mere paas le aao.

Phir jab Jadugar aa gaye to Musa (as) ne unse kaha jo tumhe phenkna hai phenko. Jab unhone Rassiyon ko phenka to Musa (as) ne kaha: 'Tumne jo kuchh pesh kiya hai ye Jadu hai, Allah abhi ise Baatil kar dega. Allah Mufsedeen ke kamon ko banne nahi deta. Aur Allah Apne Kalemat ke zariye se Haq ko Haq sabit kar dekhata hai chahe Mujrimon ko kitna hi nagawar kyon na ho."

(Surah Yunus: 75 - 82)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

In Ayaat mein Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Musa (as) aur Firaun ke Darbar mein Jadugaron ka waqea bayan kiya hai.

Ye waqea (Surah A'raf: 105 - 131) ke zel mein tafseel se zikr kiya jaa chuka hai. (20/6/2019).

In Ayat mein Jadu aur Mo'ajze mein farq ki wazahat ki hai.

Jadu kuchh practice ka natija hota hai. Jadu ka maqsad sirf chamatkar dikhana hota hai. Jadu Insaan ki Ankhon ka dhoka hai, Haqeeqat nahi. Ye sirf entertainment ke liye hota hai. Amaliyat Jadu mein shumar nahi hote.

Jabke Mo'ajza Nabi ya Imam Khuda ki ata kardah Qudrat se baja lata hai, baghair koi practice ke. Iska maqsad sirf logon ko Allah ki taraf Hidayat hoti hai. Mo'ajza Haq hai, jabke Jadu jhoot hai. Hazrat Musa (as) ka Firaun ke Darbar mein Jadu aur Mo'ajze ka muqabila tha, jiske natije mein Jadugar sajdah rez ho gaye.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Insaan ko chahiye ke apne aapko doosre Gunahgar se afzal na samjhe kyunki ain mumkin hai ke jise woh Gunahgar samajh kar giri hui nazro'n se dekh raha hai uske Gunah Ma'af ho chuke ho'n aur ye hisaab mein mubtela ho. Kya tu ne (Firoun ke) jaadugaro'n ka qissa nahi padha ke woh kitne bade Gunahgar the aur kis tarah se woh achanak Naaji (Nijaat paaye hue) ban gaye."

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p426)

🤲🏻

"Aye Apni Gunehgar Makhlooqaat par jaldi Azaab na karne wale aur Hazrat Musa (as) ke muqabile mein aanewale Jadugaron ko Azaab se Bachanewale......"

(Dua - Mafateeh)

   ♦ TAWAKKUL - BHAROSA ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1485)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَمَاۤ ءَامَنَ لِمُوسَىٰۤ إِلَّا ذُرِّیَّةࣱ مِّن قَوۡمِهِۦ عَلَىٰ خَوۡفࣲ مِّن فِرۡعَوۡنَ وَمَلَإِی۟هِمۡ أَن یَفۡتِنَهُمۡۚ وَإِنَّ فِرۡعَوۡنَ لَعَالࣲ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَإِنَّهُۥ لَمِنَ ٱلۡمُسۡرِفِینَ *  وَقَالَ مُوسَىٰ یَـٰقَوۡمِ إِن كُنتُمۡ ءَامَنتُم بِٱللَّهِ فَعَلَیۡهِ تَوَكَّلُوۤا۟ إِن كُنتُم مُّسۡلِمِینَ *  فَقَالُوا۟ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ تَوَكَّلۡنَا رَبَّنَا لَا تَجۡعَلۡنَا فِتۡنَةࣰ لِّلۡقَوۡمِ ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ.

"Phir bhi Musa (as) par Imaan nahi laye magar unki Qaum ki ek Nasl aur unhe bhi Firaun aur uske Sardaron ki taraf se ye dhadka tha ke woh kahin unhe azmayish mein na dal de. Yaqeenan Firaun Zameen mein ghalba rakhta tha aur woh hadd se tajawuz karnewalon mein se tha.

Musa (as) ne apni Qaum se kaha: 'Aye meri Qaum! Agar tum Allah par Imaan la chuke ho to Usi par bharosa karo, agar tum waqean Uske Farmabardar ho.' Unhone ne kaha: 'Hamne Khuda par Bharosa kiya. Aye hamare Rab! Hame Zalim logon ke liye Fitna na banana aur Apni Rehmat se hamen Kafiron se Najaat dena."

(Surah Yunus: 83 - 85)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Silsila e Zikre Hazrat Musa (as) jari hai:

👉🏻

Imam Baqir (as) ne Ayat (10:84-85) ke zel mein farmaya:

"Qaum e Musa (as) ko Aale Firaun ne apna Ghulam bana liya tha aur woh kehte the ke agar Khuda ko unse zarra barabar bhi Mohabbat hoti to ham un par kabhi bhi ghalib na aate.'

Isliye Hazrat Musa (as) ne apni Qaum se farmaya tha ke 'agar tum Haqeeqi Muslim ban chuke ho to kisi ki baaten sunne ki zaroorat nahi hai. Tum apne Rab par Bharosa rakho. Wohi tumhe Kamyabi dega.' Un logon ne jawab mein kaha tha ke 'hamne apne Rab par Bharosa kiya hai aur unhone Khuda se ye Dua ki thi ke Zalimon ko ham par musallat na karna aur hame unke Fitne mein na karna."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Tafseer Ayyashi, Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Allah par Tawakkul (bharosa) karo, Woh tumhari kifaalat karega."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p45)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Jo Duniya par bharosa kar ke mutmaeen ho jata hai, Duniya use daga de jati hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p371)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Agar tum Allah par Tawakkul (bharosa) karte to tumhe aise Rozi deta jaise parindo ko deta hai, Subah khaali Pet hote hain aur shaam ko Pet bhara hota hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4)

🕌

Imam Taqi (as):

"Allah par Bharosa har bulandi tak pahunchne ka zariya hai."

(Tanzeemul Makatib, 38322)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Allah par Bharosa rakhne wale Ghareeb ki khuddari, kisi maaldaar ki zaruratmand ko ki hui khairaat se behtar hai."

(Islamic Morals)

🤲🏻

Imam Ali (as):

یَا سَیِّدِیْ یَا مَنْ عَلَیْہِ مُعَوَّلِیْ یَا مَنْ اِلَیْہِ شَكَوْتُ اَحْوَالِیْ....

"Aye mere Sardaar! Aye Wo ke jis par mera bharosa hai. Aye Wo ki jiski bargaah mein main apni har haalat ki shikayat karta hun."

(Dua e Kumail)

♦ HADIYANE ILAHI KA GHAR QIBLA HAI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1486)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَنَجِّنَا بِرَحۡمَتِكَ مِنَ ٱلۡقَوۡمِ ٱلۡكَـٰفِرِینَ * وَأَوۡحَیۡنَاۤ إِلَىٰ مُوسَىٰ وَأَخِیهِ أَن تَبَوَّءَا لِقَوۡمِكُمَا بِمِصۡرَ بُیُوتࣰا وَٱجۡعَلُوا۟ بُیُوتَكُمۡ قِبۡلَةࣰ وَأَقِیمُوا۟ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَۗ وَبَشِّرِ ٱلۡمُؤۡمِنِینَ.

"Aur Hamne Musa (as) aur uske bhai ki taraf Wahy ki ke Misr mein  kuchh Makaan apni Qaum ke liye mohayya karo aur apne Gharon ko Qibla bana lo aur Namaz qaem karo aur Ahle Imaan ko Bashaarat de do."

(Surah Yunus: 86 - 87)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

"Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Masjid mein apna aur Ali (as) ka Darwaza khula rehne diya tha aur baqi logon ke darwaze band karwa diye the to us waqt Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

"Aye logon! Allah ne Musa (as) wa Haroon (as) ko Hukm diya tha ke woh Misr mein apni Qaum ke liye kuchh Ghar banayen aur unhe ye Hukm diya tha ke unki Masjid mein koi Junub Shab basari (Night sleep) na kare aur Masjid mein Biwiyon se maqarebat (sex) na ki jaye magar Haroon (as) aur uski Aulad isse mustasna (exception) hai. Ali (as) ko mujh se wohi Manzelat hasil hai jo Haroon (as) ko Musa (as) se hasil thi. Kisi ke liye bhi haalat e Janabat mein Masjid mein Shab basari jaez nahi hai aur kisi ko Biwiyon se Masjid mein maqarebat ka haq hasil nahi hai albatta Ali (as) aur uski Aulad is Hukm se mustasna (exception) hai. Jise ye baat nagawar ho to phir woh udhar chala jaye." ye keh kar Aap (saww) ne apne haath se Shaam (Syria) ki taraf ishara kiya."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Reza (as):

"Ummat aur Itrat mein 12 farq hain.

Chautha Farq ye hai ke Rasoolullah (saww) ne Ummat ke Darwaze jo Masjid mein khulte the sab band karwa diye the magar Itrat ka Darwaza khula rehne diya tha. Logon ne is par bahut etraz bhi kiye the hatta ke Abbas bin Abdul Muttalib ne bhi Rasoole Khuda (saww) se ye arz kiya tha: "Ya Rasoolullah! Aapne Ali (as) ko to rehne diya aur hame bahar kar diya!!"

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya tha: "Maine ise yahan apni marzi se chhoda nahi hai aur tumhe apni marzi se nikala nahi hai. Allah ne Uske Darwaze ko rehne diya aur Usi ne hi tumhare Darwaze band kar diye hain." AanHazrat (saww) ne aisa karke Duniya ko ye bataya tha ke mein Misaal e Musa (as) hun aur Ali (as) Misaale Haroon (as) hain."

"Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne etraz karnewalo se farmaya tha:" Yaad rakho, ye Masjid hai Muhammad wa Aale Muhammad (saww) ke alawa kisi Junub ke liye ye Halaal nahi hai."

"Allah Ta'ala ne Musa o Haroon (as) ke Gharon ka ishaara karte hue farmaya hai:" Tum apne Gharon ko Qibla bana lo (10:87)."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Agar Allah chahta to bando'n ko khud hi Apni Ma'arefat ata kar deta. Lekin Usne humen Apna Darwaza, Apni Siraat aur Apni Sabeel qaraar diya hai aur wo wajah muqarrar kar di jis se Us tak pahunch sakte hain. Pus, jo log hamari Wilayat se mu'nh mod le'n ya hum par kisi doosre ko fazilat den, unhi ko Allah ne farmaya hai ke, 'Wo raah e raast se hat jaane wale hain'.

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p101)

🤲🏻

..وَ اَحَلَّ لَهٗ مِنْ مَسْجِدِهٖ مَا حَلَّ لَهٗ وَ سَدَّ الْاَبْوَابَ اِلَّا بَابَهٗ ثُمَّ اَوْدَعَهٗ عِلْمَهٗ وَ حِكْمَتَهٗ فَقَالَ اَنَا مَدِیْنَۃُ الْعِلْمِ وَ عَلِیٌّ بَابُھَا فَمَنْ اَرَادَ الْمَدِیْنَۃَ وَ الْحِكْمَۃَ فَلْیَاْتِھَا مِنْ بَابِھَا....

(Dua-e-Nudba)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               3rd Zilhajj 1441

      25th July 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ HAZRAT MUSA (as) KI BAD-DUA ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1487)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ مُوسَىٰ رَبَّنَاۤ إِنَّكَ ءَاتَیۡتَ فِرۡعَوۡنَ وَمَلَأَهُۥ زِینَةࣰ وَأَمۡوَ ٰ⁠لࣰا فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا رَبَّنَا لِیُضِلُّوا۟ عَن سَبِیلِكَۖ رَبَّنَا ٱطۡمِسۡ عَلَىٰۤ أَمۡوَ ٰ⁠لِهِمۡ وَٱشۡدُدۡ عَلَىٰ قُلُوبِهِمۡ فَلَا یُؤۡمِنُوا۟ حَتَّىٰ یَرَوُا۟ ٱلۡعَذَابَ ٱلۡأَلِیمَ *  قَالَ قَدۡ أُجِیبَت دَّعۡوَتُكُمَا فَٱسۡتَقِیمَا وَلَا تَتَّبِعَاۤنِّ سَبِیلَ ٱلَّذِینَ لَا یَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Aur Musa (as) ne kaha ke aye hamare Parwardigar! Tu ne Firaun aur uske Sardaron ko Duniyavi Zindagi mein Zeenat aur Amwaal de rakha hai. Aye Rab! Kya ye isliye hai ke woh logon ko Teri Rah se bhatkayen? Aye Rab unke Amwaal barbaad kar de aur unke Dilon par aisi sakht Mohr laga de ke ye Imaan na laane payen jab tak Dardnak Azaab na dekh len."

"Allah ne kaha ke tum dono ki Dua maqbool hui, tum dono apne Raaste par qaem raho aur un logon ke raaste ki hargiz pairavi na karna jo Ilm nahi rakhte."

(Surah Yunus: 88 - 89)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Silsila Tazkara e Hazrat Musa (as) jari hai.

👉🏻

Hazrat Musa (as) ne apni Bad-Dua mein Firaun aur unke Sardaron ki Daulat ka tazkara kiya. Daulat kabhi bhi Insaan gumrah kar sakti hai aur Imaan se door rakhti hai. Insaan fitri taur par Daulat ki taraf khichta hai. Yehi Daulat Insaan ko barbaad kar deti hai.

Akhirkar Hazrat Musa (as) ne Firaun aur uske hamnawaon ke liye Bad-Dua ki. Firaun par Economic attack hua. (Iqtesaadi mar padi) Economic Recession Insaan ko halakat ki taraf le jata hai. Unke Dilon par Khuda ki Mohr lag jati hai, tab Insaan Imaan kya cheez hai, nahi samajh pata. Pas Imaan ka hona bhi ek Ilahi Ne'mat hai. Ye ata e Khuda wandi hai. Ye Bakhshis use ata hoti hai jo ise qubool kare. (isliye ye Jabr nahi hai)

Jab ek Nabi Bad-Dua kare to Khuda zaroor qubool karega aur phir Firaun aur uske Lashkar par Azaab nazil hota hai jiska tazkara agli Ayat mein hoga.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Duniya Daulat se haasil ki jaati hai aur Akherat Amal se."

(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)

🌎

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Allah Ta'ala Dost aur Dushman sab ko Daulat aur Duniya ata karta hai lekin Imaan sirf Apne Dost ko ata karta hai."

(Mishkaat ul Anwaar (Urdu), p80)

🤲🏻

وَ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ كَمَا رَحِمْتَ بِهِ الْعِبَادَ وَ اَحْيَيْتَ بِهِ الْبِلَادَ وَ قَصَمْتَ بِهِ الْجَبَابِرَةَ وَ اَهْلَكْتَ بِهِ الْفَرَاعِنَةَ.......

"Aur Rehmat nazil farma Hazrat Muhammad (saww) par. Jis tarah Tu ne inke zariye Bando par Rahem kiya aur Shehron ko zinda kiya aur Jabiron ki kamar tod di aur Firaunon ko halaak kar diya....."

(Salwat e Masoomeen (as) Amaal baroz Juma  - Mafateeh)

♦ HAALATE NAZA' MAIN IMAAN LAANA BEKAAR HAI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1488)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَجَـٰوَزۡنَا بِبَنِیۤ إِسۡرَ ٰ⁠ۤءِیلَ ٱلۡبَحۡرَ فَأَتۡبَعَهُمۡ فِرۡعَوۡنُ وَجُنُودُهُۥ بَغۡیࣰا وَعَدۡوًاۖ حَتَّىٰۤ إِذَاۤ أَدۡرَكَهُ ٱلۡغَرَقُ قَالَ ءَامَنتُ أَنَّهُۥ لَاۤ إِلَـٰهَ إِلَّا ٱلَّذِیۤ ءَامَنَتۡ بِهِۦ بَنُوۤا۟ إِسۡرَ ٰ⁠ۤءِیلَ وَأَنَا۠ مِنَ ٱلۡمُسۡلِمِینَ.

"Aur Hamne Bani Israel ko Samandar paar kara diya. Firaun aur uske Lashkar ne Zulm o ziyadti ki gharz se unka unka taqqub (follow) kiya hatta ke jab woh doobne laga to kehne laga. 'Mein Imaan laata hun us Khuda par jis par Bani Israel Imaam laye hain, Uske siwa koi Ma'bood nahi hai, aur mein bhi Ita'at Guzaron mein se hun."

(Surah Yunus: 90)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Silsila e tazkara Hazrat Musa (as) jari hai.

👉🏻

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

"Bani Israel ne Hazrat Musa (as) se arz kya ke Khudara hame yahan se nikal le jayen aur Firaun ke zulm se najaat payen. Hazrat Musa (as) ne Allah se Dua maangi tab Khuda ne farmaya: Tum apni Qaum ko yahan se le jao. Samandar ko Hukm dunga ke tumhari ita'at karte hue tumhe raasta de dega. Chunanche Hazrat Musa (as) apni Qaum ko saath le kar Firaun ke shaher se guzre. Kuchh der baad Firaun ko maloom hua to usne apni afwaaj ko saath liya aur unko follow kiya. Ab ek taraf Firaun aur uska Lashkar tha doosri taraf Samandar tha. Allah ke Hukm se Hazrat Musa (as) ne Samandar mein Asa mara, Samandar phat gaya, aur woh apni Qaum ko le kar chal pade. Firaun ko ye dekh kar tajjub hua. Pichhe pichhe Firaun aur uska Lashkar bhi cross karne laga. Udhar jaise hi Hazrat Musa (as) Samandar se bahar nikle Samandar phir apas mein mil gaya aur Firaun aur uska lashkar doob gaya. Doobte waqt Firaun ne Imaan laane ki duhai machai." (Khulasa)

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

🌊

Imam Reza (as) se sawal hua ke Firaun ko gharq kyon kiya jabke woh Imaan la chuka tha?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Woh Naza' ke waqt ( نزع - At Death bed) Imaan laya tha aur haalate Naza' ka Imaan qabile qubool nahi hota. (kyonki us waqt marne walon ki Aankhon se Hijaab hat jate hain aur Aalam e Akherat ko apni Aankhon se dekh raha hota hai.) Allah Ta'ala ne Apne Usool ko bayan karte hue farmaya: "Jab unhone Hamare Azaab ko dekha to kehne lage ham Khuda e Wahid par Imaan la rahe hain aur isse pehle ham jo shirk karte the Uska inkaar kar rahe hain. Unke is Imaan ne unhe koi fayda na diya jise woh Hamare Azaab dekhne ke baad laye the. (Ghafir: 84-85)"

"Allah ne Apni isi Ravish ko yun bayan kiya, 'To uska Imaan lana use koi fayda na dega (An' am: 158)"

(Surah Nisa: 18 mein bhi)

"Is tarah Firaun bhi us waqt Imaan laya tha jab woh Khuda ke Azaab mein giraftar ho chuka tha. Chunanche jab usne Khuda e Wahid par Imaan laane ke Kalemat kahe to jawab mein ye kaha gaya (10:91)"

(Kitab Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"…Adl (Justice) Kufr ke saath baaqi reh sakta hai lekin Jor o Zulm Imaan ke saath baaqi nahi reh sakta."

(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p212)

🤲🏻

وَ جَاوَزْتَ بِبَنِىْ اِسْرَاۤئِيْلَ الْبَحْرَ وَ تَمَّتْ كَلِمَتُكَ الْحُسْنىٰ عَلَيْهِمْ بِمَا صَبَرُوْا وَ اَوْرَثْتَهُمْ مَشَارِقَ الْاَرْضِ وَ مَغَارِبِهَا الَّتِىْ بَارَكْتَ فِيْهَا لِلْعَالَمِيْنَ وَ اَغْرَقْتَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَ جُنُوْدَهُ وَ مَرَاكِبَهُ فِيْ الْيَمِّ.....

(Dua e Simaat - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      27th July 2020, Monday

♦ GHARQE FIRAUN EK IBRAT HAI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1489)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ءَاۤلۡـَٔـٰنَ وَقَدۡ عَصَیۡتَ قَبۡلُ وَكُنتَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُفۡسِدِینَ * فَٱلۡیَوۡمَ نُنَجِّیكَ بِبَدَنِكَ لِتَكُونَ لِمَنۡ خَلۡفَكَ ءَایَةࣰۚ وَإِنَّ كَثِیرࣰا مِّنَ ٱلنَّاسِ عَنۡ ءَایَـٰتِنَا لَغَـٰفِلُونَ

"(Allah ne Firaun ko Jawab diya) Ab Imaan lata hai! Jabke isse qabl tu ne Nafarmani ki hai aur tu Fasaad karnewalon mein se tha. Pas aaj ke Din Ham tere badan ko najaat denge taake tu baad walon ke liye (Ibrat ki) Nishani ban jaye. Yaqeenan logon ki aksariyat Hamari Ayaat se ghafil hai."

(Surah Yunus: 91 - 92)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Silsila Tazkara e Hazrat Musa (as) jaari hai:

🌊

(Riwayat Cont'd....)

Imam Baqir (as):

"Jab Firaun doobne laga aur usne apna Imaan jataya to Allah ne is tarah Jawab diya (Ayat 10:91)"

"Lashkare Firaun jaise hi dooba to Malaika ne un sabke Ajsaam (bodies) ko Dozakh mein dal diya. Sirf Firaun ki Laash sahil par payi gayi taake har shakhs uski Laash ko dekh kar uski halakat ka yaqeen hasil kare aur uske anjaam se Ibrat pakde."

"Firaun jo kal tak Rubiyyat ka dawedar tha woh ek Murdaar ki surat mein Samandar ki sahil par pada hua tha. Firaun ki Laash Insaano ke Ibrat hai, lekin Ibrat hasil karne wale log bahut kam hain."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

For Latest info read:

Preservation of  Pharaoh's Body:

https://jacktheladhub.wordpress.com/2015/08/18/preservation-of-pharaohs-body/

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Momin Duniya ko Ibrat (lesson) ki nigaah se dekhta hai aur utni hi giza haasil karta hai jiske liye shikam ki zarurat usay majboor karti hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p53)

🤲🏻

یَا مَنْ فَلَقَ الْبَحْرَ لِبَنِىْۤ اِسْرَاۤئِیْ لَ فَاَنْجَاهُمْ وَجَعَلَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَجُنُوْدَهُ مِنَ الْمُغْرَقِیْنَ

(Dua e Imamd Husain (as) Roze Arafa. - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     28th July 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ BANI ISRAEL PAR ILAHI NAWAZISH ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1490)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَقَدۡ بَوَّأۡنَا بَنِیۤ إِسۡرَ ٰ⁠ۤءِیلَ مُبَوَّأَ صِدۡقࣲ وَرَزَقۡنَـٰهُم مِّنَ ٱلطَّیِّبَـٰتِ فَمَا ٱخۡتَلَفُوا۟ حَتَّىٰ جَاۤءَهُمُ ٱلۡعِلۡمُۚ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ یَقۡضِی بَیۡنَهُمۡ یَوۡمَ ٱلۡقِیَـٰمَةِ فِیمَا كَانُوا۟ فِیهِ یَخۡتَلِفُونَ.

"Hamne Bani Israel ko bahut achha thikana diya aur Hamne unhe Pakeeza Rizq ata kiya, phir unhone apas mein ikhtilaf nahi kiya. Magar us waqt jab unke paas Ilm aa chuka tha. Yaqeenan tera Rab Qayamat ke Din unke darmiyan us cheez ka Faisla karega jis mein woh ikhtelaf karte hain."

(Surah Yunus: 93)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Silsila e Tazkara Hazrat Musa (as) ka akhira hissa pesh e khidmat hai.

Bani Israel ne khwahish ki thi ke unhe Firaun ke Zulm se nijaat mile. Isliye unhone Hazrat Musa (as) ka daman thama aur Allah ne unhe nijaat di. Firaun aur uske Lashkar ka khatma hua. Aur Allah ne Bani Israel ko ek achhe thikane ( *مُبَوَّأَ صِدۡقࣲ*) par pahunchaya aur bahut si Ne'mato'n se bhi nawaza. Bani Israel Egypt, Syria, Palestine mein abaad hue jahan bahut se Anbiya ka jaye maqam hai.

Quran mein in Ayaat mein bhi iska tazkara kiya gaya hai:

"Firauniyon ki naboodi ki baad Baugh, Chashme (Well), Zameenen, Mahallat aur unki jo Ne'maten reh gayi thi, Hamne doosre giroh (Bani Israel) ko de din." (Dukhan: 25-28)

"Hamne ye Baugh, Chashme, Khazane aur Mahel Bani Israel ko de diye." (Shu'ara: 57-59)

Unko Pakeeza khaane bhi mohayya kiya.

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Yahoodiyon ko ye sab yad dahani karayi lekin phir kuchh Rasoole Khuda (saww) par Imaan laye lekin aksariyat ne Aap (saww) se ikhtelaf kiya. Sab kuchh jaanne ke baad bhi ikhtelaf kiya to Allah hi unka Qayamat ke Din Faisla karega

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Hazrat Dawood (as):

"Aye Bani Israel! Apne shikam mein Pakeeza Ghiza daakhil karo to tumhari Zabaan se Pakeeza baaten niklegi."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p109)

🤲🏻

وَعَدْتَهٗ اَنْ تُظْھِرَ دِیْنَهٗ عَلَی الدِّیْنِ كُلِّهٖ وَ لَوْكَرِهَ الْمُشْرِكُوْنَ وَ ذٰلِكَ بَعْدَ اَنْ بَوَّئْتَهٗ مُبْوَّءَصِدْقٍ مِنْ اَھْلِهٖ وَ جَعَلْتَ لَهٗ وَ لَھُمْ اَوَّلَ بَیْتٍ....

"Aur Tu ne unse Waada kiya ke unke Deen ko tamam Adyaan par ghalib banayega chahe Mushrikon ko kitna nagawar guzre aur *ye sab us waqt hua jab Tu ne inhe Sadaqat ke Markaz par mustaqir kar diya* aur unke liye aur unke Ahl ke liye is Pehle Ghar ko qarar diya..."

(Dua-e-Nudba)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             7th Zilhajj 1441

  29th July 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ WAHY-E-ILAHI MEIN SHAK ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1491)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَإِن كُنتَ فِی شَكࣲّ مِّمَّاۤ أَنزَلۡنَاۤ إِلَیۡكَ فَسۡـَٔلِ ٱلَّذِینَ یَقۡرَءُونَ ٱلۡكِتَـٰبَ مِن قَبۡلِكَۚ لَقَدۡ جَاۤءَكَ ٱلۡحَقُّ مِن رَّبِّكَ فَلَا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ ٱلۡمُمۡتَرِینَ.

"Ab tujhe is mein Shak hai jise Hamne Aap ki taraf nazil kiya hai to Aap un logon se poochhen jo Aap (saww) se pehle Kitab padh rahe hain. Yaqeenan Aapke Rab ki taraf se Aapke paas Haq aa chuka hai. Shak karnewalon mein se hargiz na hona."

(Surah Yunus: 94)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Mohd Taqi (as) se is Ayat ke bare mein sawal kiya gaya ke Allah Nabi (saww) se khitab kar raha hai, kya Nabi shak kar sakta hai?

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Is Ayat ka Khitab Nabi Akram (saww) se hi hai jabke ye bhi ek haqeeqat hai ke Nabi Akram (saww) ko Wahy e Ilahi mein koi Shak bhi nahi tha. Asl baat ye hai ke Jahil logon ne apni Jihalat se ye kaha tha ke agar Allah ne Apna Paigam hamare paas rawana karna hi tha to Usne kisi Farishte ko Rasool bana kar hamare paas kyon na bheja? Jabke ye Rasool hamari tarah se khata peeta hai aur Bazaron mein chalta phirta hai.

Allah Ta'ala ne Aapki taraf Wahy ki tumhe unke is sawal se pareshan hone ki zaroorat nahi hai. Aap (saww) un Ahle Kitab se poochhen Pichhle Anbiya bhi khaate peete the aur Bazaron mein bhi jate the.

Nabi ko Wahy e Ilahi mein Shak nahi tha. Baat ye hai ke kabhi bar sabeel e tanazzul aapne apko aam logon ke level par bhi lana padta hai jaise ke Mubahila ki Ayat mein. Agar Ayat is tarah hoti 'Aao Mubahila kare aur tum par La'anat karen.' to koi bhi Christian Mubahila qabool nahi karta. Khuda ko bhi maloom tha ke mera Rasool sachcha hai lekin is tarah se Sadaqat ko zyada wazeh karna tha." (Apne aap ko saamne wale ke level par laake saabit karna.)

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab AanHazrat (saww) ko Meraj hui aur Shabe Meraj ki guftugu mein Allah ne Ali Ibne Abi Talib (as) ki bahut si Fazilaten bayan farmayi. Aap (saww) jab Zameen ki taraf aane lage to Baitul Ma'moor par Allah ne tamam Anbiya ko jama kiya aur AanHazrat (saww) ne tamam Anbiya ko Namaz padhayi. Us waqt Aap (saww) ke zahen mein ye khalish se paida hui ke kya Ali (as) itne Azeem Manaqib o Fazael ke hamil hain to us waqt Allah Aap par ye Ayat nazil farmayi (10:94)"

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ جَدِّدْ بِهِ مَا امْتَحٰى [مُحِيَ‏] مِنْ دِيْنِكَ وَ اَحْيِ بِهِ مَا بُدِّلَ مِنْ كِتَابِكَ وَ اَظْهِرْ بِهِ مَا غُيِّرَ مِنْ حُكْمِكَ حَتّٰى يَعُوْدَ دِيْنُكَ بِهِ وَ عَلٰى يَدَيْهِ غَضَّا جَدِيْدًا خَالِصًا مُخْلِصًا لَا شَكَّ فِيْهِ وَ لَا شُبْهَةَ مَعَهُ وَ لَا بَاطِلَ عِنْدَهُ وَ لَا بِدْعَةَ لَدَيْهِ...

(Salwat Abul Zarab Isfahani)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ SHAQI INSAAN ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1492)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ ٱلَّذِینَ كَذَّبُوا۟ بِـَٔایَـٰتِ ٱللَّهِ فَتَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡخَـٰسِرِینَ *  إِنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ حَقَّتۡ عَلَیۡهِمۡ كَلِمَتُ رَبِّكَ لَا یُؤۡمِنُونَ *  وَلَوۡ جَاۤءَتۡهُمۡ كُلُّ ءَایَةٍ حَتَّىٰ یَرَوُا۟ ٱلۡعَذَابَ ٱلۡأَلِیمَ.

"Aur un logon mein se na hona jinhone Allah ki Ayat ko jhutlaya hai warna nuqsan uthane walon mein se qarar paoge. Haqeeqat ye hai ke jin logon par tere Rab ka Qaul sabit ho chuka hai woh Imaan nahi layenge. Unke saamne khwah tamam Nishaniyan kyon na aa jayen jab tak woh Dardnak Azaab na dekh lenge."

(Surah Yunus: 95 - 97)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Ayat mein Azali Ashqiya (Permanent Naughty) ke mutalliq Khuda ne farmaya hai ke khwah woh Khuda ki tamam Nishaniyan kyon na dekh len, phir bhi woh Imaan nahi layenge albatta Firaun ki tarah se Dardnak Azaab dekh kar agar woh Imaan le bhi aayen to bhi woh Imaan ke liye soodmand (beneficial) sabit na hoga.

Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi mein is Ayat ke zimn mein Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ki Wilayat ke Munkarin ko bhi shumar kiya gaya hai.

Agar Ayat se murad Imam ko len to iske maani honge Imam ke Jhutlane wale.

👉🏻

Is Ayat mein 'Jabr' (Compulsion) ka concept nahi hai, kyonki Allah Ta'ala Ayatul Kursi mein farmata hai 'Deen mein koi Jabr nahi.' Allah ne unko Shaqi nahi banaya balke woh khud apne Aamaal ki wajah se Shaqi hue. Hamare Aamal apna asar rakhta hai. Har shakhs khud apne Ikhtiyar se Amal karta hai. Ek pyase shakhs ke saamne do Paani ke Glass rakhe hain, ek saaf aur ek alooda ya ganda. Usko ikhtiyar hai dono mein se koi bhi pee sakta hai. Ganda Paani piyega to asar to karega is mein kisi aur ka kya dosh. Isi tarah agar woh kisi bhi tarah ka Gunaah karta hai uska effect woh khud dekhega. Saamne wala use sirf Nasihat kar sakta hai, maane ya na maane. Ab agar nasihat ke bawajood bhi woh wohi kaam kare jo uske liye nuqsaandeh hai to saamne wala sakhs uske bare mein yehi kahega ye pagal ho gaya hai iski samajh mein aane wala nahi, isko iske haal par chhod do.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Sabse zyada Khasaara (Nuqsaan) uthhane wala woh shakhs hai jo Haq baat kehne par qudrat rakhne ke bawajood Haq baat nahi kehta."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p83)

🤲🏻

يَا مَوْلَايَ شَقِيَ مَنْ خَالَفَكُمْ وَ سَعِدَ مَنْ اَطَاعَكُمْ فَاشْهَدْ عَلٰى مَاۤ اَشْهَدْتُكَ عَلَيْهِ وَ اَنَا وَلِيٌّ لَكَ بَرِيۤ‏ءٌ مِنْ عَدُوِّكَ فَالْحَقُّ مَا رَضِيْتُمُوْهُ وَ الْبَاطِلُ مَاۤ اَسْخَطْتُمُوْهُ وَ الْمَعْرُوْفُ مَاۤ اَمَرْتُمْ بِهِ وَ الْمُنْكَرُ مَا نَهَيْتُمْ عَنْهُ

(Ziyarat Aale Yasin - Mafateeh)

             11th Zilhajj 1441

     2nd August 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ HAZRAT YUNUS (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1493)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَوۡلَا كَانَتۡ قَرۡیَةٌ ءَامَنَتۡ فَنَفَعَهَاۤ إِیمَـٰنُهَاۤ إِلَّا قَوۡمَ یُونُسَ لَمَّاۤ ءَامَنُوا۟ كَشَفۡنَا عَنۡهُمۡ عَذَابَ ٱلۡخِزۡیِ فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَمَتَّعۡنَـٰهُمۡ إِلَىٰ حِینࣲ.

"Phir kya aisi koi Misaal hai ke koi Basti Azaab dekh kar Imaan layi ho aur uska Imaan uske liye Nafabakhs sabit hua ho? Siwai Yunus ki Qaum ke. Woh Qaum jab Imaan layi thi to Hamne Dunyavi Zindagi mein unke upar se Ruswai ka Azaab door kar diya tha aur Hamne unhe ek muddat tak chain se rehne diya tha."

(Surah Yunus: 98)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Guzishta Ayat mein us giroh ka zikr kiya tha jo Azaab ko dekh kar bhi Imaan nahi lata.

Is Ayat mein us Qaum ka Zikr hai jo Azaab dekhte hi Imaan le aayi. Aaj se Hazrat Yunus (as) ke waqeat ki shuruaat karte hain:

👉🏻

Riwayat:

Hazrat Yunus (as) ko Allah ne unki Qaum ki taraf Rasool bana kar bheja. Elaan e Nabuwwat ke waqt unki Umr 30 Baras thi. Aap (as) ne 33 Baras tak apni Qaum ko Tableegh ki, lekin pure arse mein sirf 2 askhas Imaan laye, Rubail aur Tanukha. (780 BC)

Rubail ka talluq Ilm o Nabuwwat o Hikmat ke Gharaane se tha, jabke Tanukha ek Abid o Zahid shakhs the. Rubail Bakriyan charaya karte the aur Tanukha Ladkiyaan kat kar Rozi haasil karte the. Janab Yunus (as) ki nazar mein Rubail ka khusoosi maqam tha.

Hazrat Yunus (as) jab apni Qaum ki Nafarmani se tang aa gaye to Bargahe Khuda wandi mein un par Azaab ki darkhwast ki.

Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:

"In mein Pregnant Aurten aur Masoom Bachche, Budhe aur kamzor log bhi maujood hain. Jabke Mein Aadil Hukmaran hun. Meri Rehmat Mere Ghazab par sabqat rakhti hai. (prefer) Mein badon ke Jaraem (crimes) ki Saza chhote Bachchon ko nahi deta. Ye log mere Bande hain, Meri Makhlooq hain aur Mera hi Kunba hai. Mein inhe Mohlat dena chahta hun aur Mein unki Tauba ka Muntazir hun. Meine tujhe Apni Rehmat ka Badal bana kar bheja hai, tumhe in par Rahem karna chahiye. Zara Nooh (as) ko to dekho unhone kitna taweel arse tak Sabr se kaam liya tha aur jab taweel arse ke baad Bad-Dua ki thi to Maine uski Bad-Dua ko qubool kiya tha."

Hazrat Yunus (as) ne arz kiya:

"Parwardigar! Mein to Teri wajah se hi un par naraaz hun. In logon ne jab Tere Ghazab ko dawat di to mein ne in par Bad-Dua ki. Mujhe Teri Izzat ki Qasam! Mein in par taras nahi khaonga. Tujh se meri yehi darkhwast hai ke in par Apna Azaab nazil farma. Ye log Imaan laane wale nahi."

Allah ne farmaya:

"Yunus! Zara ye to socho tere Qaum ki abaadi is waqt ek Lakh se bhi kuchh zyada hai. Tum sirf zahir ko dekh rahe ho jabke Mein Batin ko bhi dekh raha hun. Haan tumhare israar ki wajah se un par Azaab nazil karunga aur Mera Azaab Budh ke Roz 15 Shawwal ko nazil hoga aur Mera Azaab Tulu' e Aftaab (Sunrise) ke baad nazil hoga."

Hazrat Yunus (as) ne ye suna to unhe ek guna khushi mehsoos hui. Unhone apne Shagird Tanukha ko is baat se agaah kiya aur usse farmaya ke aao ham is tabkaar Qaum ko unke anjaam se agaah karen.

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Tehzeebul Ahkam, Ilalush Sharaye, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Al Kaafi, Rauza e Kaafi, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*

🙇

الصّادقُ (عَلَيهِ الّسَلامُ):

إذا أرادَ اللّه‏ُ بعَبدٍ خيراً عَجَّلَ عُقوبَتَهُ في الدنيا ، وإذا أرادَ بعَبدٍ سوءاً أمسَكَ علَيهِ ذُنوبَهُ حتّى يوافِيَ بها يومَ القيامةِ

"Agar Khuda ek Nek Bande ko chahta hai to Woh is Duniya mein Apni Saza mein tezi lata hai, aur agar uske liye bura chahta hai to Woh uski Saza ko Qayamat ke Din ke liye taal deta hai."

(Biharul Anwaar, Vol 81, P-177, H-18, Mizaanul Hikmah, No 3881)

🤲🏻

يَا مَنْ اَنْزَلَ الْعَذَابَ عَلٰى قَوْمِ يُوْنُسَ وَ هُوَ يُرِيْدُ اَنْ يُعَذِّبَهُمْ فَدَعَوْهُ وَ تَضَرَّعُوْا اِلَيْهِ فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابَ وَ مَتَّعَهُمْ اِلٰى حِيْنٍ قَدْ تَرٰى مَكَانِيْ وَ تَسْمَعُ دُعَاۤئِيْ وَ تَعْلَمُ سِرِّيْ وَ عَلَانِيَتِيْ وَ حَالِيْ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ...

(Dua baad Namaz Amaal  e Masjid e Kufa)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    3rd August 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   ♦ HAZRAT YUNUS (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1494)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَوۡلَا كَانَتۡ قَرۡیَةٌ ءَامَنَتۡ فَنَفَعَهَاۤ إِیمَـٰنُهَاۤ إِلَّا قَوۡمَ یُونُسَ لَمَّاۤ ءَامَنُوا۟ كَشَفۡنَا عَنۡهُمۡ عَذَابَ ٱلۡخِزۡیِ فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَمَتَّعۡنَـٰهُمۡ إِلَىٰ حِینࣲ.

"Phir kya aisi koi Misaal hai ke koi Basti Azaab dekh kar Imaan layi ho aur uska Imaan uske liye Nafabakhs sabit hua ho? Siwai Yunus ki Qaum ke. Woh Qaum jab Imaan layi thi to Hamne Dunyavi Zindagi mein unke upar se Ruswai ka Azaab door kar diya tha aur Hamne unhe ek muddat tak chain se rehne diya tha."

(Surah Yunus: 98)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Ayat mein us Qaum ka Zikr hai jo Azaab dekhte hi Imaan le aayi. Hazrat Yunus (as) ke waqeat ka agla hissa pesh e khidmat hai:

👉🏻

Riwayat: (Cont'd...)

Hazrat Yunus (as) ne jab Azaab ke bare mein bataya tab Tanukha ne kaha:

"Hamen unhe batane ki zaroorat nahi unhe unke haal par chhod do taake unke upar Azaab aa jaye.

Hazrat Yunus (as) ne Rubail ko bhi bataya to unhone arz kiya:

"Aap (as) Allah ke Rasool hain, apne Rab se darkhwast karen ke Woh Azaab ke Faisle ko tabdeel karde. Kyonki Allah ko unhe Azaab dene ki zaroorat nahi hai, aap Shafqat o Narmi se kaam len aur logon ko Zinda rehne ka haq den."

Is tarah dono ki raye mein ikhtelaf hua.

Janabe Yunus (as) ne Tanukha ko apne saath liya aur Shaher ke centre mein jaa kar logon ko Azaab ka ailaan kar diya. Jab unhone ye suna to na sirf aapki Takzeeb ki balke Aap (as) par pur tashaddud ho gaye aur Shaher se bahar nikal diya. Janabe Yunus (as) apne student Tanukha ko saath lekar Shaher ke kuchh faasle par chale gaye aur wahan reh kar Qaum ka anjaam dekhne ka Intezar karne lage jabke Rubail ne Shaher nahi chhoda.

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Tehzeebul Ahkam, Ilalush Sharaye, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Al Kaafi, Rauza e Kaafi, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Tajjub hai us shakhs par jo Azaab ka darr to rakhta hai lekin (jin Badkaariyo'n ki wajah se Azaab hoga unse) woh rukta nahi aur Sawaab ki Ummeed to rakhta hai lekin (Gunaho'n se) na to rukta hai aur na (Sawaab ke liye) amal karta hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p337)

😨

﻿Imam Reza (as):

"Jo (Khuda se) khauf karta hai, woh Azaab se mehfooz rehta hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p349)

🤲🏻

وَ لَا تُعَذِّبَنِيْ بِقَبِيْحٍ كَانَ مِنِّي فَاِنَّ عَفْوَكَ وَ جُوْدَكَ يَسَعُنِيْ اِنَّكَ عَلٰى كُلِّ شَيْ‏ءٍ قَدِيْرٌ ۔

(Dua e Imam Hasan - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUNUS (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1495)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَوۡلَا كَانَتۡ قَرۡیَةٌ ءَامَنَتۡ فَنَفَعَهَاۤ إِیمَـٰنُهَاۤ إِلَّا قَوۡمَ یُونُسَ لَمَّاۤ ءَامَنُوا۟ كَشَفۡنَا عَنۡهُمۡ عَذَابَ ٱلۡخِزۡیِ فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَمَتَّعۡنَـٰهُمۡ إِلَىٰ حِینࣲ.

"Phir kya aisi koi Misaal hai ke koi Basti Azaab dekh kar Imaan layi ho aur uska Imaan uske liye Nafabakhs sabit hua ho? Siwai Yunus ki Qaum ke. Woh Qaum jab Imaan layi thi to Hamne Dunyavi Zindagi mein unke upar se Ruswai ka Azaab door kar diya tha aur Hamne unhe ek muddat tak chain se rehne diya tha."

(Surah Yunus: 98)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Ayat mein us Qaum ka Zikr hai jo Azaab dekhte hi Imaan le aayi. Hazrat Yunus (as) ke waqeat ka agla hissa pesh e khidmat hai:

👉🏻

Riwayat: (Cont'd...)

Jab Mahe Shawwal shuru hua to Rubail ne Pahad ki choti par chadh kar ailan kiya:

"Logo! Mein tumhara Khairkhwah (Well-wisher) hun. Meri baaton ko tawajjo se suno. Shawwal ka Mahina shuru ho chuka hai aur tumhare Nabi ne 15 tarikh, Budh ko Azaabe Ilahi ki khabar di hai. Yaad rakho unhone ye khabar Wahye Ilahi ke baad hi sunayi hai. Ab tum khud socho tumhara anjaam kya hone wala hai."

Jab logon ne Rubail ki dardmandana guftugu suni to unke Dil kaanp uthe aur Rubail se kaha:

"Tum ek Sahibe Ilm o Hikmat aur Shafeeq Insaan ho. Aap hi batayen ham kya karen?"

Rubail ne kaha:

"Jab Budh ka Din aaye to Tuloo e Fajr (Sunrise) ke saath hi Mard Aurton se juda ho jayen aur Maayen Bachchon se alaihda ho jayen aur Janwaron se unke Doodh peene wale Bachche door kar liye jayen aur sab cheekh o pukar kar Khuda ki Bargah mein Tauba karen aur Usse Ma'afi talab karen aur apna Rukh Aasmaan ki taraf karke kahen:

_"Parwardigar! Hamne Zulm kiya, ham ne Tere Nabi ki Takzeeb (denial) ki hai. Ab ham apne Gunahon ki tujh se Ma'afi talab karte hain. Agar Tu ne ham par Rahem na kiya to ham Muazzib log (Punished) mein qarar payenge. Aye Arhamur Rahemeen! Rahem farma aur hamari Tauba qubool farma."_

Rubail ne kaha ke jab tak Azaab ke tamam asaar khatm na ho jayen us waqt tak musalsal girya o buka karte raho aur ro ro kar Duayen maangte raho."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Tehzeebul Ahkam, Ilalush Sharaye, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Al Kaafi, Rauza e Kaafi, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 Tauba:

Imam Baqir (as):ہ

"Jab saa'ns yahaa'n tak aa jaaye (ishara kiya apne halq ki taraf), to oos waqt Aalim ki Tauba to qubool na hogi, albatta jaahil ki hogi."

(Al Kaafi, v5, p41)

😟

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab banda e Momin khaalis Dil ke saath Tauba karta hai to Khuda us se Mohabbat karta hai aur uske Aibo'n ko Duniya aur Akherat mein chhupa deta hai." Raawi ne sawaal kiya, "Uske Aibo'n ko kyun kar chhupaye jaate hain?" Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Dono Farishto'n ne uske Gunah qalam-bund (likhe) hote hain, Wo unhe faramosh kar deta hai…aur jab woh Khuda ke Huzoor pahu'nchta hai, uske khilaaf uske Gunaho'n ki Gawahi dene wali koi cheez nahi hoti."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p808)

🤲🏻

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Mere Aaqa! Mere Dil se Duniya ki Mohabbat nikaal de aur mujhe Apni Makhlooq mein sab se behtar, Nabiyo'n ke khaatim Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) aur unki Aal (as) ke qareeb jagah inaayat farma aur mujhe Apne huzoor Tauba ke maqaam ki taraf palta de. Aur mujhe khud apne aap par Rone ki Taufeeq de kyunki main apni umr taal matool aur Jhooti Aarzuo'n mein ga'nwa di…"

(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)

     5th August 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUNUS (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1496)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَوۡلَا كَانَتۡ قَرۡیَةٌ ءَامَنَتۡ فَنَفَعَهَاۤ إِیمَـٰنُهَاۤ إِلَّا قَوۡمَ یُونُسَ لَمَّاۤ ءَامَنُوا۟ كَشَفۡنَا عَنۡهُمۡ عَذَابَ ٱلۡخِزۡیِ فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَمَتَّعۡنَـٰهُمۡ إِلَىٰ حِینࣲ.

"Phir kya aisi koi Misaal hai ke koi Basti Azaab dekh kar Imaan layi ho aur uska Imaan uske liye Nafabakhs sabit hua ho? Siwai Yunus ki Qaum ke. Woh Qaum jab Imaan layi thi to Hamne Dunyavi Zindagi mein unke upar se Ruswai ka Azaab door kar diya tha aur Hamne unhe ek muddat tak chain se rehne diya tha."

(Surah Yunus: 98)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Yunus (as) ka waqea  jari hai:

👉🏻

Riwayat: (Cont'd...)

"Ahle Shaher ko Rubail ki baat pasand aayi. Jab wo Din aaya sab ne waisa hi kiya. Sab apna shaher chhod kar khule Maidan mein gaye. Bachchon ko Maaon se alag kiya. Janwaron ko Bachhron se alag kiya to masoom Bachche rone lage aur dakraane lage.

Tulu e Aftaab Azaab e Ilahi ke asaar namudar hone lage. Zard Aandhiyan chalne lagi, sab jagah tareeki chha gayi. Log cheekh pukar karne lage, girya zaari shuru ho gayi, Tauba karne lage.

Tanukha Janabe Yunus (as) ke saath Shaher ke Cheekho pukar sun kar Allah se Dua kar raha tha ke Allah aur Azaab nazil kare.

Jabke Rubail ne Azaab ki wajah se Shaher chhod diya tha aur wahan unki gidgadahat sunta aur Allah se Dua karta Bare Ilaha un logon par Rahem farma aur Azaab door kar de.

Akhirar Zawal ka waqt aa gaya, Azaab qareeb tha, log Dil ki gehrayyon se Dua kar rahe the, Rehmat e Khuda Wandi josh mein aayi, aur Khuda ne Israfeel Farishte se farmaya ke tum jao aur apne Paron ki quwwat se Azaab ko dhakel kar Musal ke Pahado par gira do. Usne aisa hi kiya aur Pahad lohe ka ho gaya.

Algharz Zawal ke waqt Azaab ke Badal chhat gaye. Maon ne apne Bachchon ko Seeno se lagaya. Logon ne apne apne gharon ko wapsi ki aur Allah ka Shukr ada kiya.

Doosri taraf Hazrat Yunus (as) Shaher ki taraf aaye taake dekhen kya haal hai. Lekin unhe ye dekh kar tajjub aur sadma hua ke log apne apne kamon mein masroof hain, Azaab ka koi asar nahi hai. Janabe Yunus (as) ne socha pehle to log unko Nabi manne ko tayyar nahi the, ab to woh inko jhoota samjhenge. Aur to aur unke saamne unko munh dikhane ke qabil nahi rahe. Ye soch kar woh wapas Behre Eliya ki taraf rawana ho gaye. Aur Tanukha apni Basti mein laut aya.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Raaste mein Tanukha ki Rubail se mulaqat hui to Rubail ne usse farmaya: "Tanukha! Tumne ab dekh liya hai ke ham dono mein se kiski ray wazni thi. Ab batao tumhari Ray sahih thi ya meri?"

Tanukha ne kaha:

"Mein tasdeeq karta hun ke aapki Ray meri se behtar thi. Mein aaj se qabl apne Zohd ki wajah se apne aapko tumse afzal samajhta tha, lekin ab mujhe andaza hua hai ke Aalim, Zahid se kahin afzal hota hai."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Tehzeebul Ahkam, Ilalush Sharaye, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Al Kaafi, Rauza e Kaafi, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.......)

🤲🏻

Imam Ali (as):

"Teri Izzat o Azmat ki Qasam, Aye mere Aqa wa Maula! Agar Tu ne meri goyaee (talk) ko baqi rakha to mein Ahle Jahannum ke darmiyan bhi Umeedwaron ki tarah nala o shewa karunga aur aziz e gum kardah ki tarah Teri doori par aah o buka karunga aur Tu jahan bhi hoga Tujhe awaaz dunga....."

(Dua-e-Kumail - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁🍁

               15th Zilhajj 1441

     6th August 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUNUS (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1497)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَوۡلَا كَانَتۡ قَرۡیَةٌ ءَامَنَتۡ فَنَفَعَهَاۤ إِیمَـٰنُهَاۤ إِلَّا قَوۡمَ یُونُسَ لَمَّاۤ ءَامَنُوا۟ كَشَفۡنَا عَنۡهُمۡ عَذَابَ ٱلۡخِزۡیِ فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَمَتَّعۡنَـٰهُمۡ إِلَىٰ حِینࣲ.

"Phir kya aisi koi Misaal hai ke koi Basti Azaab dekh kar Imaan layi ho aur uska Imaan uske liye Nafabakhs sabit hua ho? Siwai Yunus ki Qaum ke. Woh Qaum jab Imaan layi thi to Hamne Dunyavi Zindagi mein unke upar se Ruswai ka Azaab door kar diya tha aur Hamne unhe ek muddat tak chain se rehne diya tha."

(Surah Yunus: 98)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Yunus (as) ka waqea  jari hai:

👉🏻

Riwayat: (Cont'd...)

"Hazrat Yunus (as) Behre Eliya ki taraf chale aur ek Kashti mein sawar ho gaye. Kashti jaise hi gehre Paani mein dakhil hui to ek badi Machhli namudar hui. Kashti mein sawar sabhi musafir ghabhra gayi. Janabe Yunus (as) jo front side par baithe hue the to woh backside par aa gaye. Mallah ne kaha maloom hota hai ke yahan koi bhaga hua ghulam sawar hai jab tak Machhli use nighal na legi wo Kashti ko sahil tak nahi pahunchne degi. Ham sab Qura andazi karte hain jiske naam ka Qura niklega woh Kashti ke bahar chhalang laga de taake baqi logon ki Jaan bach jaye.

Qura mein Janabe Yunus (as) ka Qura nikla aur aapne  Kashti se chhalang laga di aur Machhli ne aapko nigal liya. Riwayat ke mutabiq 3 ya 7 Din aap (as) Machhli ke Shikam (Pet) mein rahe. Aap (as) Machhli ke Machhli ke Shikam mein ye Ayat padhte rahe: *لَّاۤ إِلَـٰهَ إِلَّاۤ أَنتَ سُبۡحَـٰنَكَ إِنِّی كُنتُ مِنَ ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ.*  (Anbiya:87) ki Tasbeeh padhte rahe. Akhirkar Allah Ta'ala ko aap (as) par Taras aaya aur Machhli ko Hukm diya ke wo unhe bahar ugal de.

Machhli ne aapko bahar ugla to aap nihayat hi kamzor ho chuke the. Allah ne aap (as) ke liye ek Kaddu  (Pumpkin) ki bel ugayi jiske saye mein aap (as) poora Hafte araam karte rahe. Phir ek Hafte ke baad chalne phirne ke qabil hue to Allah ne Kaddu ki jad par ek Keeda musallat kiya jiski wajah se wo Bel khushk ho gaya.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Jab Janabe Yunus (as) ne Bel ko sookha dekha to bahut ghamgin hue. Janabe Yunus (as) Allah Ta'ala se farmaya: "Ye Bel to Khushk (dry) ho gayi. Mein is Bel se manoos ho chuka tha magar Tu ne ise khushk kar diya."

Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:

"Yunus (as)! Is Kaddu ki Bel ko kya Tu ne apne haath se kasht kiya tha? Aur Tu ne ise Paani pila kar bhi parwan nahi chadhaya tha. Ab agar Bel khushk ho gayi to tujhe iska ranj ho raha hai jabke tu ne ek lakh se zyada abadi par Bad-Dua ki to Rahem na aaya. Ab jao poori Qaum ko tumhara intezar hai. Woh tujhe Nabi maanenge, ab ja kar unki Rahnumai karo."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Tehzeebul Ahkam, Ilalush Sharaye, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Al Kaafi, Rauza e Kaafi, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.......)

🤲🏻

یَاۤ اِلٰهِىْ فَبِذُنُوْبِىْ بَعْدَ حُجَّتِكَ عَلَىَّ وَاِنْ تَعْفُ عَنِّىْ فَبِحِلْمِكَ وَجُوْدِكَ وَكرَمِكَ لَاۤ اِلٰهَ اِلَّاۤ اَنْتَ سُبْحَانكَ اِنِّى كُنْتُ مِنَ الظَّالِمِیْنَ، لَاۤ اِلٰهَ اِلَّاۤ اَنْتَ سُبْحَانَكَ اِنّىْ كُنْتُ مِنَ الْمُسْتَغْفِرِیْنَ........

(Dua-e-Arafa - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             16th Zilhajj 1441

      7th August 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUNUS (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1498)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَوۡلَا كَانَتۡ قَرۡیَةٌ ءَامَنَتۡ فَنَفَعَهَاۤ إِیمَـٰنُهَاۤ إِلَّا قَوۡمَ یُونُسَ لَمَّاۤ ءَامَنُوا۟ كَشَفۡنَا عَنۡهُمۡ عَذَابَ ٱلۡخِزۡیِ فِی ٱلۡحَیَوٰةِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَمَتَّعۡنَـٰهُمۡ إِلَىٰ حِینࣲ.

"Phir kya aisi koi Misaal hai ke koi Basti Azaab dekh kar Imaan layi ho aur uska Imaan uske liye Nafabakhs sabit hua ho? Siwai Yunus ki Qaum ke. Woh Qaum jab Imaan layi thi to Hamne Dunyavi Zindagi mein unke upar se Ruswai ka Azaab door kar diya tha aur Hamne unhe ek muddat tak chain se rehne diya tha."

(Surah Yunus: 98)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Yunus (as) ka waqea  jari hai: (Last Part)

👉🏻

Riwayat: (Cont'd...)

Hazrat Yunus (as) Nineveh ki taraf chal pade. Jab aap (as) Nineveh ke qareeb pahunche to aapko sharm maane hui ke wahan jayen to kaise jayen. Nineveh ke qareeb ek Charwaha (Shepherd) jo masroof tha usse kaha ke jao shaher jaa kar keh do Hazrat Yunus (as) wapas aa gayen hain. Usne kaha aap jhoot bol rahe hain, unko to Machhli kha gayi, ab wapas nahi aa sakte. Hazrat Yunus (as) use kehte rahe lekin woh manne ko tayyar nahi tha. Phir aap (as) ne kaha ke agar teri ye Bakri Gawahi de de to maan lega. Usne kaha haan. Aap (as) ne Bakri ki taraf ishara kiya aur usne fasih lehja mein Gawahi di.

Charwaha Shaher mein gaya to logon ne bhi iski baat nahi maani aur Charwahe ko maarne daude  tab usne kaha yaqeen nahi aata to is Bakri se poochh lo. Tab phir uski Bakri ne Gawahi di.

To phir logon ka ek hujum Shaher ke bahar Hazrat Yunus (as) ke Welcome ke liye umad pada. Aapko Salam kiya aur aap (as) ko bade ehteram se Shaher mein laye aur sab logon ne Imaan qabool kiya."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Tehzeebul Ahkam, Ilalush Sharaye, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Al Kaafi, Rauza e Kaafi, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

Dastaane Qaume Hazrat Yunus (as) ko tasfeel se pesh karne ka maqsad yehi tha ke iske har zikr mein ek Hidayat ka gosha hai.

Kulli taur par pata chala ke agar Insaan Sidq Dil se Tauba kare to uski Tauba ya Dua zaroor qabool hogi. Qaum par Azaab to akhari marhala hota hai, Allah kafi mohlat deta hai.

Aaj log Covid ki Beemari se pareshan ho gaye, ab ye Azaab hai ya Imtehan, jo bhi ho, Insaan bebas ho gaya. Ye Pandemic Insaan ke liye out of Control ho gaya. Yahan agar sab mil ke sidq Dil se agar Tauba o Isteghfar karte aur Dua maangte to kya ham itna bhi Imaan nahi rakhte ke Khuda is Waba ko khatm kar sakta hai. Logon ko kya karna chahiye tha ye Qur'an ne iska tareqa bata diya.

Hazrat Yunus (as) Qaum ke Inkaar ki wajah se Ghaibat chale gaye, unse ojhal ho gaye. Lekin Qaum ki Tauba o Isteghfar ki wajah se Allah ne unke darmiyan unke Hadi o Rehbar, Nabi ka Zahoor kiya aur unki Zindagi ne Kamyabi ka Raasta ikhtiyar kiya.

Aaj bhi wohi haal hai, agar logon ki Tauba / Dua qubool ho jaati to ein mumkin hai Imam Mahdi (as) ka Zahoor ho jata, delay hamari taraf se hai, Allah ki taraf se nahi. Ham ye keh kar nahi chhot sakte ke jab Allah chahega Zahoor ho jayega. Ye bhi sahi hai lekin jab tak ham maangege nahi ye Ne'mat nahi mil sakti. Faqat unke Zahoor ke liye Sidq Dil se zyada se zyada Dua karen.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Jo shakhs mujh par Imaan rakhe aur Ali (as) se Mohabbat kare aur unki Wilayat ka bhi qaael ho, uspar Jahannum haraam hai. Khuda Laa'nat kare uspar jo Ali (as) ka munkir aur unka dushman hai…"

(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v2, p365)

🤲🏻

...وَ اَسْاَلُكَ یَا رَبِّ تَوْبَةً نَصُوْحًا تَرْضَاهَا وَ نِیَّةً تَحْمَدُهَا وَ عَمَلًا صَالِحًا تَقْبَلُهُ وَ اَنْ تَغْفِرَ لِیْ وَ تَرْحَمَنِیْۤ اِذَا تَوَفَّیْتَنِیْ وَ تُهَوِّنَ عَلَیَّ سَكَرَاتِ الْمَوْتِ وَ تَحْشُرَنِیْ فِیْ زُمْرَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَّ اٰلِهِ صَلَوَاتُ اللهِ عَلَیْهِ وَ عَلَیْهِمْ....

(Dua baad az Ziyarat Aimma (as) - Mafateeh)

     3rd September 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   ♦ DEEN MEIN JABR NAHI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1499)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَوۡ شَاۤءَ رَبُّكَ لَـَٔامَنَ مَن فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ كُلُّهُمۡ جَمِیعًاۚ أَفَأَنتَ تُكۡرِهُ ٱلنَّاسَ حَتَّىٰ یَكُونُوا۟ مُؤۡمِنِینَ.

"Agar tere Parwardigar ki Mashiyyat hoti (ke tamam log hi Imaan le aayen) to tamam Zameen wale sab ke sab Imaan le aayen to kya tu logo'n ko Majboor karega ke woh Momin ban jayen?"

(Surah Yunus: 99)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Mamoon Rashid ne Imam Reza (as) se is Ayat ke bare sawal kiya to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Mere Abaa e Tahereen (as) ki Sanad se mujh tak ye Riwayat pahunchi hai ke Madina mein kuchh Sahaba ne AanHazrat (saww) ko mashwara diya tha ke jo log Aap (saww) ke haath ke neeche hain unhe jabran Kalma padhwayen, isse hamari tadaad mein izaafa hoga aur Dushman ham se mar'oob (terrified) honge."

"AanHazrat (saww) ne farmaya: "Mein koi Bid'at ijaad kar ke Khuda ke Huzoor pesh hone ka khwahish mand nahi hun. Allah ne jo cheez mere zimme aayed nahi ki mein use apni taraf se ijaad karna pasand nahi karta." Is par Allah Ta'ala ne ye Ayat nazil farmayi aur is Ayat ke zariye Apne Habib ko ye Paigham diya ke Khuda kisi ko Majboor karke Imaan qabool karana nahi chahta. Agar aisa hota to koi bhi shakhs Sawab o Jaza ka Haqdar na hota. Khuda ye Chahta hai ke log Azaad aur Mukhtar ho kar apni marzi o raghbat se Imaan layen taake woh Jaza aur Maqam e Taqarrub ban saken."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🍃

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Apna mamla Khuda ke liye banao, logon ke liye na banao, kyonki jo mamla Khuda ke liye hoga wo to khalis Khuda le hi shumar kiya jayega aur jo mamla logon ke liye hoga to woh Khuda ke haan Sharaf e Qubooliyyat hasil na karega aur apne Deen ke liye logon se jhagda na karo, kyonki jhagda Dilon mein Bimari paida karta hai. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: "Aap jisse Muhabbat rakhen use Raahe mustaqeem chala nahi sakte, Allah jise chahe Raahe Mustaqeem par chalaye." (Qasas: 56) aur Ayat (10:99)."

"Logon ko unke haal par rehne do. Logon ne logon se Deen hasil kiya hai jabke tumne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se Deen liya hai. Meine apne Waalid (as) se suna tha ke jab Allah kisi Bande ko is Amr (Aqeeda e Wilayat) mein dakhil karna chahta hai to Woh itni tezi se is mein dakhil hota hai jaisa ke Parinda apne Ashyane mein tezi se dakhil hota hai."

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Reza (as) se Mamun ke darbaar mein sawaal kiya, "Ye farmaiye ke kya Bande majboor hain?" Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Khuda Aadil hai. Ye mumkin nahi ke Wo logo'n se jabran Gunah karaaye aur phir uspar unko saza de." Fazal ne kaha, "Achcha, to phir bilkul azaad hain?" Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Nahi. Uski (Allah ki) Hikmat se ye baeed hai ke Woh Apne Bande ko bilkul Azaad naqaa e be-mehaar (camel without strings / belagaam Oo'ntt) ki tarah chhod de."

(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v5, p177)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"....Salam ho us Mazloom par  jo Be Yawar o Madadgar tha. Salam ho Paak o Pakeeza Khaak mein basne wale. Salam ho Buland o Bala Qubah wale par. Salam ho us par jise Khuda e Buzurg o Bartar ne Paak kiya. Salam ho us par jiski khidmat guzari par Jibrael ko nazaan tha. Salam ho us par jise Mikaeel ne Gehware mein Lori di....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

     4th September 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ HATDHARMO KO NASIHAT KARNA BEKAAR HAI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1500)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَمَا كَانَ لِنَفۡسٍ أَن تُؤۡمِنَ إِلَّا بِإِذۡنِ ٱللَّهِۚ وَیَجۡعَلُ ٱلرِّجۡسَ عَلَى ٱلَّذِینَ لَا یَعۡقِلُونَ *  قُلِ ٱنظُرُوا۟ مَاذَا فِی ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِۚ وَمَا تُغۡنِی ٱلۡـَٔایَـٰتُ وَٱلنُّذُرُ عَن قَوۡمࣲ لَّا یُؤۡمِنُونَ.

"Aur Kisi Nafs ke ikhtiyar mein nahi hai ke Parwardigar ki Ijazat ke baghair Imaan le aaye aur Khuda ka tareeqa ye hai ke jo log Aql se kaam nahi lete un par (Kufr ki) gandgi dal deta hai."

"Aap keh den ke Aasmaan aur Zameen mein jo kuch hai use (ghaur se) dekho *aur jo log Imaan laana hi nahi chahte unko Ayaat o Tanbihaat (warnings) koi fayda nahi pahunchati."*

(Surah Yunus: 100 - 101)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ayaat ( آيات ) se Aimma aur Nuzur ( النذر ) se Anbiya murad hain."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Shaane Nuzool:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Habib e Khuda Meraj par gaye to Jibrael (as) Aap (saww) ke liye Buraaq laye aur us par sawar ho kar Baitul Muqaddas gaye aur wahan Anbiya Karam (as) se mulaqat hui. Wapas aane par Aap (saww) ne Sahaba se iski ittela di aur farmaya ke jab mein wapas aa raha tha to Abu Sufyan ka Tijarti Qafila dekha jo ek Paani ke kinare khada tha aur unka ek surkh rang ka Oont gum ho gaya tha aur log usko talaash kar rahe the."

"Kuffar e Quraish ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko azmana chaha. Kafi arse ho gaya Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko Shaam (Syria) gaye hue, ab to bahut wahan changes ho chuke honge. Wahan ke bare mein sawal poochhenge, agar jawab na de paye to hazimat hogi."

"Jibrael (as) ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke saamne Shaam ko present kar diya aur Aap (saww) ne unke saare sawalaat ka jawab diya. Magar iske bawajood intihai kam afraad Aap (saww) par Imaan laye. Allah ne in logon ke liye ye Ayat (10:101) nazil ki."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

Jo hatdharmi log hote hain unke saamne apna Dil bhi nikal kar rakh do, woh nahi paseejenge. Ye Ayat Andbhakt logon ke liye hai.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki Ma'arefat hai aur badtareen Andhaapan hamare fazl se Aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as) ne ek sawaal ke jawab mein farmaya:

"Hamare awaam aur Ulema aur Yahud ke awaam aur Ulema mein farq bhi hai aur ek lihaaz se masawaat (similarity ) bhi hai. Awaam e Yahud ko maloom tha ke unke Ulema Jhoot bolte hain, Haraam khaate hain, rishwat lete hain aur Sifaarisho'n aur Rishtedariyo'n aur Rawadariyo'n ki bena par Ahkaam e Khuda ko tabdeel kar dete hain; jin logo'n par naraaz hon, unko huqooq se mehroom kar dete hain aur jin par raazi hon unko na-haq amwaal (maal) dilwaate hain, wagairah. Lihaza, Khuda Wande Kareem ne unki is Andha-dhund Taqleed ki mazammat farmayi hai."

(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v2, p128)

🤲🏻

الامام العصر (عج):

بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيْمِ لَا لِاَمْرِهِ تَعْقِلُوْنَ وَ لَا مِنْ اَوْلِيَاۤئِهِ تَقْبَلُوْنَ حِكْمَةٌ بَالِغَةٌ فَمَا تُغْنِيْ النُّذُرُ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْنَا وَ عَلٰى عِبَادِ اللّٰهِ الصَّالِحِيْنَ.

(Letter of Imam e Asr (atfs) before Ziyarat e Ale Yaseen - Mafateeh)

🤲🏻

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Salam ho us par jiski Dushmanon ne uske  aur uske Ahle Haram ka silsile mein apne Paiman (Covenant) ko toda. Salam ho us par jiska Khoon Zulm ke sath bahaya gaya. Salam ho Zakhmon se Nahane wale par. Salam ho us par jise Pyas ki Shiddat mein Noke Sina ke talkh ghoont pilaye gaye. Salam ho us par jise itni badi Kaynat mein yako tanha chhod diya gaya."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

   5th September 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ INTEZAAR ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1501)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَهَلۡ یَنتَظِرُونَ إِلَّا مِثۡلَ أَیَّامِ ٱلَّذِینَ خَلَوۡا۟ مِن قَبۡلِهِمۡۚ قُلۡ فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ *  ثُمَّ نُنَجِّی رُسُلَنَا وَٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ حَقًّا عَلَیۡنَا نُنجِ ٱلۡمُؤۡمِنِینَ.

"Kya ye log apne se pehle logon jaise bure din dekhne ka Intezar kar rahe hain? Inse keh do ke tum Intezar karo mein bhi tumhare saath Intezar karne walon mein hun."

"(Aise waqt mein) Ham Apne Rasoolon aur un logon ko Najaat dete hain jo Imaan laate hain. Hamara yehi Tareeqa hai. Ham par ye Haq hai ke Ahle Imaan ko Najaat den."

(Surah Yunus: 102 - 103)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Guzishta Ayat mein Allah ka Khitab un Anbhakton se tha jo apni ravish ko badalna nahi chahte. Unko samjhana bekar hai, unko unke haal par chhod diya jaye aur unke upar hone wale nataij ka Intezar kiya jaye.

Allah yake baad digar Apne Hadi Hazrat Adam (as) se le kar H. Khatam tak bhejta raha, yaha tak ye silsila Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke baad 12 Aimma (as) ke zariye jari raha. Lekin in Hadiyaan aur unke Pairokaron par Zulm o sitam hota raha. Inhone Anbiya (as) ko qatl kiya, sabhi Aimma (as) ko shaheed kiya, lekin Allah ne is silsile ki Akheri kadi ko logon se ojhal kar diya. Ab us Din ka Intezar Rasoole Khuda (saww), khud Allah aur tamam Mo'meneen kar rahe hain, jis Din Zulm ka khatma hoga aur in Munkarin ko waise hi saza milege jaise guzishta gumrah Qaumo ko mili hai. Aur Mo'meneen ke liye Imam Mahdi (as) ka Zahoor Kushayesh ka Din hoga.

Poori Duniya usi Maseeha ke Intezaar mein hai. Lekin Allah ka waada hai agar koi Muntazir Intezaar karte karte mar bhi gaya to use bhi us Din uthaya jayega jaisa ke Dua e Ahd mein hai.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Reza (as) se Sawaal kiya ke kushaysh (Faraj) kab hogi?Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Kya tum nahi jaante ke Kushayesh ka Intezaar bhi Kushayesh ka ek hissa hai. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ.

"Sabr aur Kushayesh ka Intezaar behtareen cheez hai. Kya tu ne Allah ka ye farman nahi suna:

وَٱرۡتَقِبُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُمۡ رَقِیبࣱ (Hud: 93)

فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ. (7: 71)

"Lehaza tumhe Sabr se kaam lena chahiye. Hamesha Mayusi ke Waqt hi Kushayesh utarti hai. (Kyonki Shab e Siyah ka khatema hamesha Subah par hua karta hai.)Tumse pehle log tumse bade Sabir the."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنْ حَالَ بَيْنِيْ وَ بَيْنَهُ الْمَوْتُ الَّذِيْ جَعَلْتَهُ عَلٰى عِبَادِكَ حَتْمًا مَقْضِيًّا، فَاَخْرِجْنِيْ مِنْ قَبْرِيْ مُؤْتَزِرًا كَفَنِيْ شَاهِرًا سَيْفِيْ مُجَرِّدًا قَنَاتِيْ

(Dua-e-Ahad)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Salam ho us par jise yun Uryan chhoda gaya jiski misal nahi milti. Salam ho us par jiski Shaye Rag kaati gayi. Salam ho Deen ke us hami par jisne baghair kisi madadgar Difayi Jang ladi. Salam ho us Reshe Aqdas par jo Khoon se rangeen hui. Salam ho Aapke Khaak Alooda Rukhsaron par. Salam ho lute aur nuche hue Badan par. Salam ho Kati hui Shaye Rag par. Salam ho Neze par buland kiye jaane wale Sar e Aqdas par. Salam ho un Muqaddas Jismon par jinke tukde Sehra mein bikhar gaye."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

     6th September 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ TAUHEED-E-ILAHI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1502)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قُلۡ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ إِن كُنتُمۡ فِی شَكࣲّ مِّن دِینِی فَلَاۤ أَعۡبُدُ ٱلَّذِینَ تَعۡبُدُونَ مِن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ وَلَـٰكِنۡ أَعۡبُدُ ٱللَّهَ ٱلَّذِی یَتَوَفَّىٰكُمۡۖ وَأُمِرۡتُ أَنۡ أَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُؤۡمِنِینَ *  وَأَنۡ أَقِمۡ وَجۡهَكَ لِلدِّینِ حَنِیفࣰا وَلَا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ *  وَلَا تَدۡعُ مِن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ مَا لَا یَنفَعُكَ وَلَا یَضُرُّكَۖ فَإِن فَعَلۡتَ فَإِنَّكَ إِذࣰا مِّنَ ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ.

"(Paighambar (saww)) Aap keh den: Aye Insaano! Agar tumhe mere Deen mein koi Shak hai (to suno) mein unki Ibaadat nahi karta jinki tum Khuda ko chhod kar Ibaadat karte ho. Balke mein to sirf Usi Khuda ki Ibaadat karta hun Jo tumhe Maut dega aur mujhe ye Hukm diya gaya hai ke mein Imaan walon ka hissa ban kar rahun, Yaksu ho kar (Upright) apne aap ko theek theek is Deen par qaem kar de aur kabhi bhi Mushrekin mein se na hona. Aur Khuda ko chhod kar unhe na pukaren jo na to aapko fayda pahuncha sake aur na hi nuqsaan de sake aur Aapne aisa kiya to Aapka shumar Zulm karnewalon mein se hoga."

(Surah Yunus: 104 - 106)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

In Ayaat mein Tauheed e Khuda ka zikr hai.

Kuffar chahte the ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) apne Khuda ke saath saath unke Khuda ko bhi maane. Yahan Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko Allah ne bata diya ke yahan Aqeede mein koi Rawadari nahi chalegi. Ye bhi achhe woh achhe yahan nahi chalta. Deen e Islam Deen e Hanif hai, jo ke mukammal Tauheed ka qael hai. Kafir un Ma'bood ko maante hain jo koi kaam ke nahi, bas Patthar ke But hain. Islam ne jis Khuda ka tarruf karaya Woh Khuda Maut o Hayaat deta hai. Ye wo cheez hai jiska har koi mushaheda karta hai, sabit karne ki koi zaroorat hi nahi. Is Khuda ko chhod kar kisi aur se kuchh milne wala nahi.

Lekin Allah ko samajhne ke liye Babullah (Ali as) ke Darwaze se dakhil hokar Madinatul Ilm (Rasoole Khuda (saww)) se Ma'arefat e Ilahi hasil karni hogi. Warna Kufr o Jihalat ke Jungalon mein bhatakta phirega.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Taqi (as):

"Jo bolne waale ki baat kaan dhar-ke sune usne (goya) uski parastish / Ibaadat ki. Pus, agar bolne wala Khuda ki baat keh raha hai to usne Khuda ki ibadat ki aur agar bolne waala Shaitan ki zabaan bol raha hai to usne Shaitan ki parastish ki."

(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205)

🤲🏻

لَاۤ اِلٰهَ اِلَا اللهُ اِلٰهًا وَاحِدًا وَ نَحْنُ لَهُ مُسْلِمُوْنَ لَاۤ اِلٰهَ اِلَا اللهُ وَ لَا نَعْبُدُ اِلَّا اِيَّاهُ مُخْلِصِيْنَ لَهُ الدِّيْنَ وَ لَوْ كَرِهَ الْمُشْرِكُوْنَ لَاۤ اِلٰهَ اِلَا اللهُ رَبُّنَا وَ رَبُّ اٰباۤئِنَا الْاَوَّلِيْنَ لَاۤ اِلٰهَ اِلَّا اللهُ وَحْدَهُ وَحْدَهُ وَحْدَهُ اَنْجَزَ وَعْدَهُ وَ نَصَرَ عَبْدَهُ وَ اَعَزَّ جُنْدَهُ وَ هَزَمَ الْاَحْزَابَ وَحْدَهُ فَلَهُ الْمُلْكُ وَ لَهُ الْحَمْدُ يُحْيِىْ وَ يُمِيْتُ وَ يُمِيْتُ وَ يُحْيِىْ وَ هُوَ حَىُّ لَايَمُوْتُ بِيَدِهِ الْخَيْرُ وَ هُوَ عَلٰى كُلِّشَىْءٍ قَدِيْرٌ۔

(Dua Taaqibaat e Namaz - Mafateeh)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aqa! Hamara Salam e Niyaz o Adab qubool farmayye, nez Aapke Qubbe  ke gird parwanawar fida hone wale, Aapki Turbat ko hamesha ghere rehne wale, Aapki Zareeh e Aqdas ka hamesha Tawaf karne wale aur Aapki Ziyarat ko aanewale Farishton par bhi hamare Salam nichhawar hon."

"Aqa! Mein Aapke Huzoor mein Shauq ka Hadye liye Kamyabi o Kamrani ki aas lagaye hazir hua hun....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

         18th Muharram 1442

   7th September 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               ♦ MUSIBAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1503)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَإِن یَمۡسَسۡكَ ٱللَّهُ بِضُرࣲّ فَلَا كَاشِفَ لَهُۥۤ إِلَّا هُوَۖ وَإِن یُرِدۡكَ بِخَیۡرࣲ فَلَا رَاۤدَّ لِفَضۡلِهِۦۚ یُصِیبُ بِهِۦ مَن یَشَاۤءُ مِنۡ عِبَادِهِۦۚ وَهُوَ ٱلۡغَفُورُ ٱلرَّحِیمُ.

"Aur Agar Allah tujhe kisi Musibat mein dal de to Uske siwa use aur koi door nahi kar sakta aur agar Woh tere liye kisi Bhalai ka iraada kare to Uske Fazl ko rokne wala koi nahi hai. Woh Apne Bando mein se jise chahta hai Bhalai ata karta hai. Woh bada Bakhshnewala, Meherban hai."

(Surah Yunus: 107)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Guzishta Ayat se paiwast hai. Tauheed ke zikr ko jaari rakhte hue is Ayat mein Khuda hamari Fitrat ko jhanjhod kar farma raha hai ke Wohi Apne Bando ko Musibat mein mubtila karta hai to Wohi isse nikalta bhi hai.

Ek Baap apne Bete se bahut muhabbat karta hai to use utna hi tambi bhi karta hai. Beta bhi Baap se Muhabbat karta hai. Lekin jab Baap Bete ko uski Shararat ki wajah se marta hai to Beta apne aapko bachane ke liye ghairon se duhai nahi karta balke khud usi Baap se lipat jata hai aur usi se madad mangta hai. Jabke dono ek doosre Dushman nahi hain. Baap ka Bete par strict hona uski Muhabbat ka taqaza hai warna use laparwah chhod deta jisse usi ka nuqsaan hai.

Is misal se aap samajh gaye honge ke Allah kyon Apne Bando ko Musibat mein mubtila karta aur phir Wohi use bachata bhi hai. Usi tarah agar Woh Apne Bande par Bhalai karta hai to koi Use rok nahi sakta.

🕌

Allah Ta'ala farmata hai:

'Balaa o Musibat se maayus mat ho; Jaise Sona Aag mein pighla kar parkha jaata hai waise Momin balaa'on mein parkha jaata hai."

(Al-Hadith Al-Qudsi - ABISN, Nairobi, Kenya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Musibat ke waqt ghabra jaana musibat se badh-kar musibat hoti hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p68)

🍃

Imam Reza (as):

"Musibat mein Sabr karna ek achchi Neki hai, magar Haraam kaam se parhez karna usse afzal Neki hai."

(100 Maxims)

🍂

Imam Ali (as):

"Jiski Musibat badh jaye use Maut ko yaad karna chahiye, is tarah woh Musibat uske liye halki ho jayegi…"

(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Musibat)

🤲🏻

فَصَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَاٰلِهِ، وَاَعِنَّا عَلىٰ ذٰلِكَ بِفَتْحٍ مِنْكَ تُعَجِّلُهُ، وَبِضُرٍّ تَكْشِفُهُ، وَنَصْرٍ تُعِزُّهُ وَسُلْطانِ حَقٍّ تُظْهِرُهُ، وَرَحْمَةٍ مِنْكَ تَجَلِّلُنَاهَا وَعَافِيَةٍ مِنْكَ تُلْبِسُنَاهَا، بِرَحْمَتِكَ يآ اَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِيْنَ۔

(Dua-e-Iftetah)

https://youtu.be/UhlVFo8w674

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"....Aaqa! Aise Ghulam ki Aqeedat se bhar poor Salam qubool kijiye jo Aapki Izzat o Hurmat se aagah, Aapki Wilayat mein Mukhlis, Aapki Muhabbat ke Waseele se Allah ke taqarrub ka Shaida nez Aapke Dushmanon se bari o bezaar hai."

"Aaqa! Aise Aashiq ka Salam qubool farmayye niska Dil Aapki Musibaton ke sabab zakhmon se chhalni ho chuka hai aur Aapki yaad mein Khoon ke Aansu bahata hai......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

   8th September 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ DEEN MEIN JABR NAHI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1504)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قُلۡ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ قَدۡ جَاۤءَكُمُ ٱلۡحَقُّ مِن رَّبِّكُمۡۖ فَمَنِ ٱهۡتَدَىٰ فَإِنَّمَا یَهۡتَدِی لِنَفۡسِهِۦۖ وَمَن ضَلَّ فَإِنَّمَا یَضِلُّ عَلَیۡهَاۖ وَمَاۤ أَنَا۠ عَلَیۡكُم بِوَكِیلࣲ *  وَٱتَّبِعۡ مَا یُوحَىٰۤ إِلَیۡكَ وَٱصۡبِرۡ حَتَّىٰ یَحۡكُمَ ٱللَّهُۚ وَهُوَ خَیۡرُ ٱلۡحَـٰكِمِینَ.

"Aap keh den ke Aye logon!  Tumhare paas tumhare Parwardigar ki jaanib se Haq aa chuka hai. Ab jo Hidayat hasil kare to woh apne liye hi Hidayat hasil karta hai aur jo Gumrah ho jaye to uska nuqsan bhi usi ko hoga, mein tumhara zimmedar nahi hun.

Aap us Wahy ki itteba' karen jo Aap par bheji jati hai aur Sabr o Isteqamat se kaam len yahan tak ke Allah Faisla kar de aur Woh Behtareen Faisla Karnewala hai."

(Surah Yunus: 108 - 109)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ye is Surah ki ikhtetami do Ayaat pure Sure ko Conclud (khulasa) kar rahi hain.

Logon se khitab kiya jaa raha hai ke Deen mein koi Jabr, Compulsion, zabardasti nahi. Insaan apni Free Will azadai se Deen samajh kar ise qubool kare. Irshad ho raha hai ke Haq (Truth) aa gaya. Aql ka taqaza hai jab kisi ke saamne Sachchai sabit ho jaye aur Jhoot ka parda fash ho jaye to use qubool karna, apne upar Insaaf karna hoga warna tumne apne upar zulm kiya.

Deen e Islam ke Ahkam wa Hidayaat khud Insaan ke fayde ke liye hain, un par amal karega to usi ko fayda pahunchega, warna nuqsaan bhi wohi uthayga. Uske maanne ya na maanne se Rasool (saww) ya Aimma (as) ko koi farq nahi padta. Ye Shakhsiyaat to Insaan ki Hidayat (Guidance) ke liye hain jo Allah ki taraf se moayyan hain na ke inko Insaan ne banaya hai. Zaroorat is baat  ki hai ke Ilahi Numaindon aur Fake Numaindon mein farq wa tameez wa taskhees karen. Jab aap Haq ko pehchaan lenge to aap Siraate Mustaqeem (Straight Path) par aa jayenge warna idhar udhar bhatakte hi rahenge.

📙

Surah Yunus tamaam hota hai.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen andhaapan hamare fazl se aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اهْدِنِيْ لِمَا اخْتُلِفَ فِيْهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ بِاِذْنِكَ اِنَّكَ تَهْدِيْ مَنْ تَشَاۤءُ اِلٰى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيْمٍ۔

(Taqibaat Namaz e Subh - Misbah, Mafateeh)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aaqa! Is chahnewale ka Adaab qubool kijiye jo Aapke Gham mein nidhaal, behaal o bechain hai.

Aaqa! Is Jaanisar ka Hadiya e Salam qubool kijiye. Jo agar Karbala mein Aapke saath hota to Aapki hifazat ke liye Talwaaron se takra kar apni Jaan ki baazi laga deta. Dilo Jaan se Aap par fida hone ke liye Maut se Panja Azmayi karta, Aapke saamne Jang o Jihad ke johar dikhata, Aapke khilaf baghawat karne walon ke muqabile mein Aapki madad karta aur anjamkar apna Jism o Jaan, Rooh o Maal aur Aal Aulaad sab kuchh aap par qurban kar deta....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)
